11TH-01 洪水之后 / After the Flood

生活与想象力有关。
Everyone imagines their future.

我们出生、学习、成长，成为他人的友伴与爱人，铭记令祖辈骄傲的故事。
In most, they grow up, they make friends, get married, and hope to make their fathers and grandfathers proud.

带着这些旧日的一切，我们被抛向一个新的时代。
We entered this new era full of those same hopes for our future. We had no idea what lay in wait for us.

他们说，这是一个“伟大的时代”，是历史赐予一代人的成年礼——
We called it the triumphant opening to the "greatest era in history," a rite of passage for every man-to-be.

结伴而行的冒险，互相鼓励的热忱；载誉而归的欢喜，流传子孙的传奇……
"Join us in an adventure side by side, bound by courage and loyalty! Return home victorious, and let your legend be told for generations to come!"

——这是原本存在于我们想象中的事物。
That was the future we imagined.

可战争撕碎了我们的想象力。
Now those sweet and fitting lies have melted away.

那些年轻的，尚未成长的人，永远见不到本该属于他们的未来。
Barely more than children, we find ourselves bound, not for adventure, but for an open grave of mud and ruin.

而那些有幸存活下来的人，成为了难以想象的东西——
Those of us who were lucky—or unlucky—to survive this battlefield were forged into something new.

麻木。
Numb.

残忍。
Cruel.

堕落。
Corrupted.

……在地狱中求生的魔鬼。
The earth became fire and mud, and all of us devils.

无数次，我自问——我会做出怎样的选择？
What was it that we wanted from this war?

是想被人铭记为英雄，还是……成为一场永恒灾难的牺牲品？
To be remembered, celebrated as heroes, or to forget and be forgotten?

可在我见过太多次毫无价值的死亡之后，我知道——
The answer may seem obvious, but the question itself lies at fault. Because death, meaningless death, came for thousands of us every day, and we knew ...

我没有选择。
We soldiers never had a choice.

？？？：你看见了什么？
???: What do you see?

？？？：还有什么？
???: Anything else?

？？？：时代消失了吗？
???: Is the era gone?

？？？：那么，我们来到了哪一个时代？
???: Well then, what year is it now?

？？？：……
???: ...

？？？：潜意识领域稳定……未检测到侵入性幻觉……认知-现实匹配度良好……
???: Subconscious stable. No sign of invasive illusions. Cognition-reality match rate normal ...

？？？：……苏醒……
???: Our test subject awakens.

小梅斯梅尔：最后一个问题——这是什么？
Mesmer Jr.: Last question. What's this?

维尔汀：大象。
Vertin: An elephant.

提问者在意料之外的耿直面前沉默了一会儿。
Her questioner realizes she should have expected nothing less than a blunt answer.

小梅斯梅尔：答对了，很欣慰你没有给我奇怪的答案。
Mesmer Jr.: Correct. A plain and simple answer like that is an excellent sign.

维尔汀：它有很多头，很多肢体，以怪异的方式生长，如同奇异扭曲的橡树。
Vertin: Something with an abnormal number of heads and limbs, growing larger in a disturbing manner, a bit like a Yateveo.

维尔汀：它是一只奇美拉。
Vertin: Perhaps it's a chimera.

小梅斯梅尔：……我认为是你的视觉出现了重影。
Mesmer Jr.: I believe you're experiencing some double vision.

小梅斯梅尔：但精神应该没有问题。
Mesmer Jr.: But the good news is your mental status is within normal parameters, for you at least.

维尔汀：死亡的阴影，无可辨析的恶魔。
Vertin: The shadow of death, where a devil lurks within.

维尔汀：它像是要撕碎一切理性与光明，未来在它面前黯淡无光。
Vertin: Its claws are so sharp they might tear someone into pieces, shredding all rationality and hope.

小梅斯梅尔：我讨厌你不合时宜的幽默感，维尔汀。
Mesmer Jr.: Not funny, Vertin. What a horrid image.

维尔汀：好的。它是一只大象。
Vertin: Pardon me. Then it must be an elephant.

小梅斯梅尔：……至少你的精神没有问题。
Mesmer Jr.: Bad jokes aside. Your mental status is within tolerances.

维尔汀：这感觉不像过去的人工梦游。
Vertin: This test isn't like the others from the Artificial Somnambulism we used to go through.

小梅斯梅尔：从南极归来的行动人员都要接受特殊的精神检测流程。顺带一说，我并没有参与开发。
Mesmer Jr.: It's a special examination we've prepared for all personnel involved in the Antarctic operation. It wasn't my idea, by the way.

人工梦游治疗师将所有仪器关闭，焦躁的电流嗡鸣声忽然消失不见。
She powers down her equipment, the whirs and hums of its electric current fading with a soft drone.

小梅斯梅尔：按照病情来看，你不应该在我这里待这么久，但我需要按照规范完成诊疗程序。
Mesmer Jr.: I would say, based on your recovery so far, you could have been discharged a week ago, but we had strict orders to complete our entire course of treatment outlined in the Medical Manual.

小梅斯梅尔：无论南极的冰盖下藏着什么东西，它都显然没有对你的神智造成任何损害。
Mesmer Jr.: Whatever it is that hides under the Antarctic, it didn't do any additional harm to your mental health.

小梅斯梅尔：很多人没有这么幸运——他们受到的精神创伤虽然不致命，但也会影响日常生活的便利。
Mesmer Jr.: You're lucky, you know. Many others have suffered irreversible damage that will limit their day-to-day lives.

维尔汀：诺谛卡和“无名者”小姐怎么样了？
Vertin: What about Nautika and Ms. Stranger?

小梅斯梅尔：我无权得知“无名者”的情况，对她的收容和诊疗是其他专门机构的职责。
Mesmer Jr.: I have no access to Ms. Stranger's information. All I know is she's been sent to another department for treatment.

小梅斯梅尔：至于诺谛卡……她很健康。
Mesmer Jr.: As for Nautika ... she's doing great.

小梅斯梅尔用简单的词语下达判断。
Mesmer Jr. offers her judgment in plain terms.

维尔汀：科算中心为她提供了足够的活动空间吗？
Vertin: Where is she now? Does she have enough space to stretch?

小梅斯梅尔：阿德勒先生为她临时腾出了一间阶梯式报告厅，不算舒适，也不会很拥挤。
Mesmer Jr.: Mr. Hoffman cleared out a lecture hall for her. I wouldn't call it a palace, but it's spacious enough to meet her needs.

小梅斯梅尔：不过现在她身边围绕着一大群神秘生物学家、古代传说痴狂者与疯疯癫癫的仪式学家。
Mesmer Jr.: Too bad, though; now she's being cornered in there by every arcane biologist, ancient myth enthusiast, and crazy ritualist we have on staff.

小梅斯梅尔：他们都希望从诺谛卡身上得知有关南极神话的蛛丝马迹。
Mesmer Jr.: I guess they've decided she's an invaluable opportunity to learn more.

小梅斯梅尔：如果你关心她，不需要来问我，你有权直接与诺谛卡接触。
事实上，她一直在询问你的情况。
Mesmer Jr.: You do have access to that hall if you really want to know how she's doing. Just go knock on her door. She's also been asking about you.

治疗师移开视线，就此问题不愿再聊。她开始按照规范收拾病房。
The therapist averts her gaze and shifts away to end the conversation as she begins to tidy the ward.

轻细的叩门声驱散了病房空气中漂浮着的那一丝尴尬。
A soft knock at the door breaks the awkward tension.

十四行诗：司辰？
Sonetto: Timekeeper?

小梅斯梅尔：……
Mesmer Jr.: ...

维尔汀：进来吧，十四行诗。
Vertin: Come on in, Sonetto.

属于第一助手的橘色出现在被灰白色统治的病房内。她首先礼貌地看向另一位昔日同窗。
The splash of orange from her hair is a welcome break from the dull gray and white. Sonetto casts a polite glance toward her old classmate.

十四行诗：小梅斯梅尔，司辰的状况还好吗？
Sonetto: Hi, Mesmer. How's the Timekeeper doing?

小梅斯梅尔：她很好，不需要再待在我这里了。
Mesmer Jr.: She's good to go.

十四行诗：好的，我们很快就离开。
Sonetto: Thank you. Just a minute.

十四行诗回忆起今日的行程。
Sonetto recalls today's agenda.

十四行诗：司辰，Z女士说你之前委托的“暴雨”时代调查已经有了结果。她正在副会长的办公室等你。
Sonetto: Timekeeper, Madam Z said the "Storm" investigation team is back. She's waiting for you in Madam Vice President's office.

维尔汀：我们现在就去。
Vertin: Let's head that way, then.

小梅斯梅尔：那么——再见，二位。
Mesmer Jr.: You two have fun. Take care.

小梅斯梅尔送走客人，留在病房内做最后的收尾工作。
Mesmer Jr. sees the guests out, staying behind to wrap up her final tasks.

刚刚过去的第十次“暴雨”仍在基金会内部传递余震。
The aftershocks of the tenth "Storm" still ripple through the Foundation.

即使已经习惯了时代的更迭，但此时在几何形构筑的走廊内穿梭的职员们仍然显得有些慌乱。
Though they've long grown used to changing times, the staff move through the geometric corridors less like a well-oiled machine and more like a clogging artery.

十四行诗：……看起来大家的情绪仍然相当不安。
Sonetto: There's so much tension in the air now.

维尔汀：这一次的“回溯”与所有人的设想都略有不同。
Vertin: I suppose because this "Storm" was different from the ones we've seen before.

维尔汀：走吧，Z女士应该准备了更准确的消息。
Vertin: I look forward to hearing what Madam Z has to say about it.

基金会委员：……那就不用再浪费时间了。
Foundation Commissioner: I don't intend to waste my time on this anymore.

十四行诗：……？
Sonetto: ...?

一名委员从办公室中疾步走出。相比整洁体面的制服，他的面孔已经变得面目全非。
A Committee member strides out of the office, his face completely distorted, in contrast to his neat uniform.

另一人竭尽所能地克制着步伐，从门后追出来。
Another man rushes behind him, doing his best to keep his pace in check.

佩德拉：伊里内伊，我以为你已经与我们达成了一致。
Pedra: Please, I thought we reached an agreement, Irinei.

然而，他要追逐的对象早已走到道路另一头的分岔路口。
However, the one he's chasing has already reached the fork at the far end of the hall.

伊里内伊：是的，我说过——我同意会议的决策。
Irinei: Naturally, I accept the Committee's decision.

伊里内伊：如果你们觉得在这个时代可以放着重塑之手不管，那么你们就放手去做吧。
Irinei: If you really think we don't have to prioritize the Manus, then be my guest.

佩德拉：恢复这个时代的和平与秩序是当务之急，你应该充分理解——
Pedra: Our top priority is to restore peace and order to this era. You should know that ...

伊里内伊：我们处在一场比你想象得更宏大的战争之中，和平主义者。
Irinei: We're at war, Mr. Pacifist, one far more dangerous than you could possibly conceive.

佩德拉：和平主义者……你在暗示什么？
Pedra: Pacifist ... What do you mean "Pacifist"?

伊里内伊没有作答，他拐向左边的岔路，隐没了身形。
Irinei doesn't respond. He turns down the left path and disappears from view.

佩德拉：……！
Pedra: ...!

“和平主义”委员放弃了追逐，走另一条的岔路离开了。
The "pacifist" Committee member gives up his chase and takes the other path.

十四行诗：……？他们刚刚出来的房间……
Sonetto: Umm. The room they just came out of, is that ...?

维尔汀：没错，是副会长的办公室。
Vertin: It does appear so: the Vice President's office.

维尔汀：客人走了，我们进去吧。
Vertin: Let's go.

十四行诗：……好的。
Sonetto: After you.

办公室的主人不见踪影，只有她的幕僚长在室内等候。
The expected occupant is nowhere to be seen. Only her chief of staff waits inside.

Z：时间正好，司辰，十四行诗。
康复中心告诉我不需要为你们的健康担心，很高兴能亲眼验证这一点。
Z: Very nearly perfect timing, Vertin, Sonetto. I had heard that the Rehab Center cleared you for release, but it's all the more reassuring to see it for myself.

她放下一沓散乱的文件。显然，一场激烈的争吵在此处留下了不少混乱。
The signs of the fierce argument that took place linger in the mess of documents strewn over the table.

维尔汀：Z女士，我在门口遇见了伊里内伊和佩德拉。
Vertin: Madam Z, we saw Irinei and Pedra at the door.

Z：我们暂时不讨论他们的问题。
Z: Let's not talk about them for now.

维尔汀：好的。你说关于“暴雨”时代的调查已经有了结果？
Vertin: Understood. So, the "Storm" investigation team has returned?

Z：没错，根据委外合约小队与各地调查员汇总的情报，我们验证了你的猜想——历史出现了错谬。
Z: Correct. Thanks to the Field Agent Squad and our investigators, we've collected enough proof to verify your hypothesis. History has changed.

Z：……第十次“暴雨”把我们带到了一个错误的1920年，在外部，一场本不应存在的战争正在肆虐。
Z: The tenth "Storm" has brought us to an entirely different 1920 than we knew, one with a war still raging that should have long been over.

维尔汀：能确定错谬发生的原因吗？
Vertin: Do we understand why history has changed?

Z：我得知科算中心对历史错谬发生的诱因有两个推测。
Z: Laplace has two hypotheses.

Z：第一种观点认为，南极的仪式虽然未能完全成功，但它引发的“洪水”仍然导致“暴雨”的性质发生了改变。
Z: The first centers on the ritual held in the Antarctic—despite being interrupted—its "Flood" might have changed the "Storm's" nature ...

Z：在新的“暴雨”之下，时代状况会与真实历史记载产生更大的偏差——这算是较为乐观的推测。
Z: Which has resulted in an even greater deviation from history as we knew it. Don't look so discouraged; that would be much better than the other theory—

Z：比较悲观的推测则认为，阿尔卡纳经过“复活”这一神秘学机制，获得了通过“暴雨”影响历史进程的力量。
Z: After her "revival," Arcana may have obtained the power to use the "Storm" to alter the course of history.

十四行诗：如果真是这样，那我们此刻身处的时代，还有这场战争……
Sonetto: If that is the case, in all likelihood, that means this war ...

康斯坦丁：——很可能就是阿尔卡纳意志之下的产物，重塑之手或许想利用战争带来的混乱。
Constantine: —Is likely a result of intentional manipulation by Arcana. Manus Vindictae is trying to bring more chaos to the world.

庄重肃穆的房间迎来了它的主人。
The solemn room welcomes its master.

康斯坦丁：我们很久没有在这里见过面了，司辰。
Constantine: It's been a long time since we last met in this room, Timekeeper.

维尔汀：嗯，这里一点变化也没有。
Vertin: It seems like nothing has changed.

康斯坦丁：呵呵……恰好你在这里，佩德拉和伊里内伊也不在场，我可以向你补充一些新消息。
Constantine: Heh heh. But there's no time to dwell on that. I have some critical updates for you.

康斯坦丁：外部的战争正处在末期，虽然军事行动仍在继续，但交战国之间已经有了较高的停火意愿。
Constantine: This war may be close to its end. Though the fighting continues, we've begun engaging each side's leaders, and we believe a truce is possible.

康斯坦丁：联合委员会已经决定以调停人的身份介入交战国之间的谈判——维护和平永远是基金会的第一诉求。
Constantine: There will be a peace talk, and the Committee has decided to act as its mediator. Peace is always the Foundation's top priority.

康斯坦丁：另外，稳定的外部局势更有利于我们与重塑之手对抗。
Constantine: After this situation is stabilized, we'll pool our resources and focus on the Manus.

维尔汀：那谈判有进展了吗？
Vertin: I see. How's the progress so far?

对此细节问题，幕僚长代为作答。
The chief of staff answers on her behalf for this minor detail.

Z：各个分部的负责人已经为我们搭建起了沟通渠道，并确定了部分共识性条款。
Z: Our branch leaders have built lines of communication, and we have reached an agreement on some of the terms with their respective governments.

Z：佩德拉将代表基金会抵达前线与各国军事长官会晤，争取在这个月内先达成一份前线停火协定。
Z: Pedra will go to meet the commanders on behalf of the Foundation, with the aim to reach a lasting truce by the end of the month.

Z：如果一切顺利，今年结束前就有望达成最终的和平。
Z: If everything goes well, we may be able to restore peace before the new year.

现在，是时候提出一直萦绕在脑中的疑问。
Now is the time to ask the question that's been lingering in her mind.

维尔汀：我听见伊里内伊把佩德拉说成“和平主义者”，这个词是在针对和平政策？
Vertin: As we arrived, I heard Irinei call Pedra a "Pacifist." Does Irinei disagree with the Foundation's policy regarding the war?

康斯坦丁：……准确来说，是在针对以外交手段维护和平的方式。
Constantine: It isn't a matter of the policy, but the means by which we achieve it, to be precise.

维尔汀：为什么？
Vertin: How do you mean?

康斯坦丁：伊里内伊和他的追随者认为，在以武力手段消灭重塑之手前，维护和平的尝试必然失败。
Constantine: He and a few others believe all attempts to restore peace are bound to fail unless we destroy the Manus first.

康斯坦丁：他们希望基金会立刻进入备战状态。
Constantine: In short, he wants to do things the tough way.

11TH-02 旧军靴 / Old Boots

士兵们费了许多努力，终于将尸体以较为安然的姿态摆放在一块相对干燥的活木板上。
Soldiers lay a corpse on a dry wooden plank, making an effort to place their fallen comrade in something resembling a peaceful pose.

这块用来运送尸体的木板由拆散的弹药箱拼接而成，曾经当过木匠的士兵为它钉上了轮子。
The plank, formed from dismantled ammo crates, has been formed into a makeshift sledge complete with a small set of wheels.

卡戎：……
Charon: ...

战壕中的收尸人宁静地伫立在尸体旁，空洞的呼吸在灰白斗篷之下起伏不止。
The handler stands resolutely by the body at the edge of the trench, his tattered cloak making him look the part of a grim reaper.

他俯下身，掰开死者身上的识别牌，收走了下半部分。
He kneels, prying off the soldier's dog tag, and pockets the bottom half.

弗兰兹·施莱耶。
Franz Schreyer.

威利：能找到的东西都在这里了，卡戎。你能把他带走吗？
Wilhelm: This is all we could find. Can you take care of him, Charon?

卡戎：把他交给我，我会体面地为他安葬。
Charon: Naturally. He will be given a proper burial.

罗尔夫：他真是太倒霉了——我听说这个冬天就要停火了。
Rudolph: I thought they said this war would end before the winter came.

挥之不去的忧郁又从罗尔夫厚重的镜片之下流出来，如同眼泪。
A now familiar gloom seeps out from behind Rudolph's thick glasses, like tears.

弗兰兹躺在木板上，对自己的运气不置可否。
Franz lies still, indifferent to the scene.

埃里希：呵……
Erich: Heh ...

另一个满面愤懑的士兵挤进来，往木板上放了一只没有穿靴子的腿。
Another soldier shoves his way through their small crowd, puffing with frustration, places another leg on the board, completing the set.

接着，他自顾自地把尸体另一条腿上的靴子也脱下来。此刻他手中拎着一双靴子。
Then without a word, he removes the boot from the corpse's other leg—matching it with another.

埃里希：这下凑齐了。
Erich: Now he'll be ready for the march home.

威利：埃里希，你拿走了他的腿？
Wilhelm: You sure that was Franz's leg?

好心肠的威利为此惊骇不已。
The kind-hearted Captain Wilhelm looks at his soldier in horror.

埃里希：这是我自己爬出去找回来的。我认得他的靴子，他答应过，如果他死了，这靴子就归我。
Erich: Better be. I risked my life up there grabbing it. He promised I could have his boots if he got scraped off.

威利：这真是……好吧，我记得是有这么回事。
Wilhelm: My God. I remember when he said that.

他还想再说些什么，但又把话咽了回去。
He starts to say something but swallows it back.

士兵们凑在一起，在战壕的狭窄拐角处围成一个圈。
The soldiers huddle together in the narrow bend of the trench.

卡戎：可是……
Charon: But ...

卡戎有些迟钝地开口，似乎刚才的小争执并没有被他听进耳朵里。
Charon's words come out in a slow drip, seemingly unaware of the conversation around him.

卡戎：……安德烈森在一次攻势中走失了，没有它的帮助，我很难把死者送到常去的墓地。
Charon: Andreas went missing in the last attack. The body will be impossible to move off the frontlines without him.

埃里希：哦，安德烈森——这么说你的小马不见了。它可能死了。
Erich: Eh, your pony? Good bet it's worm food.

威利：埃里希——闭嘴！
Wilhelm: Shut up, Erich!

卡戎：我会试着在更接近防线的地方寻找一片宁静之地，但这会需要一些时间。
Charon: Please, don't worry. There will be somewhere quiet nearby, but it may take a while to find it.

威利：那就这样吧，卡戎。现在天气不像夏天那样炎热，时间不算紧迫。
Wilhelm: Take your time, Charon. The weather's cool these days.

连长威利安抚性地拍了拍这位负责处理尸体的士官。
Wilhelm attempts a pat on Charon's shoulder.

在不远处，营长艾伯哈特·布劳恩少校一直坐在一只空的冷却水桶上。他没有看向这方哀悼的现场，而是盯着面前的战壕胸墙。
Not far away, Major Eberhard Braun, the company commander, sits on an empty water drum. His eyes fixed coldly on the trench wall ahead.

他扔下一颗烟头，站起身。
He drops a cigarette butt and stands.

布劳恩少校：卡戎，过来一下。
Major Braun: Charon, come here.

卡戎：是。
Charon: Yes, sir.

他响应长官的召唤。
He responds to his superior.

布劳恩少校：蒙佩——还记得吗？就是我们身后不远的那个小镇子。
Major Braun: You remember Montpaix? The town near our rear?

卡戎：夏天的时候，那座镇子就是前线，老营长在那场战斗中阵亡了。
Charon: Certainly. We fought there in the warmth of summer. Our Lieutenant Colonel died in that battle.

卡戎：当时你还是连长，在那场战斗中负伤，去了后方休养。
而我用了很长时间才清理完堆积如山的遗骸。
Charon: You were in charge of a company, until you were injured and sent to recover. There were many graves to be dug, but the days were warm and dry.

布劳恩少校：该死的。但我们最终还是把敌人赶了出去，现在他们就缩在我们前面不到两百米的地方。
Major Braun: It was a hard fight to drive our enemy from that town, a damn good one. Even if our lines have only moved a short distance past it since.

卡戎：为什么你会突然提到蒙佩？
Charon: But why this talk of Montpaix all of a sudden?

布劳恩少校：总参谋部决定和基金会就停火展开谈判，会面的地点在蒙佩，希施费尔德上校会作为代表与基金会见面。
Major Braun: Army Command has decided to attend a parley held by the Foundation in Montpaix. Colonel Hirschfelder will be present on behalf of our nation.

布劳恩少校：现在那个镇子成了基金会的地盘，他们把那里叫做“安全区”。
Major Braun: We've handed it over to the Foundation. Pfft, they're calling it a "safe zone."

卡戎：希望停火能在这个冬天之内实现。
Charon: Many hope that peace will come before the winter.

营长未对这个问题做出直接回应。
The major's response is blunt.

布劳恩少校：我们距离胜利只有一步之遥。和平当然会到来，但它只能建立在我军的完全胜利之上。
Major Braun: The only end to this war I can accept is victory—total victory over our enemies.

布劳恩少校：东边的胜利已经让我们从困境中摆脱出来，人员、物资和装备正在向这里汇聚。
Major Braun: They say we've broken through on the eastern front; we only need to push our advantage, and they'll collapse. Once we've freed up all that manpower and material, we'll be able to crush our enemies here too.

卡戎：但这些也不足以支撑我们继续一场庞大的战争，少校，胜利不会带来什么，我们已经失去了一切。
Charon: We may run ourselves dry of ammo and blood before then, sir. No cries of victory are loud enough to wake the dead.

布劳恩少校：你不明白眼下的局势。
Major Braun: Winning here is a part of something far bigger than you could understand.

卡戎：你好像还在发烧——返回前线的路上，你有些过于亢奋，眼神中冒着火。
Charon: Is it? When you returned to the front after your injury, you came with eyes red as a furnace. You wore an old face, a mask of war.

卡戎：这样的神情我只在第一次与你开赴前线时才看到过。四年前，那时我们和三班的同学一起结束了训练营的训练。
Charon: You haven't worn that mask in many years, since before our first taste of battle and blood.

卡戎：……那时我们还不知道战争与死亡的真容。
你需要休息。
Charon: A whole class volunteered. Nothing more than schoolboys, we marched obliviously into the killing field. You should rest.

少校抿起本就纤薄的嘴唇，直到它成为一条刀刻般的细缝。
The major's already-thin lips press together into a sharp, blade-like line.

布劳恩少校：我需要你去一趟蒙佩。
Major Braun: Enough with the poems, soldier. I called you with an order. You must go to Montpaix.

布劳恩少校：穆伦贝格先生寄送了一些私人物品给我们，它们被堆积在安全区，而我没有时间去取。
Major Braun: Mr. Mühlenberge sent us a package, and I need someone to fetch it for me.

布劳恩少校：我想，你也是他的学生，替我取来这个包裹最合适不过。
还有，把你该收拾的那些尸体送走，不要让他们在战壕里腐烂。
Major Braun: I know you'll do your duty for the fatherland, my friend. Take as many bodies with you as you can; we can't leave them rotting in the trenches.

布劳恩少校：没别的了……就这样吧。
Major Braun: Dismissed.

少校转身离去。
The major gets up and moves down the trench.

“蒙佩，一座距离前线不算太远的城镇，四处可见的弹坑仍然在低诉着过往血腥的拉锯战。”
"Montpaix looks like it had been a nice little town before the war. Now, its old streets and laneways are pocked with craters and crumbling buildings—cruel reminders of the brutal battles that raged through it."

“断壁颓垣构成了一座宁静的空壳，只有死者才能在其中寻求安息。”
"Silent screams still echo to me from its laneways, a reminder that a man who has seen war will only find peace when he is dead and buried."

卡戎：……
Charon: ...

这座几乎被战火摧残殆尽的废弃城镇，已经很久没有迎来如此多的车辆和人员。
The town has seen the worst of the war, but with the sudden influx of traffic and activity, it seems to breathe new life.

挤占空间的并非只有军队，还有为数众多的灰白格子在刚刚清理出来的街道中穿梭。
The streets, barely cleared, are swarming with uniforms, some military, and others checkered gray-and-white.

？？？：请问你需要帮助吗，先生？
???: Are you looking for help, sir?

卡戎：……？
Charon: ...?

他缓缓回过头，一名看似医务人员的年轻女人出现在近旁。
His head creaks in the direction of the voice, finding a young woman, likely a medic.

金色的徽章表明了她基金会的身份，不过，更加醒目的是她套在外套之上的盔甲。
Her golden badge marks her as the Foundation's employee, but even more striking is the armor layered over her coat.

玛尔纱：你可以叫我玛尔纱，方便移除面部的遮挡物，让我核验你的身份吗？
Marsha: Hold on, soldier. I'm Nurse Marsha. Please show your face so I can verify your identity.

卡戎：你好，玛尔纱女士。出于某些理由，我无法展示容貌，恳请你接受用其他方式核验我的身份。
Charon: Good day, sister. What lies beneath this mask will not give you the answer you seek. Here, let this serve for identification.

他取出随身携带的记事本，从中取出夹在纸页中的一张证件。
He rummages out a notebook from his coat, retrieving a folded ID card from within.

卡戎：我是艾伯哈特·布劳恩少校的士官，这是我的身份证明。
我代他来取走一个包裹，可是我不知道应该找谁。
Charon: Major Eberhard Braun is waiting on a package from Montpaix. He sends his NCO to collect it. He did not say from whom.

基金会职员接过士官的证件。
She receives it, studying the card.

玛尔纱：这样也行。你的名字是保罗……
Marsha: I see. Your name is Paul ...

卡戎：如果你不介意的话，可以用卡戎称呼我，像其他人那样。至于我的名字……我想它并不真的属于我。
Charon: Charon. That is the name the soldiers use, and the one you should use as well. The name you see there doesn't belong to this war any longer.

玛尔纱：我明白了。
Marsha: I've heard your name before.

她把证明文件交还给士官，随后有些尴尬地捏了捏自己的掌心。
She returns the document, then scans around as she wrings her hands.

玛尔纱：这里确实有很多从后方邮寄来的包裹，应该也有给布劳恩少校的，不过……现在办收件手续可能会费一番周折。
Marsha: You'll find plenty of packages here. Go ahead and look for whichever one belongs to your Major Braun, but there'll be more paperwork to sign before you can leave with it.

玛尔纱：也许得等到希施费尔德上校与基金会的会谈结束之后，他们才能匀出人手处理文书工作。
Marsha: If you're willing to wait, things will get moving again once the parley has finished.

卡戎：没关系，我可以等待。
Charon: Time is a resource the dead have in abundance.

说完，他默然地站在原地。
He looks back at her, his body seeming almost rooted to the spot.

玛尔纱：你——还好吗？
Marsha: Are you certain you're alright, soldier?

卡戎：……我很好。抱歉，我的反应力比以前要差很多了。我正在思考下一个问题。
Charon: The war has taken its toll, but there is nothing you can do to fix these old wounds.

卡戎：请问你是一名战地医生吗？
Charon: You said that you are a medic, Sister Marsha. Is that why you ask?

玛尔纱：算是吧。原本我应该待在医疗站里，但因为实在缺人，所以我就出来帮个忙。
Marsha: Yes, of course. Ordinarily I would be at the clinic, but I was asked to lend a hand here.

卡戎：医疗站里死去的人是如何处理的？
Charon: Where are the dead from your clinic laid to rest?

战地医生面色平静地思忖有关死者的问题。
She reflects on his words.

玛尔纱：现在蒙佩的医疗站还没有死亡的病人，不过这确实是个问题。
Marsha: We don't have any yet, by the grace of God. Though, I don't expect that to remain the case.

玛尔纱：刚过来的时候，我在附近看到过一个可以用作墓地的小坡，如果真的出现无法救治的人……
Marsha: There is a bare slope just outside of town; I noticed it when we first arrived here. It could serve that purpose were someone to die ...

卡戎：这正是我想要的。
Charon: That is good to hear.

玛尔纱：……无法救治的人？
Marsha: That someone might die?

慢一拍的回应导致了一些小误会。
The delayed reply leads to misunderstanding.

卡戎：不，我是说墓地。
Charon: Ah, no. The slope.

卡戎：我正在寻找一片足够安宁与平静的土地，用以安葬在前线死亡的士兵。
Charon: A quiet place is needed. Many of us from the frontlines could find rest there.

玛尔纱：你是为战友收尸的人吗？
Marsha: You mean your brothers in arms?

卡戎：不仅是战友。只不过，作为一名挂靠在营里的士官，我穿着的衣服会限制我的行动。
Charon: All who need burial are my brothers in arms. Though they may have once fought on different sides.

卡戎：如果你愿意与我共享墓地，我可以为你充当守墓人，替基金会埋葬尸体，准备棺材与墓碑。很抱歉，这是我仅能提供的报酬。
Charon: Should there be any in your clinic that need it, they will find rest there too. In a coffin under a marker to remember their place, as is fitting. If you will allow it.

玛尔纱：这样的话……好吧，我可以带你去。
Marsha: So be it. You're offering them more decency than most others would. I'll show you the spot.

蒙佩郊外。
The outskirts of Montpaix.

密林掩藏了大多醒目的痕迹，与此同时，一些细微的动静则会被放大。
Dense woods conceal most obvious traces, yet small sounds are amplified.

士兵？：——什么人？
Soldier?: Who's there?

？？？：你迟到了。
???: You've run late.

士兵？：……这片区域被基金会看得很死，我好不容易才溜进来。
Soldier?: I barely made it. This whole area is under heavy guard.

士兵眯起眼，警惕地打量着眼前身穿灰蓝色制服的军人。
The soldier squints, eyes narrowing at the gray-blue uniformed figure ahead.

士兵？：艾克特去哪儿了？他从来没有说过自己和一个女人一起行动。
你的口令呢？
Soldier?: Where's Hector? He never mentioned you. Give me the countersign.

他举起枪，陌生人的轮廓被他框在照门之内。
He raises his weapon, framing the stranger in his sights.

士兵？：喂，说话！表明身份。
Soldier?: You hear me? Who the hell are you?

面对枪口，受威胁的一方只是流露出一丝厌倦。
Yet his target is unfazed.

？？？：我可以给你两个选择。
???: Two paths lie ahead for you.

士兵？：你在说什么？
Soldier?: W-What are you talking about?

？？？：回答问题，你的长官躲在哪里。或者……
???: In one, you lead me to your commander. In the other ...

她以肃穆到近似祈祷的姿态取下步枪——对方不禁为此呆愣一秒。
She lowers her rifle and bows her head in a motion almost like prayer. It stuns the soldier for a moment.

？？？：——下地狱吧。
???: You are led into perdition.

最后一声枪响在浓密的树林间回荡，最终消失不见。
The final gunshot rings through the thick forest, then fades away.

她蹲下，从倒地敌人身上取下一只地图包。
She crouches, retrieving a pouch from the fallen enemy.

在杂乱的图纸间，她找到了自己需要的纸条。
In the mess of documents and maps, she finds the note she needs.

？？？：基金会，谈判，希施费尔德……
???: Foundation, parley, Hirschfelder ...

阅读完毕，她抬头望向东北方——在林木掩映之外，伫立着蒙佩的废墟。
After reading it, she looks northeast. Beyond the treeline lie the ruins of Montpaix.

？？？：……今天。
???: Today.

11TH-03 鹰喙 / Battle of the Birds

红弩箭：你真不和我一起去吗，头儿？
Lilya: Are you sure you won't come with me, Captain?

在经过了一段长时间的休整之后，飞行女巫已经做好执行新任务的准备。
After a long rest, Lilya readies up for her next mission.

维尔汀：这是索姆将军交给你的任务，不涉及司辰小队。
Z女士要求我留在基金会总部。
Vertin: Admiral Somme assigned this mission to you personally, not the whole team. Besides, Madam Z asked me to stay in the headquarters.

红弩箭：难道你还没有受够这个无聊的地方吗？根据那个《暴雨改革》法案，司辰小队不受基金会的制约。
Lilya: *sigh* Isn't it going to be boring waiting around here? The Storm Reformation directives said Team Timekeeper isn't subject to the Foundation's orders. We can go wherever we want.

十四行诗：但司辰本人仍然需要对Z女士负责，红弩箭小姐。
Sonetto: Yet it also says the Timekeeper is still bound by Madam Z's orders, Lilya.

红弩箭：——这真是有够人受的。
Lilya: Ugh, soooo frustrating.

渴望自由的飞行员闷闷不乐地接受了这个事实。
Reality slams up against her freedom-loving impulses.

红弩箭：我原本以为有机会带你去看看真正的草原，那个场面一定会让你永生难忘。
Lilya: I thought I'd finally be able to show you what things are really like out on the steppe. It's going to be a view to remember.

维尔汀：以后会有机会的。
Vertin: We'll have other chances.

红弩箭：呵，不管是什么时代，那里的景色倒也都没什么区别。
不过你“留在总部”的任务要什么时候才能结束？
Lilya: Yeah. I suppose a view like that doesn't change much no matter what era it is. Anyway, any idea when they're going to set you loose again?

维尔汀：我猜要等到基金会的动荡结束之后，我才有机会独自行动。
Vertin: I think it will have to wait until after the tension clears.

红弩箭：动荡？
Lilya: What are you talking about?

十四行诗：你听过关于“鸽派”与“鹰派”的争端吗？
Sonetto: Haven't you heard about the Doves and the Hawks?

红弩箭：没听过，这段时间我都在休息。
Lilya: We got birds now? Nah. I just got back from vacation.

红弩箭：这听起来又是一些无聊的政治斗争。我已经玩过一次，除非维尔汀再被扣押，否则我绝不想玩第二次。
Lilya: Let me guess, same thing as ever: politics. Go on, just tell me enough so I know who to blast if someone kidnaps Vertin again.

十四行诗：……简单来说，联合委员会在和平战略的问题上分裂成了“鸽派”和“鹰派”。
Sonetto: Simply put, the Committee has split into two factions on the Foundation's course of action: the Doves and the Hawks.

十四行诗：“鸽派”坚持要维护政治原则，以外交方式达成和平，以此在战后的政治秩序中获益。
Sonetto: The Doves insist on seeking peace through diplomacy, hoping to secure advantages in the post-war political landscape.

红弩箭：那“鹰派”呢？
Lilya: Uh-huh, and the Hawks?

十四行诗：“鹰派”相信重塑之手已经渗透了军队高层，外交手段无法实现和平。
Sonetto: They believe that the governments we're dealing with have been infiltrated too deeply by Manus Vindictae, so diplomacy is off the table.

十四行诗：他们想要打破过去处理时代问题的准则，以更直接的手段逮捕涉嫌与重塑之手合作的军政界高层。
Sonetto: They want to take more direct action, by arresting any high-ranking military and political figures suspected of collaborating with the Manus.

红弩箭：这听起来更有效率，不过也许会搞出大乱子。
Lilya: Really? I would have never thought we'd do something like that. Efficient, the kind of plan I like, but also like it could be the mother of all messes.

维尔汀：所以，目前是“鸽派”的政策占据上风。
Vertin: Precisely. That's why the Doves prevailed, at least for now.

红弩箭意兴阑珊地摇摇头。对她来说，政治问题说到这个程度已经够她受了。
Lilya shakes her head. She's had enough of politics for one day.

红弩箭：这太复杂了。头儿，你站哪边？
Lilya: Complicated. So, what side you on, Captain?

维尔汀：我不会站在任何一方。
Vertin: I'm not on any side.

出发的时间已到，飞行女巫跨上Su-01ве。
Departure time. She mounts her Su-01ве.

红弩箭：总之，我站在你这边。
Lilya: No matter then. I am on your side.

红弩箭：再见！
Lilya: See you later!

飞行扫帚呼啸着喷射出强劲的气流，老练的驾驶员很快消失在了云层之中。
With a sharp roar, the flying broom shoots out a blast of air, and soon enough the seasoned pilot vanishes into the clouds.

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

康斯坦丁：……战争延长的每一天都会造成大量无谓伤亡，为了尽快做出应对，参与决策的人数应该尽可能少。
Constantine: People are dying out there. We have to reduce the number of decision-makers. We can't afford any delays.

康斯坦丁：在联合委员会开始前，我需要各派的领袖在这间办公室里先行达成一致。
Constantine: I need all the faction leaders to reach an agreement before the Committee meeting starts.

维尔汀：所以你之前召集了佩德拉和伊里内伊。
Vertin: That's why Pedra and Irinei were here.

康斯坦丁：没错，让伊里内伊妥协不是一件容易的事，好在最终还是说服了他。
Constantine: Yes. It was not an easy task to persuade Irinei, but we did it.

维尔汀：我不代表任何派别，没必要留在这里。
为什么不批准我的外勤申请？
Vertin: Good. But I'm not on either side. It seems like there's no need for me to stay. Why are you keeping me around?

康斯坦丁：这是出于其他的理由。
Constantine: I have my reasons, as I'm sure you expect.

康斯坦丁：《暴雨改革》法案无法一劳永逸地保障司辰小队的权利，维尔汀，这场派系争端一定会带来很多新的政策变更。
Constantine: The Storm Reformation Act won't keep you and your team secure forever, Vertin. The final result of this meeting, whatever it is, will change many things.

康斯坦丁：你有机会为你和你麾下的神秘学家争取比初版法案更多的权益与预算。当然，情况也可能完全相反。
Constantine: That may mean more latitude and resources for your team. Then again, it could mean the exact opposite.

康斯坦丁：如果你不想失去这次机会，那就必须留在总部，直到所有事情告一段落。
Constantine: Anyway, if you intend to seize anything from this opportunity, you'll need to stay until the meeting's over.

维尔汀：……我们走吧，十四行诗。
Vertin: Time to go, Sonetto.

？？？：真是令人印象深刻的起飞动作，那位就是红弩箭中尉？
???: Quite the take-off. That must've been Lieutenant Lilya, wasn't it?

维尔汀：……？
Vertin: ...?

转过头去，一名红发男子出现在视野中。
She turns, and a red-haired man enters the frame.

刻雷乌斯：她就是人们说的红弩箭中尉吗，司辰？
Creius: Have I got it right, Timekeeper?

维尔汀：是的。
Vertin: You have.

十四行诗：您是……刻雷乌斯先生，“Ⅻ”小队的队长？
Sonetto: You must be Mr. Creius, the captain of the "XII."

刻雷乌斯：看来我们已经通过某些渠道互相认识了。
Creius: Seems you're already acquainted then.

十四行诗：是的，我读过南极行动的详细报告，其中就有您的名字……
Sonetto: I've read the report on the Antarctic operation; your name was mentioned.

行动队长向第一助手点头致谢，随后，他换上更加审慎的目光。
Creius nods to Sonetto in thanks before adopting a more guarded expression.

刻雷乌斯：在前往南极之前，我也了解过你的事迹，司辰。
Creius: I've been reading up on you. Just a few choice selections from your after-action reports before our Antarctic expedition.

刻雷乌斯：不光是南极，还有之前的几次“暴雨”，你的小队挫败了重塑之手的很多阴谋。
Creius: Seems we have you and your team to thank for thwarting many a wicked scheme hatched by Manus Vindictae in previous "Storms."

刻雷乌斯：可惜，南极行动的结局不算太完美，眼下又有一场战争拦在我们面前……
Creius: Shame we couldn't put a stop to Arcana's revival too. Now look at the dog's breakfast of an era we stepped into ...

“哔——哔——”
"beep—beep—"

一则通讯请求恰好在此刻接入。
A communication request comes through at that exact moment.

刻雷乌斯还想说些什么，但也只好无奈地就此作罢。
Creius is about to speak again but lets it go.

刻雷乌斯：我想，以后我们还会有其他合作的机会——如果你有任何需要的话，司辰，都可以与我联系。
Creius: I do hope we'll have the chance to cooperate more closely in the future. Feel free to call on me if you find yourself in need, Timekeeper.

维尔汀：……好的。我也必须要离开了，刻雷乌斯先生。
Vertin: Thank you, Mr. Creius. I'm afraid further introductions will have to wait; we're called elsewhere.

三人结束了这场短暂的偶遇。
The brief encounter ends.

刻雷乌斯留在原地，摁下了通讯器的接通按钮。
Creius remains where he is, pressing his communicator.

刻雷乌斯：……
Creius: ...

刻雷乌斯：说。
Creius: Speak.

？？？：照你说的，我已经向部分到访安全区的政要警告了重塑之手可能在渗透高层的情况，但他们信不信我不知道。
???: I passed along our intel about Manus Vindictae's possible infiltration of the safe zone; anyone's guess if they're gonna do a damned thing about it.

？？？：另外，玛尔纱和一个引人注目的士官离开了蒙佩。
???: And Marsha was seen leaving the safe zone with an odd-looking German soldier.

刻雷乌斯：什么理由？
Creius: Any idea where she's heading?

？？？：我可不会凑上去听——毕竟，我不想在不该出现的时候露脸。
???: I kept my distance. Didn't wanna risk exposure.

刻雷乌斯：说说你的判断。
Creius: Should I have any concerns about it?

？？？：那个士官的外貌很怪异，但从行为上看不太像是重塑之手的人。
???: Whatever he is, I don't get the impression he's with the Manus.

？？？：他和玛尔纱只是偶然相见，就站在路中间说话。
???: He came up from the lines, started a conversation, and just like that, they started walking away.

？？？：说实在的，你从南极回来之后多少有些神经过敏了，觉得到处都有重塑之手。
???: You're jumping at shadows, Creius. Ever since Antarctica, it seems like you've been imagining phantom oil stains on everyone we meet.

讽刺的言辞落了个空，通讯另一头的人等来的是一条明确的指令。
He leaves the remarks unanswered. On the other end is a clear directive.

刻雷乌斯：跟上玛尔纱。
Creius: All the same, keep an eye on her.

？？？：蒙佩这边不需要我盯着了吗？你之前还说，怀疑有重塑之手的人混入了会场……
???: And take my eyes off the town? What about searching for those infiltrators?

刻雷乌斯：那里有基金会的安保人员。
Creius: The Foundation has enough security on-site to keep things in check.

？？？：希望那些石头脑袋能顶用吧……梅蕾尔和帕拉维扬都已经调到总部了？
???: Yeah, right, let's just hope those hay-for-brains can do their job. Haven't Merel and Paravyan been transferred to HQ?

刻雷乌斯：……对。不过他们要和我一起行动，只是委员会还没通过我的外勤申请。
Creius: I hope you weren't expecting a hand. I need them for my field mission as soon as our application is approved.

？？？：呵——基金会还是信不过你？
???: Hah, still waiting for that—they haven't learned to trust you yet?

刻雷乌斯：完成你的任务，叶尔莫莱。
Creius: Focus on your mission, Yermolai.

“士兵们通常没有机会一观战壕的全貌，而我常常将它想象成一种爪痕。”
"Not many of us have any real idea what it's like to view the trenches from above. But in my haunted dreams and flashes of imagination, I picture them as claw marks."

“有关爪痕的印象在心中挥之不去——庞大而黑暗的怪兽撕开土地，我们则躲藏在它创造的沟壑中瑟瑟发抖。”
"I keep returning to that thought over and over again: the image of some terrible monster ripping the earth apart with its claws, then we hide, trembling like maggots in the wounds it leaves behind."

玛尔纱：我们到了。
Marsha: Here.

卡戎驻足凝视着这片布满壕沟的坡地，时间还不足以消弭此地的伤疤。
Charon stops, staring out over the woods, only just beginning to advance on a slope that bears the scars of trench work and artillery.

卡戎：总的来说，这是个安静的地方……也许战壕中还有不少没有被清理的尸体。
Charon: It is quiet enough, but the dead may come to outnumber the empty lodgings below.

玛尔纱：唯一的问题是，这里离蒙佩有一些距离了。
Marsha: I wouldn't have thought the dead mind having neighbors. The real trouble is how far it is from the clinic.

收尸人的目光在丘陵与玛尔纱之间来回移动，最终锁定在后者身上的盔甲。
He lets his gaze drift from the hills to Marsha, settling on her armor.

卡戎：我有一个问题想要问你。
Charon: There is something about you—a contradiction lying under cloth and steel.

玛尔纱：没错，我之前的确在军队中服役。
Marsha: I know what you want to ask. Yes, I was a knight once.

她早已知道问题，干脆抢先一步做出回答。
She preempts the question, one she's learned to expect.

卡戎：……
Charon: ...

玛尔纱：我过去是骑士团的成员，和其他神秘学家一样，开战之后就作为特殊部队被投入战场。
Marsha: Like other arcanists, I was enlisted in a special unit and sent to the front as soon as the war started.

玛尔纱：出于某些原因，我现在是一名战地医生……但我还是习惯把一部分旧时的盔甲穿在身上。
Marsha: This armor is only a habit. I'm a medic now.

玛尔纱：它虽然无法挡住步枪弹，也没有承载太好的回忆，但我希望以此纪念那些永远不会再见的战友。
Marsha: It's not much for protection; modern bullets go through steel this thin like paper. But I want to remember.

卡戎：军队严禁士兵擅自退出服役，你是怎么转而为基金会服务的？
Charon: Only in death does duty end. Yet, you live again with the Foundation.

玛尔纱：……
Marsha: ...

玛尔纱：我现在不想回答这个问题。
Marsha: Another of your questions? This time I won't give you an answer.

士官如同一名笨拙的士兵，狼狈地跌进了泥坑里。
He stumbles at her retort, like a clumsy soldier stuck in mud.

卡戎：是我有失考量，但是……至少请你相信，我没有在追究你。
Charon: There was no ill intent. The ways of this war do not fall upon your shoulders.

卡戎：如果我能摆脱当前的命运，我也会永远离开军队。
Charon: Our path is not chosen, nor can it be escaped. The end to our war is found in the grave.

玛尔纱：我明白。
Marsha: I know.

玛尔纱：也许等和约签订之后，你就能得偿所愿，很快军队就不需要那么多军人了。
Marsha: Death shouldn't be the only way a soldier like you can find peace.

骑士回望来路——通向蒙佩的道路被一座茂密的森林隔断。
Marsha glances back. The view of Montpaix is blocked by a dense forest.

玛尔纱：我该回去了，再见，卡戎。
Marsha: I'm needed back at the clinic.

卡戎：……再见。
Charon: And there is work to be done here.

卡戎：再次向你表达我的歉意，女士。
Charon: Please hear this apology. You have chosen a noble path.

安全区内，第一轮会谈已经结束。
Inside the safe zone, the first round of talks has concluded.

希施费尔德上校从悬挂着基金会旗帜的房屋走出，在他身后，军官们紧密地围成一道屏风。
Colonel Hirschfelder exits the building draped in Foundation banners. Adjutant officers flank him tightly, like remoras swimming beside a shark.

上校：……该走了。
Colonel: This meeting is over.

上校的勤务兵为他披上外套。军方代表的心情不算太好，他急于结束这场会谈的意向相当明显。
His aide drapes a coat over his shoulders. The colonel's mood is sour. His eagerness to end the talks is obvious.

佩德拉委员以次要位置伴随在希施费尔德上校身旁，不失风度。
Commissioner Pedra follows at a respectful distance, maintaining proper decorum.

佩德拉：……这是一个对所有人都有利的方案，我恳请您和总参谋部认真考虑，上校先生。
Pedra: Our proposal really is in everyone's best interest. Please give it a bit more thought, Colonel.

上校：我军目前在战争总体局势上占据着优势，如果要签订停火协定，这一点必须得到承认。
Colonel: Our best interest, yes? You have failed to convince me. All I see is the insistence that we pretend this war is not going in our favor.

上校：另外，关于重塑之手的讨论，我希望基金会在未来能谨慎措辞。
Colonel: And I will have no more of these ridiculous conspiracies concerning Manus Vindictae.

上校：我们的战略与你们所谓的邪教团体毫无关联，军方的抉择符合目前对整体局势的理性考量。
Colonel: Our war and our victory have nothing to do with this terrorist organization—or cult, as it may be. The decisions of His Imperial Majesty's government will only align with a rational assessment of the facts at hand.

佩德拉：基金会充分理解这个问题。
Pedra: We fully understand your concerns.

上校：那就再好不过。
Colonel: Words without action.

佩德拉：至少，多方之间可以先达成初步停火协定——士兵仍然可以驻扎在前线，但这个冬天不必再进行大规模军事行动。
Pedra: Would you at least consider a temporary truce? Keep your forces at the front, but halt all active military operations?

军方代表坐上已经在路边停留等候的车辆。
The military delegates enter the car idling roadside.

上校：这取决于对方是否会表达出足够的善意。我认为，首先必须停止的是对我方军事人员的刺杀行动。
Colonel: There are two sides to every truce, Mr. Negotiator. Our enemy has yet to show any hint of sincerity.

佩德拉：刺杀？
Pedra: You're referring to the assassinations?

上校：敌人一直在派遣狙击手，渗透到我军后方，刺杀高级——
Colonel: Do these bastards have any honor? Sending their snipers after our high-ranking ...

一个凝固的瞬间。
Time freezes.

首先是自上校的脖颈处绽裂的鲜血，在几声沉闷的心跳之后，在场的人才听见遥远的枪声。
A bloom of crimson explodes out from the colonel's neck. Staccato heartbeats thump in a rising crescendo to meet the distant booming crack of a rifle.

佩德拉：……！
Pedra: ...!

佩德拉：……什——怎么——
Pedra: What the ...

静滞的时间缓缓化开，一切开始恢复活力——高声呼叫、奋力奔跑、枪械开火……
Time melts back into motion. Shouts erupt, feet thunder, weapons fire off at shadows ...

佩德拉感到有人在揪他的衣领，这股牵扯的力量越来越强。
Pedra feels someone yanking at his collar, the pull growing stronger.

基金会安保：请躲入掩体，佩德拉委员！
Foundation Security Staff: Take cover, Mr. Pedra!

佩德拉：唔——
Pedra: Ugh ...

士兵们则扑向自己的长官。
Soldiers dive toward their fallen officer.

警卫士兵：狙击手，敌袭！
Security Guard: Sniper!

混乱的嘈杂最终淹没了一切。
Chaos drowns out all else.

警卫士兵：医生——上校中弹了，医生在哪里？！
Security Guard: Medic! The colonel has been hit! We need a medic!

警卫士兵：把车开走，带上校去抢救，快！
Security Guard: Move! Get the colonel to the clinic!

11TH-04 灰蓝色 / Grayish Blue

告别了收尸人的骑士，仍在赶往基金会安全区的路上。
Having parted ways with the curious gravedigger, the knight continues back to the Foundation's safe zone.

枝叶交织出的阴影中偶然会传出一些令人警惕的“沙沙”声，但最终证明只是一些胆怯的动物在制造噪音。
Tangled branches rustle, sharpening her mind into alarm. But as her hand twitches to her sidearm, a small and timid creature hops out.

玛尔纱：……只是一只兔子。
Marsha: *sigh* Just a hare.

玛尔纱：真好，现在这里已经有了兔子。
Marsha: Good to know they've returned.

或许有一日，蒙佩的居民会返回家乡，被遗弃的荒地会被重新开垦。
It feels in some way hopeful. If the hares can return, perhaps too people, flowers, life.

“砰……”
*bang*

她听见绝不可能认错的枪声。
The sound is unmistakable, and yet she questions herself.

玛尔纱：有人开枪？
Marsha: Was that a gunshot?

她迅速警惕起来，低下身子，集中注意力分辨周身的每一处动静。
She drops low, seeking its source—scanning—placing the sound.

玛尔纱：……是安全区的方向。
Marsha: From the safe zone.

久经沙场的感官在尽可能地分辨每一处细节。
Battle-honed senses strain to pick out the smallest detail.

“哔——”
*beep—beep—*

玛尔纱：……！
Marsha: ...!

……以至于通讯器的提示音让她吓了一跳。
The abrupt alert tone startles her upright and out of cover.

玛尔纱：没有呼叫人的信息……但这个设备只有基金会的人能打进来。
Marsha: No ID, but it has to have come from someone in the Foundation.

她按下接通键。
She hits the connect button.

？？？：——玛尔纱，没错吧？
???: Marsha, right?

玛尔纱：你是谁？
Marsha: Who are you?

？？？：紧急情况，现在没时间玩推理。
???: No time to explain. Just listen.

？？？：第一，蒙佩发生了一起刺杀事件，希施费尔德上校在自己的汽车里被一颗步枪弹打穿了脖子。当场死亡。
???: Colonel Hirschfelder was just assassinated getting into his car right after the parley. The shot went clean through his neck, severed the carotid artery.

玛尔纱：——希施费尔德上校死了？
Marsha: The colonel's dead?

？？？：第二件事，从弹道的轨迹来判断，刺杀上校的狙击手很可能就躲藏在你身处的树林中。
???: Yeah, but the important thing is that the shot came from the forest, somewhere near your location.

玛尔纱：你……你知道我在哪儿？
Marsha: How do you know where I am?

？？？：——注意隐蔽。确保安全之后，我会提醒你。
???: Just take cover. I'll call again when it's safe.

玛尔纱：你到底是——？
Marsha: Who on earth are ...

通讯已经切断，玛尔纱只好把设备调整为静音模式，呆呆地收回去。
The call is cut. Marsha switches the device to silent and tucks it away, stunned.

玛尔纱：谈判代表被刺杀了，这样的话，谈判会……
Marsha: With the colonel dead, there isn't much hope for the peace talks.

她重复着刚刚听见的消息，嘴里有些干涩。
She repeats the message under her breath, her mouth dry.

玛尔纱：不是想这种事的时候。如果狙击手还在这片森林里……
Marsha: Can't worry about that now. The sniper may still be here.

曾经的骑士很快从突发事件带来的震撼中恢复过来——骑士团的训练让她明白如何掌控情绪与激素分泌水平。
She siphons the shock into willpower. The Order's training has taught her how to manipulate her emotions, controlling them right down to the flow of hormones.

同样，这种训练也让她不习惯坐以待毙。
They've also taught her not to sit and wait for death.

玛尔纱：身上只有一把手枪，但距离够近的话，应该没有太大的劣势。
Marsha: All I have is this pistol. Still, a bullet is a bullet. I'll just need to get close.

她拿出武器，在可供隐蔽的粗大树干与浓密灌木中不断穿梭，一步步向蒙佩的方向接近。
Retrieving her weapon, she weaves tactically between thick tree trunks and dense shrubs that offer concealment, inching her way back to Montpaix.

视线穿过无数枝条构成的缝隙，骑士捕捉到了一个清晰可见的人影。
Between the brambles and foliage, she spies armed figures in the distance.

玛尔纱：——有人。
Marsha: Over there.

？？？：……什么人？
???: Who's there?

显然，对方恰好也发现了自己。
Evidently, she has been spotted too.

玛尔纱：——！
Marsha: ...!

她本能地向下趴卧，一颗子弹在金属甲胄上留下了一道数寸长的弹痕。
On instinct, she slumps downward, and a bullet scrapes a long gash across her metal armor.

玛尔纱：手枪弹……
Marsha: Small caliber.

玛尔纱：五个人，两把冲锋枪，制服……无法分辨。
Marsha: Five of them, two with machine pistols. Their uniforms, unclear in origin.

？？？：出来！
???: Come out!

又是一连串射击，飞溅的木屑在她的皮肤上切出一道道血珠。
A flurry of follow-up shots shreds bark and skin, painting her armor with splashes of blood.

玛尔纱：——！
Marsha: ...!

她深吸一口气，将心跳调整到大约每分钟90次。
But she leans on her training, slowing her heartbeat to limit her bleeding and maintain focus.

玛尔纱：至少得留一个活的。再近一点——
Marsha: Need to leave one alive. Now, to get a little closer ...

袭击者纷纷倒下，玛尔纱小心翼翼地探出头查看，却无法分辨他们的军籍。
Her ambushers fall one by one. Marsha peeks out from cover, unable to identify their uniforms.

玛尔纱：这身衣服……看起来不像任何制式军装。也许是重塑之手的人？
Marsha: Black uniforms ... Can't tell who they might be. Perhaps the Manus?

玛尔纱：他们是被其他方向的射手击杀的……
Marsha: Never mind. Who is it that helped me? Could you—

正在思索间，几片干枯的叶片落在玛尔纱头顶。
While Marsha is pondering this, a few dry leaves land on top of her head.

？？？：抬头。
???: Cast your eyes up.

玛尔纱：嗯？
Marsha: Huh?

抬头，望向高处——陌生的身形隐藏在巨大的雨披中。
She looks up to behold a cloaked figure hidden among the branches.

玛尔纱：——！
Marsha: ...!

醒目的步枪构成轮廓上一根颇为扎眼的尖刺，不得不让玛尔纱想起杀死了希施费尔德上校的步枪子弹。
Her rescuer bears a rifle, heavy caliber, scoped, with distinct markings—the weapon of a sniper.

纵使心中已经有了危险的推断，但玛尔纱仍然在试探性地发问。
A dangerous inference is drawn in her mind. Yet Marsha begins tentatively.

玛尔纱：你是谁？刚刚那些人是你杀的吗？——你知不知道他们是谁？
Marsha: Was it you who shot these men? Do you know who they are?

她的提问仿佛力量不足的小石子，没有抛到陌生人所处的高处。
She feels as if the questions are only pebbles lobbed too lightly to reach the perched stranger.

玛尔纱：为什么你只是……这么看着？你难道不是有什么话想和我说吗？毕竟，你不必让我发现你的。
Marsha: You must have something more to say. Why bother showing yourself otherwise?

？？？：……基金会在做什么？
???: Tell me, what is it that the Foundation concerns itself with here?

玛尔纱：这不是一个秘密，基金会正在蒙佩组织停火谈判，可是……谈判代表遭到了刺杀。
Marsha: That's no secret. We're working on a parley to end this war, but one of the representatives has just been assassinated.

玛尔纱：这也许和刚才那些穿黑色衣服的人有关。
Marsha: These soldiers dressed in black could be our culprits.

？？？：不，他们是来保护希施费尔德的。
???: No. They were sent forth to protect Hirschfelder. Though they tarried too late.

玛尔纱：保护？——你知道希施费尔德？那……又是谁杀了他？
Marsha: Wait, you know Hirschfelder? Do you have any idea who shot him?

？？？：我。
???: I did.

玛尔纱：你——咳咳！果然是——咳——
Marsha: You! *cough* You ...

刺激性的浓烟几乎让她无法睁眼。
Acrid smoke stings her eyes, blinding her vision.

玛尔纱：为什——为什么——呃。
Marsha: Why ... *cough*

玛尔纱：咳咳——咳——
Marsha: *cough*

总参谋部：重塑之手……不，元帅不接受这样的解释。
Army Commander: Manus Vindictae? No. The Field Marshal will not entertain such a thing.

总参谋部：我们倾向于认为，这个团体只是你们为了实现某些目的而杜撰的假想敌。
Army Commander: You've simply conjured up some invisible enemy to achieve your goals.

总参谋部：至于这次的刺杀事件，完全是敌国的刻意羞辱，他们想借此让我们的军队陷入恐慌。
Army Commander: We can conclude only this: that our enemy agreeing to this parley was only a ruse and that the assassination of our colonel was meant to sow fear in our ranks.

总参谋部：但我们不会因此屈服。他们放弃了谈判的机会，就必须要为此付出代价。
Army Commander: We will not yield to such a contemptible tactic. They have chosen war, and we will answer in kind.

通讯被粗暴地切断，没有留下任何商量的余地。
The line is cut abruptly, leaving no room for negotiation.

混杂着茫然的紧张情绪在室内不断蔓延。
Confusion and tension ripple through the office, simmering like a pot ready to boil.

……
...

Z：蒙佩的刺杀事件发生之后，其他国家也中止了停火谈判进程。
Z: The assassination in Montpaix has been a serious blow to our global efforts. Many nations have withdrawn from our peace talks in response.

康斯坦丁：刺杀事件中，基金会方有没有人员损失？
Constantine: Did we lose anyone?

Z：没有。刺杀上校的狙击手似乎有很强的针对性。根据在现场的调查员报告，他们只听见了一声枪响。
Z: No. Our investigators on the scene confirmed they heard just a single gunshot at the time.

Z：还有一个外勤人员声称，自己目击了狙击手本人。
Z: We do have a confirmed sighting of the shooter.

康斯坦丁：目击狙击手的基金会人员没有遭到攻击，那对方的身份应该也不是重塑之手。
Constantine: Yes. I heard. Yet they didn't fire on her, which means our shooter isn't likely to be with the Manus.

幕僚长点头认同，随之将此事诱发的内部问题摆上台前。
The chief of staff nods in agreement, then lays out the situation at hand.

Z：“鹰派”对此事反应非常强烈，他们重提了让基金会进入备战状态的诉求。
Z: The Hawks have reacted strongly to this incident; they're calling for the Foundation to enter a state of war readiness again.

Z：伊里内伊在最近一次委员会会议上的说辞十分有煽动性，很多中间派也开始动摇。
Z: Irinei gave quite the speech at our last meeting. It's clear the moderates are wavering over to his side.

康斯坦丁：……
Constantine: ...

副会长将一颗棋子放在桌面，推倒，看着它以弧形的轨迹滚动。
The Vice President sets a chess piece on the desk and flicks it. It rolls in a slow arc.

康斯坦丁：平衡仍在维持，现在还没有走到不顾后果的那一步。
Constantine: True, but there are still things we can do to maintain the balance. We must consider violence our last resort.

康斯坦丁：派遣一支特别行动小队到蒙佩去，把这件事给查清楚。
Constantine: Send a special unit to Montpaix. I need to figure out what really happened.

Z：“剃刀”小队目前在东线执行其他任务，无法及时转移到西线。
Z: "Razor" is on a mission at the eastern front; they won't be back in contact for several days.

Z：正在待命中的还有“暗喻”小队，“征兆”小队，“密涅瓦”小队……但他们都不适合执行战区调查任务。
Z: There are three squads presently available for deployment: codenames "Metaphor," "Omen," and "Minerva." But I don't believe any of them are suitable for this mission.

Z：不过，还有最近新组建的“Ⅻ”小队……
Z: We're left with only one option: the newly founded "XII."

康斯坦丁：刻雷乌斯的队伍……如果这件事能完成，他在基金会的履历能添上一条相当有价值的记录。
Constantine: That's Creius's team. I'm sure he'd be eager to buff up his resume with this mission; he's eager to prove himself.

Z：“Ⅻ”小队成员都是刻雷乌斯在夜巡特遣时期的老部下，他们与这项任务有较好的适配性。
Z: All the members of the "XII" used to work for Creius at the Vigiles Bureau. Their experience could be useful for this mission.

Z：他们过去侦破过一系列神秘学犯罪事件，其中多起案件都有重塑之手的参与。
Z: Many of the arcane crime cases they cracked involved the Manus.

康斯坦丁：我听说他最近和“鹰派”的成员走得很近，甚至与伊里内伊有过多次交谈。
Constantine: I understand he's been seen in the company of several prominent Hawks. He even spoke with Irinei several times.

Z：你认为他的政治立场不适合代表基金会接受这项任务？
Z: Are you suggesting his policy leanings could pose a problem?

康斯坦丁：不，正因如此，刻雷乌斯才是一个更好的选择，让他出任前线调查的负责人能安抚“鹰派”的情绪。
Constantine: On the contrary, he'll make a fine choice precisely because his appearance at the front line will calm the Hawks' nerves.

Z：我明白了。
Z: Understood.

康斯坦丁：告诉刻雷乌斯，他和他的小队有2个小时的准备时间。
Constantine: Tell Creius he and his team will set off in two hours.

11TH-05 野菊花 / Chrysanthemum

“战争进行的每一月，每一天，每一小时……我们都在幻想，长官突然向我们宣布：战争结束了。”
"Since the first grenade exploded in our trench, we've been dreaming of the moment when the guns fall silent and our commander calls out 'The war is over.'"

“元帅们会在宫殿里与皇帝杯盏相碰，军官们胸前会别上闪亮的勋章……而我们，终于可以回家了。”
"The marshals will attend the victory banquet in His Majesty's palace, the officers will pin shiny medals on their chests, and we will get to go home."

布劳恩少校：让开——让路，不要堵住过道。
Major Braun: Out of my way, soldiers! I said make way!

威严的号令在蜿蜒曲折的战壕中传递，老兵们神色漠然地斜靠在壁上。
His call to arms is passed through the winding trenches, passing over veterans slumped against the walls with indifference.

埃里希：搞什么？
Erich: What's wrong?

营长布劳恩少校在一处拐角现身，紧随其后的是一长串低着头的新兵队列。
Major Braun, the battalion commander, storms around a corner, followed by a long line of recruits with heads bowed.

布劳恩少校：2连？威利？
Major Braun: Wilhelm, 2nd Company.

威利：在，长官。
Wilhelm: Yes, Major.

2连长勉力挺直了身体。
Wilhelm straightens up, meeting the eyes of his commander.

布劳恩少校指了指身后的新兵队列——其中有不少东欧面孔。
Major Braun points to the line of recruits behind him, their faces blank and strangely foreign.

布劳恩少校：这些小伙子归你了，他们会补到你的连里。另外你得给我从里面挑出几个能当突击队的人。
Major Braun: You'll be in charge of these runts from now on, and I'll need you to choose the pick of this litter to join the stormtroopers.

威利：……是，少校。
Wilhelm: Yes, Major.

少校拍了拍胖威利的肩膀，随后一只脚踩在射击台上。
The major claps Wilhelm on his shoulder and boldly steps up to a firing position.

他清了清嗓子。
He clears his throat.

布劳恩少校：士兵们，我不得不向你们通告一件悲剧性的事件，它就发生在半小时之前。
Major Braun: Soldiers, I have some bad news.

布劳恩少校：在中立的谈判现场，敌人的狙击手杀害了我方的谈判代表希施费尔德上校。
Major Braun: Half an hour ago in Montpaix, at the site of this so-called parley, our representative, Colonel Hirschfelder, was assassinated by a French sniper.

罗尔夫：什……什么？
Rudolph: Wh-What?

一顶顶钢盔不安地转动着。
Helmets swivel, voices turn from sharp whispers to despair.

埃里希：他妈的！他在说什么胡话？敌人怎么可能跑到战线后面去？
Erich: Nonsense! What the devil is he talking about?! How could a sniper have made it so far behind our lines!

威利：嘘——
Wilhelm: Shh!

营长没有理会身下的骚动。
The major stands above the murmurs.

布劳恩少校：那些懦弱与卑劣的人想用这种方式来散播恐惧。
Major Braun: Soldiers! We can't let our enemies sow fear within our ranks!

布劳恩少校：可他们没有想到，这种行径反而会增强我们同仇敌忾的决心。很快，他们就将尝到可耻行为的后果！
Major Braun: Let their desperate attack bring us together and give us the strength to destroy them once and for all! They will pay in blood for what they've done!

议论、疑惑与愤懑不解的声音在壕沟内杂糅出一阵不祥的嗡鸣。
The mingling of voices churns into an ominous hum within the trench.

埃里希：见鬼了，不是说要停火了吗？
Erich: What the hell! I thought this was finally going to end.

罗尔夫：说实在的，我不在乎……这一切，我都不在乎。
Rudolph: I can't. I can't even force myself to care.

布劳恩少校：……他们憎恨我们，想将我们的祖国彻底毁灭，而我们的仇恨只会比他们更多——回答我！
Major Braun: With hate and rage, they scheme to destroy our fatherland! But we march against them with the strength and cunning of wolves! Will you stand with me, soldiers? Will you stand for the Kaiser and for victory?!

士兵们：是，少校！
Soldiers: Yes, Major!

布劳恩少校：很好。
Major Braun: Very good!

布劳恩少校：这是我需要的回答，这是所有好汉该做出的回答——我知道你们都是这样的好汉。
Major Braun: You've shown me your steel, soldiers! You are the pride of the fatherland!

布劳恩少校：胜利必将属于我们，保持这样的信念——现在，回到你们的位置上去！
Major Braun: Victory lies ahead, ready for the taking! Now, take up your rifle and get back to your positions!

少校的即兴演讲结束，他离开了射击台，带着剩下的士兵向另一个连队的驻地走去。
With his impromptu speech over, he drops down from the firing platform and leads a further cadre down the line.

一些新兵留在了原地，他们中的不少人都携带着沉重的包裹。
Second Company's new recruits tote bags so heavy they look liable to sink into the mud.

2连的老兵们慢慢围了上来。
The company's vets close in to offer relief.

埃里希：嘿，老弟，你们手里拎着的是什么？——牛排吗？
Erich: Hey, boy, what's that you're holding? You got a fresh tin? Verbena? Sausages?

新兵们对提问充耳不闻。
Their questions slide off the recruits, slipping down through the cracks of the boards at their feet.

少数人从钢盔的阴影下抬起头，瞪着怪异的圆眼睛，与衣衫褴褛的老兵对视。
Some glance up from under oversized helmets, wide eyes locking with the tattered vets.

埃里希：嚯！妈的，你看见他们的眼神了吗？他们好像在挑衅我们。
Erich: God! Did you see the way they looked at us? It was like there was nothing behind their eyes.

罗尔夫：……埃里希，他们……可能听不懂我们说的话。
Rudolph: Erich, did you notice ... I don't think they understood a word you said.

埃里希：嘁！——该死的可怜鬼。
Erich: Shameful.

埃里希猛一甩手，摇着头离去。
Erich throws a hand in the air, shaking his head as he walks off.

热心的威利有身为连长的义务，他宽慰般地拍了拍新兵的头盔。
But Wilhelm musters up his sense of obligation as company commander, patting a recruit's helmet enthusiastically.

威利：来吧，好小子，跟我来，我先带你们把东西放下。
Wilhelm: Come on, boys, follow me. I'll show you to your dugout.

威利：注意脚下，别被木板的缝隙绊倒。
Wilhelm: Mind the gaps on the duckboards.

罗尔夫：威利，我想你该教他们如何分辨炮弹的声音，就像我第一次来的时候那样。
Rudolph: Wil—er, Mr. Hauptmann, perhaps first we should drill them on keeping their heads down and avoiding artillery. Remember how many comrades we lost in our first days?

威利：这种事……总会有机会的，现在——
Wilhelm: Not now. First we need to ...

罗尔夫：——！
Rudolph: ...!

威利：——寻找掩体！
Wilhelm: Take cover!

威利：快！快躲进去——别愣着！
Wilhelm: Get in there! Move!

又一具尸体得到埋葬。铁锹插入泥土。
Another body slumps to the ground. A shovel bites into the earth beside it.

炮火落在地平线上，仿佛有一只怪兽在沿着地平线一路狂奔。
The sound of artillery rumbles through the woods like a distant storm.

卡戎：……这片土地还无法得到安宁。
Charon: It seems peace lies beyond our grasp.

他俯身，轻轻刨开泥土，试着完整地取出一只腐烂一半的断臂。
He crouches and brushes aside some caked mud from a half-rotten arm.

收尸人未能注意到从山坡下开始，逐渐接近的脚步声。
He doesn't notice, or pays no heed to, the soft scrape of metal ascending up the hill.

玛尔纱：卡戎？
Marsha: Charon?

卡戎的动作逐渐凝滞，直到陷入静止。随后，他站起身。
His hands go still. Then he rises.

卡戎：……
Charon: ...

他看向来者，未发一语。
He lingers wordlessly on the face that greets him.

玛尔纱：——你忘记我了吗？
Marsha: You don't remember who I am?

卡戎：不……我需要一些时间才能反应过来。我没有注意到你接近，一些过去的事故钝化了我的感知。
Charon: Your presence is familiar, but faces and names come slowly. There are so many memories here. It can be difficult to tell what is ... from what was.

玛尔纱：那下次我会多等你一会儿。
Marsha: I'll wait a little longer next time.

山坡底部，一块风格独特的石质纪念碑吸引了她的目光。
Marsha turns her eyes to a stone monument placed at the base of the hill.

那是一块倾斜着放置在地面上的石板，雕饰以精美的纹路。
A slanted slab, laid flat on the ground, etched with elegant carvings.

玛尔纱：爱国者们……这块纪念碑是你自己雕刻的吗？
Marsha: The Patriots? Did you make this cenotaph?

卡戎：不是出自我。一位陌生人捐赠了这块纪念碑。
Charon: A stranger brought it here. A gift for the dead.

玛尔纱：喔……
Marsha: I see ...

玛尔纱：艾伯哈特·布劳恩少校的包裹，我给你送来了。
Marsha: I found your major's package. Here.

她将一只单薄的信封交到收尸人手中，一同送出的还有一纸手写的便签。
She hands the figure a thin envelope—along with it, a handwritten note.

玛尔纱：这张纸条是从前线来的指令，布劳恩少校命令你立刻到营部报道。他不知道你去了哪儿，就把信件送到蒙佩了。
Marsha: A message came for you, I think. From the front. It seems your major needs you to report back immediately.

卡戎展开便签，用相当严谨的态度读完了简短的指令。
Charon unfolds the note.

卡戎：我明白了，很快我就会离开。
Charon: Yes. Soldiers must go where they are ordered.

玛尔纱：还有一件事……刺杀事件发生之后，蒙佩的新任负责人是刻雷乌斯，他很快就会抵达。
Marsha: Another thing. They're sending a new head of security to oversee the safe zone.

玛尔纱：他是一个高个子的红发男人，负责刺杀事件的后续调查，有任何需要的话，你可以与他联络。
Marsha: His name is Creius, a tall man with red hair. He'll be responsible for investigating the assassination. You can contact him if you need anything.

玛尔纱：基金会已经加强了周边道路的警戒，你应该不会遇到……
Marsha: The Foundation has already tightened security on every road to the town. I don't think you'll run into ...

？？？：……
???: ...

她出现在杂草丛生的土路上。
She appears once again on a weed-choked dirt path.

玛尔纱：……危险——分子？
Marsha: ... any danger on your way back.

雨披，步枪，以及那独特的头饰——玛尔纱绝不会认错。
Raincloak, rifle, that distinctive headpiece—Marsha could never mistake her.

玛尔纱：是你——
Marsha: You're ...

玛尔纱向前迈出一大步，却出乎意料地遭到墓地看护人的阻拦。
Marsha steps forward, only to be blocked by the gravekeeper.

卡戎：冷静，玛尔纱，请不要在死者长眠之地制造更多的纷争。
Charon: The dead rest here. They have seen enough violence.

玛尔纱：可是，你也许不知道，但——
Marsha: You don't know what she did. She ...

急促的气流在紧紧咬住的牙缝间穿梭。即使她已经在努力克制自己的情绪，但手仍然不自觉地攀上武器。
A burst of breathy air rushes out behind clenched teeth. Though she tries to restrain herself, her hand climbs up to the sidearm at her waist.

玛尔纱：难道你认识她？
Marsha: Do you know her?

卡戎：是她为这片墓地捐赠了你刚刚看过的纪念碑……
Charon: She brought the cenotaph to honor the dead.

？？？：……
???: ...

陌生人未发一语地来到纪念碑前，垂首伫立，对身旁的敌意毫不在意。
The stranger walks to the monument, standing perfectly still before it and paying no heed to either of them.

她从披风中取出一枝白色的野菊花。
She pulls a single white wild chrysanthemum from her cloak.

在柔软花瓣的衬托下，吊唁者手上的石质皮肤格外显眼。
Her stone-like skin stands out against the soft petals.

玛尔纱：石质的……皮肤？还有这个头饰……
Marsha: Her skin ... It looks as if it were made of stone. And that headwear, I feel I've seen it elsewhere.

玛尔纱：难道……不……
Marsha: Could you possibly be ...

空气中出现了沙哑的念诵声。身处近旁的人，也不自觉地聆听未曾听闻的祷词。
Then a soft rumble, grumbling chanting. Even without hearing the words, she understands what it is: prayer.

？？？：……残破的躯壳将被遗弃，漫长的苦修行将落幕。
???: The broken shell is abandoned, granting an end to endless penance.

？？？：……愿灵魂能安然穿越黑夜中林立的廊柱。
???: May thy souls travel through the arches from darkness to peace.

？？？：……无畏血红之眼的注视，直至抵达永恒至福的国度。
???: May thy path be unfettered by eyes of red as you reach for paradise.

白色的花被放置在纪念碑前。
The white flower is left at the foot of the stone.

？？？：……
???: ...

她默想片刻，随后，在空气中勾勒出一道奇特的图形。
She pauses in thought, then traces a strange shape in the air.

仪式结束了，吊唁者转过身，对上玛尔纱满是戒备的目光。
The ritual is over. The mourner turns and meets Marsha's guarded eyes.

？？？：又见面了，小骑士。
???: We meet again, young knight.

11TH-06 反战宣言 / A Push for Peace

陌生人再次端详起玛尔纱。
The stranger studies Marsha again.

“哨兵”：不易动怒的，胜过勇士；能克制己心的，强于攻城。
Sentinel: He that is slow to anger is better than the mighty, and he that ruleth his spirit than he that taketh a city.

玛尔纱：——什么？
Marsha: Pardon?

“哨兵”：我喜欢你的冷静。
Sentinel: You possess remarkable self-control. A trait seldom seen.

莫名所以的赞许令战地医生有些摸不着头脑。
A hint of approval, odd and unspoken, leaves Marsha unsure how to react.

玛尔纱：我有问题要问你。
Marsha: My thanks. But I have a question.

“哨兵”：正好，我也需要一个答案。
Sentinel: As I have one for you.

玛尔纱：为什么你要刺杀上校？
Marsha: Why did you kill the colonel?

“哨兵”：我们的问题是相对的——为什么要保护希施费尔德？
Sentinel: Answer me likewise: why did you protect him?

玛尔纱指向身旁的山坡，简陋的墓碑伫立在纵横交错的沟壑中。
Marsha gestures toward the slope to the row of crude headstones filling the ridge.

玛尔纱：因为不要再让更多人遭到战争的摧残。
Marsha: We're trying to end the war.

“哨兵”：我也一样。
Sentinel: And I, as well.

玛尔纱：你杀死的人是停火的希望，你有什么资格为这些死去的人献花？
Marsha: You seem to mourn the dead, but you don't realize how far you've set us back? We were nearing a ceasefire.

身下，苍白的花儿在干燥的风中翻滚。
Petals from pale flowers tumble by in the dry wind.

“哨兵”轻轻靠前一步，用雨披挡住冷风，不至于让野菊花过早地被风吹走。
Sentinel leans forward, gently shielding the flowers from the wind with her cloak.

“哨兵”：战争已经进行了六年，和平不像你所想的那样容易到来。你对你——还有基金会在做的事情了解多少？
Sentinel: 6 years, and the war rages still. Do you think ending bloodshed is as simple as to say: 'tis done? Have you any mind of the mission the Foundation pursues here?

玛尔纱：我们很清楚自己在做什么。
Marsha: We know it won't be simple.

玛尔纱：总参谋部有停火的意愿，所以他们才派出代表——
Marsha: Yet each side was open to negotiation. That's why they sent ...

“哨兵”：呵——
Sentinel: Heh.

她轻声嘲笑，仿佛看到一只试图证明自己更强大的小动物。
The chuckle is wry and dark.

“哨兵”：如果你们清楚，就不会把希施费尔德当成和谈的希望。
Sentinel: You placed false hope on Hirschfelder. You invited a wolf into a bed of lambs.

“哨兵”：也许在你们看来，他的死导致前线战火重燃，可是……即使我不杀他，谈判也注定会失败。
Sentinel: You think his death to be the spark of a reignited war, but, even if I had stayed my hand from him, your plans would have been for naught.

“哨兵”：重塑之手早已做好了计划。
Sentinel: The Manus scheme and the wicked prosper.

玛尔纱：——！
Marsha: ...!

玛尔纱：你接触过重塑之手？
不，难道你的意思是说——希施费尔德是重塑之手的成员？
Marsha: Manus Vindictae. You know of their plans? Then, you're claiming that Hirschfelder was a Manus?

片刻的沉默之后，狙击手开始讲述。
She lets the question linger long enough to feel unanswered, then the sniper begins.

“哨兵”：与重塑之手有牵连的人分为两类。
Sentinel: He is not one of those devils. He is only one tool of many.

“哨兵”：希施费尔德是第一类。他们与重塑之手合作，换取继续战争的资源和技术。
Sentinel: The Manus offer the gifts of Mammon and Asmodeus: greed and destruction. Hirschfelder was tempted by their technologies and became a willing servant in their schemes.

远处，遥远的炮火声如受困巨兽的哀嚎，它越过山头，滚落到公墓所处的谷地中。
A groan rises up from the horizon, the sound of distant artillery drumming, throbbing like the heartbeat of a wounded beast.

刺杀军官的狙击手伸出了第二根指头。
She raises a second finger.

“哨兵”：第二种，是重塑之手通过神秘学手段影响的普通人。这些人对战争与荣誉抱有狂热到异常的渴望。
Sentinel: But others serve them unknowing, affected by an arcane skill which clouds their eyes in red mists, driven to blood and glory as a starving dog is to the hunt.

解说者的目光转向一旁缄口不言的收尸人。
Her eyes shift to the stiff outline of a soldier she knows as Charon.

“哨兵”：你的营长，艾伯哈特·布劳恩是第二种。
Sentinel: Your commander, Eberhard Braun, bears that mist.

卡戎：……
Charon: ...

士官缓慢地理解着对方话语中的含义。再次开口时，他的语调产生了微不可察的变化。
It takes a moment for the words to find some impact. When he speaks again, there seems to be a change in his voice.

卡戎：你会杀死他吗？——就像希施费尔德一样。
Charon: Then will you see that death comes to him, as you did Hirschfelder?

“哨兵”：这取决于他的死会带来多少价值。
Sentinel: That is not yet certain. I do not kill without purpose.

布劳恩少校的士官未作回答，即使面部被遮盖，仍能从他身上看出一种陷于困顿的茫然。
Charon does not seem to find a reply, his mask concealing any trace of emotion.

玛尔纱：你刚刚说的那些……与重塑之手有关的话，你要怎么证明？
Marsha: What you just said about the Manus ... Can you confirm any of it?

玛尔纱：如果你知道些什么，基金会可以听取你的信息，我们可以达成合作。
Marsha: The Foundation could make use of any intelligence you have. We may be able to save these peace talks.

玛尔纱：至少，你可以先证明对希施费尔德上校的指控——
Marsha: But we will need proof.

“哨兵”：我不会自证。
Sentinel: All is vain. There is nothing new under the sun.

“哨兵”：我尝试过，而且也已因此受到过审判与侮辱。
那些靴子上连泥点都没有的大人物从来不会在乎士兵们能证明什么。
Sentinel: When I told my commander about the Manus, all I received for my effort was scorn. Their eyes were not satisfied with seeing, nor their ears with hearing. Kings and generals yet still turn a blind eye to the suffering.

“哨兵”：如果他们有能力理解前线士兵万分之一的痛苦，这场战争在一开始就会结束。
Sentinel: If they had a shred of the light of God within them, they would never have pursued this war.

“哨兵”：对于你们——我不相信一群官僚能带来和平。
Sentinel: As for the Foundation ... That which is crooked cannot be made straight, and what is wanting cannot be numbered. I have no faith in them.

她收回目光，拉住雨披的一角，将自己紧紧裹住。
She looks away, pulling her cloak tighter.

“哨兵”：到此为止。
Sentinel: That is all I have to say.

卡戎：……请你——
Charon: Spare him.

在吊唁者即将离去的那一刻，卡戎突然开口，似乎方才他一直在试图理解前者对他说过的最后一句话。
Charon speaks, the change in his voice now more acute, more vivid, and more personal.

卡戎：——请你给艾伯哈特·布劳恩一个生存的机会，我会让他活着变得更有……价值。
Charon: Eberhard Braun. I need you to spare his life.

“哨兵”：这与我无关。
Sentinel: Neither mercy nor vengeance is mine to give.

“1920年，战争已经成为一种混杂不清的总体印象，它被灌注以多种形式的英雄主义与悲伤情绪。”
"It is officially 1920. I wonder at other people's impressions of this war; from what I've seen, there are two contrasting views—though in various forms—one of heroism and the other, sadness."

“它塑造出一种残酷的现实性观念：战争必然是新时代的序曲。”
"There is one truth which I have found bridges both of these visions, despite how cruel it may sound—'This war is the prelude of a new era.'"

“如若不然……如若千万计的死亡只是旧时代的一场阵痛，那么我们的文明观念将被彻底粉碎。”
"I have to believe that ... Because if this death and destruction so unparalleled in history does not herald change, then there is no hope for humanity."

刻雷乌斯：人去楼空啊。
Creius: How bleak.

“Ⅻ”小队队长站在蒙佩的街道上，凝视着希施费尔德上校遇害的现场。
The leader of the "XII" stands on the streets of Montpaix, looking over where Colonel Hirschfelder was killed.

他抵达时，所有军方人员已经从安全区撤走，只有少数仍在值守的基金会人员守着略显凄凉的废墟。
By the time he arrives, all other military forces have withdrawn. Only the Foundation remains on site to guard the ruins of the town.

“警官”：“乌鸫”，过来帮把手。
"Officer": Blackbird, give me a hand.

梅蕾尔：等我吃完这口，“警官”……
Merel: As soon as I finish my bread, Beagle.

随他一同抵达的小队成员正在重新布置镇子内的防御工事，如今他们的防线已经收缩到了街道的一角。
His team has already begun shoring up the town's defenses. Their line pulled back to just a corner of the street.

基金会安保：长官，除了您本人的小队成员，目前可供调遣的武装人员共有122名，其中23人为神秘学家。
Foundation Security Staff: There are 122 armed personnel available at your disposal, sir. 23 of them are arcanists.

基金会安保：这是他们的个人资料，请您过目。
Foundation Security Staff: I've brought you their profiles.

男人接过安保队员递来的人事资料，目光转向悬挂着基金会旗帜的临时指挥所。
He takes the personnel file from the security staff member, eyes shifting toward the makeshift HQ flying the Foundation flag.

刻雷乌斯：我会仔细阅读，现在请你回到岗位。重点确保指挥所的安全。
Creius: Right then. I'll read through these. Now get back to your position. I need eyes on our command post.

基金会安保：明白。
Foundation Security Staff: Yes, sir.

安保人员转身离去。与此同时，身穿甲胄的战地医生迎上前来。
The staff member walks away. And in the same moment, a curiously armored field medic approaches.

刻雷乌斯：是你，玛尔纱。
Creius: Marsha, is it?

玛尔纱：你知道我的名字，刻雷乌斯长官？
Marsha: You recognize me, Mr. Creius?

刻雷乌斯：我在路上读过你的报告——关于在森林和公墓中遇见的狙击手。
Creius: I read your report on my way here. You're the one that encountered our sniper. Twice now, I hear.

玛尔纱：嗯，在报告里我遗漏了两件事——刺杀事件发生时，有个不知名的人通过基金会的通讯器向我发出了警告。
Marsha: Correct. I have some additional details about my encounters. The first is that I appear to have been followed out into the forest the first time. I was warned on my device just after the shooting.

刻雷乌斯：这件事不用在意，第二件呢？
Creius: Never mind that. What about the other thing?

玛尔纱：不用……好的，另一件事是，那名狙击手应该是一个石像鬼。
Marsha: That doesn't concern you? Fine. The other thing is that I have reason to believe our sniper is a Gargoyle.

刻雷乌斯：石像鬼？
Creius: A Gargoyle?

玛尔纱：没错，这支神秘学家族裔中的一部分人在大战中加入了军队，作为神秘术反制与支援部队投入战场。
Marsha: There are records of Gargoyles participating in this war as part of arcane skill response units.

玛尔纱：他们能石化自己的器官，抵挡轻武器和流弹的伤害。同时，石像鬼似乎有方法让人忽视他们的存在……
Marsha: They're able to petrify their bodies at will, making them immune to small-caliber arms, and I believe they're able to render themselves undetectable.

刻雷乌斯：你之前和石像鬼有过交手？
Creius: Sounds as if you've fought them before.

长官的提问令报告人陷入了短暂的低落，但后者还是如实回答了问题。
The assumption pierces her more cleanly than any bullet, but she forces the emotion down, giving an answer as truthful as she can bear.

玛尔纱：……可以这么说。
Marsha: You could say that.

刻雷乌斯：所以，她是通过特殊的神秘术绕过了基金会对蒙佩的监视……应该向总部申领反制神秘术的监测设备……
Creius: It would go far to explain how she managed to enter Montpaix without being noticed. I'll have to ask HQ to send us a counter-arcanum device.

刻雷乌斯：对希施费尔德的刺杀有极强的针对性，她或许掌握了相当多关于重塑之手的情报……
Creius: She shot the colonel, but then slipped out, leaving our own agents unharmed. We can't be sure of anything, but we can't rule out that she may possess reliable intel about the Manus.

一阵急促的脚步声打断了刻雷乌斯的思考。
Rushed footsteps interrupt Creius's thoughts.

？？？：刻雷乌斯先生？
???: Mr. Creius?

一名孤独的访客突然造访，他穿着体面的服装，却难掩刚刚经过一路颠沛的现状。
The newcomer is obviously out of place—the sort of well-dressed that usually comes with fanfare.

格奥尔格：我是跨党团委员会的代表，格奥尔格。我希望代表帝国议会与基金会就和平谈判展开新的交涉。
Georg: I am Georg Kramer from the Inter-Factional Committee. I've come on behalf of the parliament to start another round of negotiation with the Foundation.

刻雷乌斯：和平谈判已经被取消了，格奥尔格先生，蒙佩已经没有政治的空间。
Creius: Didn't you get the message? The parley has been canceled, Mr. Kramer. Seems there's no more room for negotiations.

刻雷乌斯：基金会仍然留在这里，只是为了追查重塑之手的踪迹。
Creius: My job now is to investigate the possible involvement of Manus Vindictae.

议员向前一步，虽然他谨慎地压低了声音，但仍旧难掩一丝急促的激动情绪。
The visitor steps forward. Though he lowers his voice, a trace of urgency and excitement leaks through.

格奥尔格：……我正是为这个目的而来，先生。
Georg: Precisely what I'm here for, sir.

格奥尔格：我得到了基金会的警告——重塑之手正在掌控军队的权力，我对这样的前景深感担忧。
Georg: We received a warning from the Foundation that Manus Vindictae has infiltrated our armed forces and is attempting to usurp our rightful authority. I am worried this may be true.

格奥尔格：我们的国家已站在崩溃的边缘，从政治与理智上来说，这场战争毫无继续下去的理由。
Georg: I do not intend to lie, sir; Germany lies on the verge of total collapse. Both politically and rationally speaking, we have no reason to continue this war.

格奥尔格：总参谋部却对国内的艰难困境视而不见，如此失控地继续推动战争，我严重怀疑有重塑之手参与其中。
Georg: Yet it seems our army command is out of control; they are determined to drive this war to its bitter end regardless of the misery and death they're causing. And I have reason to believe the Manus are behind it.

刻雷乌斯：这么说，这是总参谋部并不知情的秘密造访。
Creius: I take it Army Command is not aware of your visit then, Mr. Kramer.

一针见血的判断令对方稍有尴尬。
The observation is sharp, to the point, and, quite obviously, correct.

或许是想显露出一些权威性，跨党团代表忽然整顿了一番自己的仪态。
Perhaps to reassert some authority, the man arches his shoulders back, adopting an almost regal pose.

格奥尔格：我代表的是帝国议会中的大多数，在和平问题上，首相也站在我们这一边。
Georg: I represent the majority of the parliament, sir, as well as the office of the Imperial Chancellor.

格奥尔格：几乎所有党派都已经联合起来，我们需要的只是一份压倒性的证据。
Georg: We are united now. All we need is some hard evidence.

格奥尔格：如果我能向皇帝和议会证明，军队已经被邪教团体掌控，他们将立刻倒台。
Georg: If it can be proven to His Imperial Majesty and to the chancellor that Army Command has been infiltrated by this Manus cult, I am certain we will have the authority to end this.

刻雷乌斯：也就是说，你希望我向你分享追查重塑之手的结果，用以对抗军队的权力。
Creius: So, you're asking me to share the result of my investigation to root out the rotten apples in your army.

格奥尔格：没错，在议会取得决定权之后，我们会尽一切努力推动和平谈判。
Georg: I am, sir. We'll do everything we can to restart the parley once we take control.

他郑重其事地点头，突如其来的冬季风还是将他的头发与衣领吹乱。
His head bows deep and serious, though the sudden winter wind tosses his hair and collar out of place.

他深吸一口气。
He pulls in a deep breath.

格奥尔格：我们愿意接受一定限度的有条件和平。当然，这不只是因为我所代表的政治立场。
Georg: And we're willing to reach a ceasefire on certain conditions. I assure you I'm not just saying this because of my stance ...

格奥尔格：为了国家和人民的未来，这场战争绝不能再继续下去了。
Georg: For the sake of my country and its people, this war must be stopped.

11TH-07 人的样貌 / Under the Veil

“在前线的前三个月，我对敌人一无所知，也不了解战壕对面究竟有什么。另一边仿佛立着一堵黑色的墙。”
"In the first three months, I had no idea who I was fighting or what lay on the other side of the trenches. It was as if there were a black wall standing between us and our enemy."

“即将到来的攻势让我彻夜难眠。我害怕被杀……不知为何，我也害怕看清敌人的样貌。”
"They could attack at any time. I can't sleep. I don't want to die. I don't want to see their faces. I don't want to know what our enemy looks like. And worst of all, I don't know why."

当士官抵达战壕时，袭扰性的炮击已经结束。除了侧翼偶尔传来一阵急促的重机枪点射，总体而言，前线恢复了平静。
By the time Charon returns to the trenches, the most recent bombardment has already ended. A trench can never really be called calm, but the rattle of machine guns and the crack of rifles slow and fade into the background.

炮火没有给战场带来更多改变——无非是一些新的弹坑取代了旧的弹坑。
The shelling hasn't changed much—a few new craters to replace the old ones.

埃里希：哦……你回来了，邮递员——弗兰兹呢？
Erich: Ah so, you're back, mailman. Tell us, where did you take little Franz?

卡戎：他已安然入土。
Charon: He lies beneath stone in a silent wood and marches no more.

埃里希闷哼一声，跺了跺脚上的新靴子，以作回应。
Erich grunts out a reply. He's standing in Franz's boots—freshly shined.

埃里希：……我和威利打赌，你会利用这个机会逃跑。看来我输了。
Erich: Hmph. I bet Mr. Willi you'd take the opportunity to keep walking and never come back. Lucky me.

卡戎：威利呢？
Charon: Where is he?

埃里希：他死了。现在我是连长了。
Erich: He's dead. I guess you'll call me "Mr. Captain" now.

埃里希看向身侧，似乎这里就是威利阵亡的地方。
Erich casts his eyes to a new crater decorating their trench.

埃里希：他挨了一炮，肩膀不见了。
Erich: He caught a shell. Just like that.

他的脸色不太好看，以至于显得有些恼怒，头顶一些发青的血管在跳动。
Erich's face pales and then runs flush red, throbbing veins straining out along his forehead.

埃里希：那家伙运气不好……他妈的——！
Erich: Lucky me. Unlucky him. That bastard!

他突然暴怒而起，三两步上前揪住士官的衣领。
He rushes to Charon, grabbing him by the collar.

埃里希：这里完全就是一片地狱，你回这鬼地方来干什么？为什么不走？！
Erich: He died, and now who do I pay up to? Why'd you even bother coming back? We have enough ghosts in this goddamn trench!

他愤怒地将士官摔在战壕的胸墙上。
Erich pulls Charon up and tosses him against the trench wall.

埃里希：四处捡一些死尸会让你好过吗？你能教会我们像你一样死而复生吗？！——你在耀武扬威吗！
Erich: You waltz through here whenever you like just to take away our brothers. You bury them. Why? Why do you get to return and they stay dead? Are you mocking us?

被摔出去的一方只是勉强站直身子，没有反抗的意思。
Charon slumps but does not fall, making no effort to fight against Erich's strength.

卡戎：……请原谅我。在这场战争中我能做的并不多，许多事情只会让我感到无能为力，埃里希。
Charon: Death does not mock. Nor can it stop its return. It is as helpless as any other soldier to do his duty.

卡戎：我对自己的命运也一无所知，死亡的黑暗笼罩在战场之上，我看不见前进的道路。
Charon: What fate lies ahead of us is unknown; its winding path cannot be seen until we step through it. None choose the hour when death finds us.

埃里希：嘁——
Erich: S**t!

埃里希燥热的情绪极速冷却下去，就像刚刚什么也没有发生。
A curse, flat and empty, and just like that, the fire and fury are gone from him.

战壕里的士兵对此早已习以为常，他们甚至连抬头观看这场争执的兴趣也没有。
Soldiers walk by, look away, and continue their work. A hundred pairs of eyes, and each of them numb to the chaotic scene.

埃里希：我会尽量死得好看点，记得把我收拾干净。
去送你的信吧。
Erich: I just want to keep myself in one piece when my time comes. Better make sure I look good for my funeral, alright? Now, off you go.

观察员：——连长，过来看看。
Spotter: Sir, there's movement coming from no man's land.

执勤的观察员打断了二人的交谈，他递给埃里希一柄战壕潜望镜。
The spotter interrupts their standoff, handing Erich a trench periscope.

埃里希：看到什么了？
Erich: What?

埃里希拿过潜望镜，趴在胸墙壁上向无人区窥视。
Erich grabs the scope and crouches up to a nearby parapet.

埃里希：嗯……我看到了……两个人。突击队？
Erich: Hmm, that's just two soldiers. Could it be a trench raid?

观察员：不可能。现在是白天，他们不仅没有任何掩护，而且好像还在吸引我们的注意力。
Spotter: I don't think so, Mr. Captain. Why would they go over the top in broad daylight? Look, they're waving their arms.

埃里希：还真是，他们在挥手，这是找死吗？等等，他们手上都缠着绷带……
Erich: Huh? What are they doing? Wait, their hands are wrapped in bandages.

观察员：有什么问题吗？
Spotter: Is that a problem?

埃里希缩回战壕，把潜望镜还给观察员。
Erich returns the periscope to the spotter.

埃里希：拿好，你继续盯着他们。我大概明白是怎么回事了。
Erich: Keep your eye on them, soldier. I think I know what's going on.

卡戎：怎么回事？
Charon: The living walk over dead men's ground.

埃里希：这些人应该是对面的逃兵，我听过——他们会朝自己的手掌开枪自残，好回到后方去。但现在这事是要判死刑的。
Erich: Deserters, I'll bet. I heard some soldiers used to shoot their own palms so they could be sent back to the rear. But they reward that kind of cowardice with bullets nowadays.

卡戎：为什么要把他们送到无人区？
Charon: Do they come seeking death or life?

埃里希：最近有很多行刑队遇刺，这事儿多了之后，两边的军官就像形成了默契，直接把死刑犯扔到无人区等死。
Erich: With all the officers keeping their heads low, maybe they decided they don't want to do the punishing themselves? Just kick these poor bastards out of the trench and tell them to walk till they drop.

卡戎：……
Charon: ...

士官花了一些时间，让新与旧的记忆在脑中交错相连。
Old and new memories intertwine in Charon's mind, forming an incomplete but certain thought.

卡戎：他们没有战斗的意志，我们有理由安全地放他们过来。
Charon: They do not march to us as warriors but as broken men.

埃里希：……你说得没错，也就两个人。嘿，谁会法语？
Erich: You're right. Pass it down the line. Does anyone here speak French?

观察员：我……我可以试试。我在学校的时候学过半年的法语课。
Spotter: Yes. A little. I took some French back in school.

埃里希：那你来喊两句，动听点儿！
Erich: Hurry, hurry! Say something!

观察员：是，长官。
Spotter: Yes, Mr. Captain.

观察员将脑袋紧紧贴在沙袋上，尽可能让声音从射击口中传出去。
The spotter presses his head against the sandbags, trying to project his voice through the firing slit.

观察员：欸——喂——
Spotter: Hey, you, over there!

逃兵：……？！
Deserter: …?!

观察员：两个，你们——你们两个，放下武器，过来，不开枪，一定不开枪。
Spotter: Let go of your—er—weapons and ... ah—just come here!

观察员：我们——
Spotter: We ...

观察员：怎么回事？！
Spotter: What the ...!

埃里希：他妈的——是哪个天杀的开的枪？！
Erich: Goddamn! Who the hell shot him?

此刻，在相隔不远的另一条战壕。
Voices carry from around the trench line.

布劳恩少校：你还在等什么？！
Major Braun: What are you waiting for, soldier?

艾伯哈特·布劳恩少校站在战壕中，面色铁青。
The major's face is ashen and stiff.

罗尔夫：他已经死了！
Rudolph: I killed him.

罗尔夫发出惨叫般的回答。他趴在沙袋上，握住步枪的手一直在发抖，一缕灰色的烟雾仍在枪口萦绕。
Rudolph stammers out the words, lying propped up against a sandbag, wisps of gray smoke lingering out from his shaking rifle.

他有严重的近视，却反倒是营中最好的射手之一。
His glasses are thick as a church window, and still he's the best marksman in the company.

布劳恩少校：还有一个，你的眼睛终于是瞎了吗？
Major Braun: And the other bastard's still standing! Are you blind?

罗尔夫：他已经投降了，他们……他们都已经丢掉了武器。
Rudolph: But Mr. Major, he's surrendered. He ... dropped his weapon.

布劳恩少校：这是一个诡计，白痴，外面那些混账可能带着炸弹，或者是传染病。
Major Braun: It's a trap, you idiot! They have a bomb or some kind of infectious disease!

布劳恩少校：我们也没有东西来养这些俘虏。
Major Braun: Do you want to keep him, soldier? You going to share your rations with him?

罗尔夫：我们不需要照顾战俘，只要能把他们送到后方的战俘营去……或者基金会也可以——
Rudolph: Mr. Major, we're supposed to accept all prisoners. There are camps to send them to ... or even the safe zone.

罗尔夫：——！
Rudolph: ...!

军官的手枪抵住狙击手的胸口。
He pulls his pistol and points it at the marksman's chest.

布劳恩少校：干掉他，这是命令。
不然我也会把你送到外面去，让你看看对面的狙击手有没有同情心。
Major Braun: That was an order, soldier. You are to shoot that foreign devil, or I'll send you out to test if their snipers are as spineless as you are.

罗尔夫：我……我——
Rudolph: I-I ...

卡戎：——少校。
Charon: Major.

浑浊的呼唤声在壕沟中传递，麇集的士兵们很快让出了一条通道。
Rasping voices ripple down the trench as bodies make way for a figure moving like a charge in slow motion.

布劳恩少校循声望去。
Major Braun turns toward the sound.

布劳恩少校：你？——是什么让你迟到了这么久，这已经严重违反了军纪。
Major Braun: Charon? What took you so long? Don't you know I could have you shot for dereliction of duty?

卡戎：我会接受迟到的惩罚，但首先，我请求你收回给罗尔夫的命令，不要向逃兵开枪。
Charon: Punish the guilty then, but the man that stands alone is innocent. Spare him.

少校为这番忤逆的说辞感到惊愕，他锋利的目光移向自己的士官。
The statement is stunning in its sharpness. Defiance is not a trait Major Braun has come to expect from him.

布劳恩少校：你没有权力指使你的长官。
Major Braun: You are not entitled to challenge my authority, sergeant.

卡戎：逃兵已经放弃了战斗，我们没有理由再向他们开枪。
Charon: His war is over. His blood should not water these fields.

布劳恩少校：软弱！
Major Braun: Cowards!

少校向前大跨一步，逼向士官，军靴响亮地敲在战壕铺设的木板上。
Major Braun strides forward in a single step, boots thudding against the trench's wooden planks.

埃里希：妈的——
Erich: Bastard!

布劳恩少校：——这是在军队里蔓延的瘟疫，是外国人的小市民思想在我们年轻人心中种下的毒瘤。
Major Braun: You're just like those foreigners, poisoning the hearts of our youth with feckless sentimentality—your weakness, this fatalism—is a plague spreading through our ranks!

布劳恩少校：敌人想灭亡我们的祖国，而你却还在为他们求情。还有你所谓的墓地，卡戎，都是这种软弱的产物。
Major Braun: That man over there is a threat to our fatherland, yet you plead for his life!

他用逼迫性的目光扫视在场的其他人。
A single unblinking stare sweeps over the gathered soldiers, cowing each man into silence.

布劳恩少校：只有战争能塑造我们的民族，铁与血会消除我们心中的怯懦和卑微，我们由此才能与祖辈的荣耀相连接。
Major Braun: I won't let this cowardice ruin our nation! We will keep fighting until no man alive stands against us! Only through their blood and our tireless sacrifice will we grow fearless and retrieve the glory of our birthright!

卡戎：这场战争已经成了毫无意义的杀戮，少校，我们从中只会得到苦难、罪恶与悔恨。
Charon: There is no glory for the dead, Eberhard. Only suffering, guilt, and regret for those that remain.

卡戎：杀死一名逃兵无法在任何人心中铸造勇气与信念，只会让他们成为蔑视生命的屠夫。
Charon: No courage is found in the blood of the innocent, only stains that can never be washed out.

布劳恩少校：一派胡言！
Major Braun: Nonsense!

卡戎：这些话和我过去对你的了解完全不同，少校，我原以为是我的记忆出现了混淆……
Charon: I remember, you, Major Braun, my old friend, would never say these things.

卡戎：难道你在后方休假的那段时间，真的与重塑之手有过接——
Charon: What lies were whispered in your ears by Manus Vindictae?

布劳恩少校：闭嘴！——这是你从哪里听来的谣言？！
Major Braun: Shut up! That's slander! Who told you that?

卡戎：请你冷静，我只是想和你谈一谈——
Charon: I ... do not slander you, Mr. Major.

布劳恩少校：我命令你解释刚才的言行，士官！
Major Braun: Explain yourself. Explain all of this!

不受控制的咆哮如轰鸣的炮火一般砸在士官身上。
The man roars, and for a second time, Charon is slammed against the trench wall.

布劳恩少校：你在——指控我——什么？！
Major Braun: Lies—Manus Vindictae—what do you mean?

卡戎：……不要这样。
Charon: These are not your eyes.

布劳恩少校：回答我！！
Major Braun: Answer me!

他猝然挥出一记猛击。
But this man's fire does not temper. It bursts.

反应过慢的士官未能成功躲避，手枪握把狠狠地砸在他的头部。
Charon reacts too slowly to evade the pistol as it is smashed across his head.

布劳恩少校：……！
Major Braun: ...!

——少校自己都没有预料到会有这般动作。
Major Braun's eyes are fixed on the pistol in his hand, anger replaced with shock.

被击伤的士官停在原地，一只手扶着低垂的头。“帷幕”之下，仿佛有什么东西正在碎裂。
Charon, now wounded, raises his hand to meet his bowed head. Beneath the "curtain," something seems to crack.

卡戎：……
Charon: ...

布劳恩少校：…………把头抬起来。
Major Braun: Raise your head, sergeant.

卡戎：不，艾伯哈特……
Charon: Eberhard ...

布劳恩少校：是布劳恩少校。现在，我命令你抬起头。
Major Braun: Do not call me that! I am your superior officer. Damn! Obey my orders!
