卡戎：……我们都不应该走到这一步。
Charon: It should not have been this way.

士官缓缓抬头，沉闷而迟缓，似乎每一寸移动都要付出极大的代价。
He raises his head. The movement is heavy and labored.

一种庞大而空洞的物质带着令人诧异的宁静，降临在狭窄逼仄的战壕中。
A hollow and foreboding presence seems to fill the trench around them.

布劳恩少校：这是……什么？
Major Braun: Good heavens ...

卡戎：生者本不应目睹这番景象，艾伯哈特。
Charon: This is not a sight fit for the living, Eberhard.

卡戎：但也许，这能唤醒一些你的回忆……
Charon: But perhaps you must be reminded.

布劳恩少校：闭——闭嘴！把你的脸……给、给我遮住——
Major Braun: No! Your face. Cover it now!

卡戎：子弹与炮火下的战栗，战友死亡时的痛苦……为什么，你对此可以遗忘一空，或是视而不见？
Charon: Do you remember the fear as bombs exploded by our sides, the pain when our brothers moaned out their last breaths? Have you forgotten, or have you only hardened your heart?

布劳恩少校：你必须要明白，战争……咳——民族的前进，势必会有牺牲。
Major Braun: This war is ... *cough* sacrifice is necessary for a nation to make progress.

布劳恩少校：每一个士兵都应该明白，牺牲是莫大的光荣，正如同你，保罗——
Major Braun: Every soldier who has died for the fatherland should feel honored for their sacrifice! You should have been honored, Paul—

卡戎：我不是在谈论牺牲。
Charon: We do not speak of sacrifice now.

布劳恩少校：——！
Major Braun: ...!

卡戎：我是在谈论死亡——那与一切伦理无关，绝对的空洞与虚无本身，它是一个单纯的生存问题。
Charon: Death is not honored—death knows no ceremony, it holds no virtues, it is emptiness and void.

卡戎：战争已经让我们对死亡的态度变得比任何时候都要轻浮，恰如现在，艾伯哈特，你对生命丧失了敬意。
Charon: You have become so numb to death that you laugh as it walks among us. It is so close to you that you have mistaken it for life, Eberhard.

卡戎：无论战争的结果究竟如何，我们已经失败了。
Charon: There is nothing to be gained from this war that will pay for what we have already lost.

布劳恩少校：我是你——你的——长官，你想杀死——
Major Braun: You ... want me dead ... then kill me ... do it.

卡戎：我不想杀死任何人。
Charon: Death will not save you, old friend.

卡戎：我只是……希望你能拯救你自己。
Charon: I want you to save yourself.

布劳恩少校：我……啊……啊——！
Major Braun: I ... Ugh ...

士兵们缩在一旁。
The other soldiers huddle to the side.

艾伯哈特·布劳恩少校瘫倒在地，双目失神，面无血色，如同刚刚阵亡的士兵。
Major Braun collapses to the ground. His eyes swirl and then go blank, looking up and nowhere at the same time. His face is bone white and stiff as a corpse.

士官低下身，为他合上双眼，如同他已经为其他死者做过的千万次那般。
Charon kneels over him and closes his eyes. A motion all too familiar to those watching.

埃里希：……妈的，这是发生什么了？
Erich: S**t! What the hell just happened?

罗尔夫战战兢兢地从人群中探出头来。
Rudolph peeks out from the crowd, managing a question both timid and brave.

罗尔夫：少、少校他……死了吗？卡戎，你该不会……
Rudolph: Is Major Braun dead? Charon, you didn't ...

埃里希：你这是……来真的？
Erich: Did you?

士官站直身子，仍旧背向所有人，迟缓而严谨地重新戴好兜帽。
Charon stands, deliberately facing away from the crowd, replacing his mask and hood with careful precision.

卡戎：艾伯哈特不会有事，他仍然活着。我会处理好他。
Charon: He will live. We will leave here together.

卡戎：埃里希，现在你的级别最高，请你接手之后的事。
Charon: You have command, Erich. Make the right choices.

卡戎：另外，我需要处理一些……泄漏出来的东西。在此之前，请不要与我对视。
Charon: I don't want you to see what lies beneath. Please, look away.

埃里希还想再说些什么，最终还是选择闭嘴。
Words bulge at the edge of Erich's lips, but he swallows them back.

战壕内的士兵们还处在震撼之中，而卡戎已经带着艾伯哈特离开。
All others stand stunned and silent as Charon departs with Major Braun in tow.

埃里希：——啧。
Erich: *tut*

埃里希：行了，让活着的那个人进来，我会检查他是不是带着危险物品。
Erich: Alright. Someone grab that deserter. I'll search him.

埃里希：好了好了，别看了，动起来！那些倒霉的家伙还在外面啃泥巴呢。
Erich: Show's over. Move it, soldiers! That poor sap is still waiting. Get moving!

11TH-08 生命的半途 / Death of the Young

不要怕，保罗，参加战争会带给我们荣耀！只要团结在一起，我们不会畏惧任何敌人！
Heh. Don't worry so much, Paul! We'll find glory on the battlefield! No man can stop us as long as we stick together!

走吧，和我一起到征兵办公室去，让穆伦贝格先生知道我们都是男子汉，父母也一定会为我们而骄傲。
Come on, let's join the war and prove ourselves to Mr. Mühlenberge. Think how proud your parents will be—their son, a war hero!

保罗：——艾伯哈特！
Paul: Eberhard!

操——操！迪特里希在哪里？！
Goddamn! Where's Dieterich?

保罗：迪特里希和贝特克都死了——拿上机枪，我们该走了！快！
Paul: He and Baethke are dead! Grab that gun. We need to go! Move!

我们能打赢这场仗吗，保罗？
Do you think we'll win, Paul?

保罗：我不知道……我想回家。
Paul: I don't know, my friend. I think I just want to go home.

如果我们输了，迪特里希，贝特克，埃尔文……他们又是为什么死了？
Dieterich, Baethke, and Elvin ... What did they die for if we just give up?

起来，坚持下去，保罗，只要能打赢这场仗……他们的牺牲就有意义。
Hang in there, Paul! The only way to make their sacrifice count is to win!

我们说过要一起回家的——保罗……保罗！
We promised we'd go home together! Paul ... Paul!

？？？：布劳恩少校，你不该再为那些无谓的情感所纠缠。
???: Major, the past is in the past. You can't change anything by letting yourself be overcome by sorrow.

？？？：我会给你渴望的胜利……
???: Don't forget that victory is the only thing that matters, and we can give it to you.

胜利……你能做什么？
Give it to me? How?

？？？：我要让你成为真正的英雄——不再恐惧，不再犹疑，不再退缩……
???: I'll make you a true hero, one without fear or hesitation.

硝烟与血的味道散尽了。
Smoke and blood fade into the distance.

他感觉自己躺在一块木板上，被某种力量拖着前进。
Eberhard lies on a wooden board dragged by some unseen force.

艾伯哈特：咳……咳咳！
Eberhard: *cough*

先是一阵猛烈的咳嗽，随后，艾伯哈特如溺水者一般吞咽着空气。泥土中埋藏的腐烂腥气灌入他的肺腔。
He swallows air like a drowning man, and immediately the foul stench of decay fills his lungs.

拖行的力量消失了。
The dragging stops.

保罗：你醒了。
Paul: You're awake.

艾伯哈特：……保罗？
Eberhard: Paul?

士官默不作声。他低下身，握住艾伯哈特向前伸出的手，将他从地上扶起。
But the man behind the mask says nothing. He only offers a hand.

艾伯哈特：我的脑袋，天呐……好痛。
Eberhard: Ah. My head ... It hurts.

他双目失神地望着周身的景物，过了很长时间才找到视觉的焦点。
Eberhard struggles to adjust to his surroundings, taking a long time to find focus.

艾伯哈特：……你要带我去哪里？
Eberhard: Where are you taking me?

保罗：蒙佩，基金会也许有更专业的医生，能帮助你从神秘术的伤害中恢复过来。
Paul: Montpaix. The Foundation may have some cure for the spell you have fallen under.

艾伯哈特：不……不不……
Eberhard: No ... No ...

从噩梦中苏醒的人仍处在一片混乱之中，他只是一味地在否定着什么。
Still dazed after the ordeal, he can only mutter in denial.

他茫然无措地四下张望，似乎是要寻找什么可以依托的东西。最终他又瘫坐在地面，脱下帽子，抓挠着稻草般的金发。
He looks around, searching for something to brace against, eventually finding the ground. He takes off his hat and scratches at his straw-like golden hair.

艾伯哈特：我……天呐，我做了什么——
Eberhard: I ... Good heavens. What did I do?

他仍在喘气，却无论如何都无法让窒息感消失。
He still can't find his breath, each gasp of air only making the choking sensation worse.

艾伯哈特：我杀死了一个……是我下的命令，我记得。
Eberhard: That deserter ... I ordered Rudolph to pull the trigger. But I was the one who killed him.

保罗：还有一个活了下来，他被作为战俘送到了后方。
Paul: The other lives. Erich saw to that.

艾伯哈特：不，不止这一个……还有很多，他们本都可以活下来……
Eberhard: He wasn't the only one. So many have died, and I was the one that sent them to their deaths.

艾伯哈特垂着脑袋，盯着身下的一小块泥土。
Eberhard lowers his head, holding his gaze at a small patch of soil beneath him.

士官透过灰白的斗篷注视着蜷缩的艾伯哈特。
Charon watches him, adjusting his dark cloak.

艾伯哈特：我……想起一首诗，歌德还是席勒……？算了，学校学的东西早就忘光了。
Eberhard: Do you remember, Paul? There was a poem by Goethe, no, Schiller maybe? Ah, those days at school feel like a fairy tale now.

艾伯哈特：我只记得你和迪特里希在黑板前因为默写不出来而抓耳挠腮的样子，穆伦贝格先生气得像一只青蛙。
Eberhard: Mr. Mühlenberge asked you and Dieterich to write it out on the blackboard. You two didn't even know where to start. I remember I thought he was going to snap you both in two.

艾伯哈特：三个月之后，不知怎么，我们就到了前线。迪特里希在第一天就死了。
Eberhard: Just a few months later, we were here. Dieterich died that very first day.

艾伯哈特：……
Eberhard: ...

艾伯哈特：那天晚上我们一起哭，以为失去迪特里希会是我们今生所经历的最大的悲伤。
Eberhard: Do you remember how we cried that night? We thought it would be the saddest day of our lives.

艾伯哈特：…………
Eberhard: ...

艾伯哈特：眼泪很快就不再有了。
Eberhard: We ran out of tears before anything else.

艾伯哈特：………………
Eberhard: ...

艾伯哈特：我很冷，保罗。
Eberhard: I'm cold, Paul.

保罗：恐惧在你体内重新生长，你可以多花一些时间，等待这阵寒冷的感觉过去。
Paul: A fear long absent is growing inside you again. Hold on to it. You'll warm up.

艾伯哈特：……
Eberhard: ...

艾伯哈特咬紧牙关，将自己撑起来。
Eberhard clenches his teeth and braces himself.

艾伯哈特：……这就是你说的那片墓地？弗兰兹埋在这里？
Eberhard: This is the place you found, isn't it? Where Franz was buried.

保罗：没错。
Paul: He lies below us.

艾伯哈特：不光是他，这么多人……他们已经在我之前死去。为什么我还活着，保罗，为什么是我？
Eberhard: There are so many graves, but I'm still alive. Why, Paul, why am I not lying among them?

保罗：战场上的生存，大多只与运气有关。
Paul: The living speak of luck. The rest are silent.

侥幸存活的人对这个答案并不满意，他沉默了一会儿。
The answer doesn't satisfy, but the lone survivor cannot find a new question. After a long silence, he speaks again.

艾伯哈特：我是否能永远保持无知？不去尝试理解眼前发生的一切，就不会……我想这也不对……
Eberhard: I wish I could forget it all now. If I didn't know what happened, I wouldn't—No, no, it's, it's not right for me to ask that ...

艾伯哈特：可是，我现在既然活着，那我还能做些什么？
Eberhard: But I am still alive. Is there anything I can do for them?

保罗：我对生者的命运一无所知，你应该自己决定你要做的事，艾伯哈特。
Paul: That isn't a question for the dead. I can't tell you what to do, Eberhard.

艾伯哈特伸手摸向衣袋，那里空空如也。他只好无奈地闷哼一声。
Eberhard reaches into his coat pocket but finds it empty. He stifles a helpless grunt.

艾伯哈特：我记得你提起过重塑之手。
Eberhard: You mentioned Manus Vindictae.

保罗：是的。
Paul: You remember.

艾伯哈特：……
Eberhard: ...

艾伯哈特：你和基金会的人打过照面，你怎么看？他们真的能结束这场战争？
Eberhard: What about the Foundation? You talked to them too, right? Do you really think they can stop this war?

保罗：结束战争不是他们能独立完成的事，但我知道他们在努力尝试。
Paul: They pursue peace, but it cannot be found by their efforts alone.

他凝视着道路另一头新生的树林。蒙佩小镇与公墓通过一条穿越森林的小路相连。
He turns from the hill to the woods. Through the thicket and further lies the town of Montpaix.

艾伯哈特·布劳恩茫然闭上眼睛，凝思片刻。
Eberhard closes his eyes and waits for his thoughts to settle.

艾伯哈特：走吧，去蒙佩。
Eberhard: Come on. Let's go see Montpaix again.

艾伯哈特：……那是在后方休假的时候，在我准备去学校探望穆伦贝格先生之前，军营里来人把我叫了过去。
Eberhard: I was about to pay a visit to Mr. Mühlenberge when someone from Army Command said the colonel wanted to see me.

艾伯哈特：我被带到一间会议室，和我一起的还有很多军官。他们和我一样，即将晋升到新的职位。
Eberhard: I was taken to a meeting room with many other officers. I recognized them. I knew many had just been promoted like me.

艾伯哈特：希施费尔德上校——没错，就是那个被刺杀的谈判代表，作为总参谋部的代表向新晋军官讲话。
Eberhard: Colonel Hirschfelder showed up to give us a speech—yes, yes, the same colonel who was assassinated after the parley.

艾伯哈特：“民族和国家到了最令英雄们渴求的光荣时刻。”他这么说，“我们将为后代赢得未来一百年的繁荣。”
Eberhard: "The time has come when our nation calls for heroes," he said, "with our foremost goal to create a prosperous new world for our children."

艾伯哈特：“过去两年的一系列行动已经预示着我们本应取得最后的胜利，可士兵却在关键时刻丧失了斗志和勇气。”
Eberhard: "We have fought valiantly, and now the war turns in our favor. We stand but one step away from total victory, yet it is at this very moment that our soldiers have lost their courage."

艾伯哈特：“他们像卑微的流浪汉一样，在敌人的仓库中喝得酩酊大醉，白白延误了战机。”
Eberhard: "They waste their time looting every barn, cellar, and shed in search of treasure and drink to numb their fears, delaying our operations."

艾伯哈特：“这种贪生怕死和缺乏战斗意志的软弱性格是阻碍我军前进的疾病，但好在，我们已经找到了治愈它的方法。”
Eberhard: "Their greed and cowardice have spread through our army like a malignant tumor. Fortunately, we have found a cure."

艾伯哈特：“一个对胜利满怀信念的民间组织，向我们提供了非同凡响的技术……”
Eberhard: "An organization that believes in the promise of our victory has provided us with an extraordinary development ..."

艾伯哈特：后来的话我没听清楚。至于这种技术的细节，我也并不了解。似乎……它能让人在战场上无所畏惧。
Eberhard: That's all I remember. I don't have a mind for technology, but it just washed the fear off me.

艾伯哈特：在场的军官是他们第一批实验对象，我们开始为胜利欢呼、呐喊，就像还未见过战争的可怜的新兵……
Eberhard: Thinking about it now, we must have been like lab rats to them. As soon as they finished their ritual, we became so sure of our victory that we began yelling and singing as one. We were just fresh-faced boys again, thirsty for a war we'd forgotten.

录音暂停，嘶嘶杂音在宽敞的室内回荡，最终消失不见。
The hiss of static echoes through the spacious room, then fades.

刻雷乌斯：各位，先听到这里。做出口述的人是部署在蒙佩周边地区的一名少校营长。
Creius: I think that's enough for now. That was a recording from a German major we encountered in Montpaix.

刻雷乌斯：我会在之后提交详细报告，包括这份口供产生的缘由与完整录音。
Creius: I intend to submit a report with full details, including his entire statement and an explanation for our inquiries.

前线调查负责人保持安静，等待后方决策者的进一步指令。
The head of the frontline investigation quiets, awaiting further instructions from the decision makers at the rear.

Z：……重塑之手的进度比我们预料得要快很多。
Z: Manus Vindictae is moving quicker than any of us could've imagined.

佩德拉：可是……这不符合常理。
Pedra: But none of these makes sense.

佩德拉委员已从前线返回，经历刺杀事件之后，此刻他还有些惊魂未定。
Pedra has returned from the front, still shaken from the assassination attempt.

佩德拉：重塑之手和基金会一同来到这个时代，他们不可能在这么短的时间内就能渗透军方决策层。
Pedra: If they came to this era at the same time as we did, how could they have already infiltrated the military higher-ups in such a short time?

Z：如果这个时代的确受到了阿尔卡纳意志的影响，那这一切并非毫无可能。
Z: We've already theorized that Arcana may now possess the power to rewrite history.

Z：我们无法参照真实历史来确定，这个时代中重塑之手的势力有多大。
Z: Which means going forward. Any records from history as we once knew it will be unreliable for estimating their strength.

佩德拉：……
Pedra: ...

委员陷入凝重的沉默。
Pedra falls into heavy silence.

康斯坦丁：佩德拉，除了希施费尔德上校之外，与你有过交涉的其他国家军方人物对重塑之手有什么看法？
Constantine: Pedra, what were the other representatives' opinions concerning Manus Vindictae?

佩德拉：……他们没有人承认重塑之手的存在。
Pedra: They all denied its existence.

康斯坦丁：这么看，现状的危急程度不允许我们再延续之前的和谈策略。
Constantine: I see. It seems as though we're left with no other option but to change policies.

佩德拉：——我仍然拒绝采用过于激进的手段。
Pedra: No. We can't resort to such radical measures.

“鸽派”的代言人预先表达了立场。
The Doves' representative states his position in advance.

佩德拉：基金会在这个时代的积累不能因为眼下的问题而挥霍一空，和平到来后，我们还需要和政府合作。
Pedra: The Foundation risks alienating any potential allies if we act too aggressively now. This war will not be the end of our fight. We will need to rely on their cooperation in the future.

佩德拉：这一切都建立在对规则的信任之上。
Pedra: And that requires trust and a sense of security.

刻雷乌斯：……至于这点，我有一个新的情况要向各位汇报。
Creius: On the subject of governments, I have some news to report.

刻雷乌斯的声音再次出现在会议室中。
Creius's voice resurfaces in the conference hall.

刻雷乌斯：目前，有一位主张和谈的议会代表秘密造访蒙佩，想要获得与重塑之手有关的线索。
Creius: A man of the Inter-Factional Committee paid a secret visit to Montpaix, hoping to obtain intel about the Manus.

佩德拉：秘密造访？
Pedra: A secret visit?

同为政客的佩德拉委员，很快意识到议会代表此行的目的何在。
As a fellow politician, Pedra immediately grasps the true intent behind their visit.

佩德拉：议会是想借重塑之手的情报，让军队高层因无法受到信任而倒台？
Pedra: What did they say? Do they intend to use our intel against the heads of their Army Command?

刻雷乌斯：正是如此，如果亲基金会的主和派政府上台，和平谈判的进程会比现在更加顺利。
Creius: You've guessed it. If their government manages to rein in the army, it'll be much easier to reach a ceasefire.

佩德拉：这种做法会让基金会被指控为颠覆国家政权，刻雷乌斯，你根本没有考虑过这个问题，对吗？
Pedra: But if anyone were to find out, we might be accused of interfering in their internal affairs. Have you considered that, Creius?

刻雷乌斯：但基金会并没有通过任何正式的方式与议会代表产生过接触，这位代表是私下造访安全区的。
Creius: Officially, the Foundation never made any contact with their government. All I did was have a candid conversation with a man about my concerns for his people.

他强调了一个关键的细节。
He stresses one key detail.

刻雷乌斯：对议会来说，他们也没有理由声张自己在与基金会合谋。
Creius: At any rate, they haven't any reason to expose their cooperation with us.

佩德拉：……这种做法在现阶段有太多的不确定性。
Pedra: There are simply too many uncertainties to consider.

惯于制衡的政治家捕捉到派系争端的意味。
The politician, accustomed to checks and balances, catches the implication of a factional dispute.

康斯坦丁：让主和派上台结束战争符合真实的历史进程，这与“鸽派”维护历史的诉求并不矛盾。
Constantine: History will only be restored to its rightful track if the peaceful factions on each side can rise to power and stop this war. This has been our goal from the beginning.

康斯坦丁：在这个时代中，构建亲基金会的外部政治环境符合我们的基本利益，我想，绝大多数委员都不会反对这一点。
Constantine: It doesn't matter which era we end up in. We always benefit from a political climate that is friendly to the Foundation. That's undeniable.

康斯坦丁：你的看法呢，佩德拉？
Constantine: What do you think, Pedra?

佩德拉：……
Pedra: ...

委员摘下眼镜，揉搓着眼球。
He removes his glasses and rubs his eyes.

佩德拉：……我也许能劝说“鸽派”在联合委员会上支持这个决定——给交战国的主和派提供重塑之手在控制军队的证据。
Pedra: I might be able to persuade some of the other Committee members to support this proposal. If we're certain of this course of action, then we'll have to provide intel to those seeking peace in all governments involved.

康斯坦丁：很好，我不希望看见派系斗争影响我们实现共同的目标。
Constantine: Good. No faction should put their own goals above those of the Foundation's.

康斯坦丁：少校的口供不够充分，基金会会增派调查员去其他地区搜集证据。刻雷乌斯，前线还有继续调查的价值吗？
Constantine: We'll need more to verify that major's statement. Send investigators to search other regions and report everything they see. Creius, continue your investigation. Follow every possible lead.

刻雷乌斯：当然。请放心，我的人很快就会找到更为确凿的证据。
Creius: Understood. We'll dig up whatever they have buried.

11TH-09 交汇地 / Paths Crossed

夜幕降临，并非一切事物都会在夜晚安歇。
Night falls, and creatures stir.

“哨兵”：……
Sentinel: ...

不远处，还有另一道影子藏匿在林间。在夜色的掩映下，也许他会被当作一根枯瘦的树干。
Not far away, there is another shadow hiding in the forest. Under the cover of night, perhaps he would be taken for a withered tree trunk.

但石像鬼本就属于黑夜，他们很轻松地在晦暗的环境中辨认出彼此。
But Gargoyles belong to the night. They recognize one another with ease in the dimness.

？？？：一个被视为有罪的人死在你的枪口之下，他未经审判，也不曾获得忏悔的机会。
???: A man is proclaimed guilty, and for this he is condemned to death, denied even the justice of a trial. His execution came as a wind, silencing him ere he might utter a word of repentance.

？？？：扣下扳机的人，可以被称作是正义的吗？
???: And this thou wouldst call righteousness?

“哨兵”：别来烦我，拉蒂斯。
Sentinel: Leave me be, Ladislas.

她轻而易举地把沉重的提问扔在地上。
She shrugs the heavy question off.

拉蒂斯：难道你真的从来不思考自己的所作所为？以杀戮中止杀戮就是你的正义之路？
Ladislas: Hast thou reflected on thine actions? Meeting eye for eye and tooth for tooth. Is it justice or vengeance still?

“哨兵”：你问错了问题，我不在乎正义。你可以随意把任何罪责加在我身上。
Sentinel: Do you think so little of me? That I would call it "justice" even were it not so? Blame me then, cousin. Damn and condemn me. I care not.

拉蒂斯：我并非要加重你的负担，而是不想让你继续被引诱上堕落的道路——我在乎的是你的灵魂，堂亲。
Ladislas: Never would I damn thee, cousin. For it is thy soul for which I am most concerned. I fear it doth wither with every act of malice.

拉蒂斯：我们是流淌着恶魔之血的族裔，即使已经历经千余年的苦修，仍然无法彻底涤净血液中的污秽。
Ladislas: Hark and listen well. Dost thou forget the nature of our unholy ancestry? We art the kin of demons. A thousand years hence, and their malevolence yet floweth thickened in our veins, and their whispers pricketh still our ears in the silence.

“哨兵”：回答我一个问题，一万人的死亡和十万人的死亡相比，哪一个更好？
Sentinel: Then answer me this question, dear cousin. You stand before the scales of a balance. On one pan, the lives of ten men, and on the other, a hundred. If you had the power to shift its weight to save the many, would you?

拉蒂斯：这个问题太过亵渎——难道……你真的在听取它的声音？
Ladislas: A question that is heavy-laced with blasphemies. Hast thou already bent thine ear to the devils' lies?

“哨兵”：你必须二选其一，否则我们的谈话无法继续。
Sentinel: Answer me, cousin. Elsewise, there is nothing more that needs be said.

拉蒂斯眉头紧蹙，他低下头，以默祷来化解涌上鼻腔的哀苦。
Ladislas furrows his brow and lowers his head, lips motioning the words of a prayer.

“哨兵”：在战争之中，你会面对无数比这更加痛苦的选择，而你甚至不敢背负回答这个问题的负担。
Sentinel: Silence? Are you truly so naive? The scales are lain far heavier for those in the throes of war, yet you have not even the courage to answer a simple question. I'm afraid you have mistaken your weakness for virtue.

“哨兵”：回教堂去吧，拉蒂斯。你有更适合自己的工作。
Sentinel: Go back to the monastery, Ladislas. This is war, red in tooth and claw, and your heart proves too quick to kindle.

拉蒂斯哀叹着消失在夜色中，如同阴影融于黑夜。
Ladislas vanishes into the dark with a sigh, his form melting into the night.

石像鬼士兵靠上树干以寻求短暂的休憩。从四肢末端开始，石化如浪潮般覆满全身。
The Gargoyle soldier leans against a tree for a brief rest. In the crook of its branches, she begins to slowly turn to stone.

你又在和他吵架了。
You are again at odds, it seems.

耳中有轻柔的声音响起，而她身旁并无第二人。
A voice rings in her ears. It speaks without a source, coming from neither place nor person.

“哨兵”：他总是这样。
Sentinel: 'Twas not a battle I sought.

拉蒂斯的学识比我们要多，如同你的胆量比我们两个人加起来都要大。
Our cousin is more learned than either of we two, but he lacks in courage compared to thee—most daring of us all.

“哨兵”：我不否认。但这对于现状并无助益。
Sentinel: I do not deny his learnedness. But there are neither letters nor prose that might aid my mission.

……可我也害怕有一天悔恨会将你压倒，就像，我也害怕你会突然死去……
Thou burnest too short a wick, and the flames of perdition rise to meet thee. I fear for thee, Marie. That thou go forth to a battle that will consume thee, whether in defeat or in triumph.

马塞尔，安托万，还有拒绝入伍的伊冯娜……他们答应过我，但是再也没有出现过……
Massel, Anthoine, and Yvonne ... They once promised to return as thou didst. Yet they fell all the same, each after the last. Yvonne was taken before she had even tasted battle.

“哨兵”：如果我活下来，或许会有悔恨的那一天，但不能是现在。
Sentinel: Let remorse consume me if it must. But God willing, I will see the end of this war first. Ere then, the fear of regret will not stay me.

“哨兵”：……绝不能是现在。
Sentinel: Not now.

“哨兵”：也许是在和平最终降临的那一天，到那时……你会回来吧？
Sentinel: And perhaps, on that day when peace finally comes, you will return to us?

声音在凌乱的风中消散了，她知道，这个夜晚它将不会再出现。
The voice vanishes in the night's breeze. She would not hear it again this night.

“哨兵”：……
Sentinel: ...

休憩宣告结束。士兵拾起武器，向线索指引的下一个目的地走去。
She shakes off the scales of stone and resumes the march toward her next lead.

帕拉维扬将一张周边地区的地图平铺在桌面上。
Paravyan lays out a local strategic map over the table.

刻雷乌斯拿起数枚子弹，将第一颗放在地图上标记为蒙佩的点，随后将剩余的子弹攥在手心里。
Creius picks up a handful of bullets, placing the first on Montpaix.

刻雷乌斯：艾伯哈特后续回忆起了一些与重塑之手有关的地点，但信息很模糊，我们应该尽快开展实地调查。
Creius: Major Braun was able to recall some of the locations that may have been used by the Manus. His coordinates aren't what anyone would call precise, so we'd best start searching ASAP.

刻雷乌斯：切斯特，你去检查这片林区，卡斯帕会在目标地点外围接应你。
Creius: Chester, you'll take the forest. Caspa will be expecting you on the edge.

一颗子弹被立在一片被描绘为森林的地点。
One bullet stands upright on a spot marked as forest.

调查员Ⅰ：我这就去找他。
Investigator I: On it.

刻雷乌斯：卡米拉，李，河道沿线交给你们。
Creius: Camila, Lee, you'll search from here and move along the river.

调查员Ⅱ：我们很快就回。
Investigator II: Will get it done, sir.

每下达一道指令，就有一颗新的子弹被立在桌面上。
Each new order is marked by another round placed upright on the table.

刻雷乌斯：查尔斯，阿曼达，你们两个一起去侦查299高地，这需要经过无人区。提前向前线军队表明身份，避开火力。
Creius: Charles, Amanda, you're on Hill 299. You'll need to cross no man's land to get there. Make sure you establish your identity with both sides in advance to avoid friendly fire.

调查员们：了解。
Investigators: Understood.

……
...

原本拥挤的房间内，人员逐渐走空。桌面上只剩下最后一颗弹壳。
The crowded room empties order by order, bullet by bullet, until only the last round remains.

刻雷乌斯：帕拉维扬。
Creius: Paravyan.

“警官”：在。
"Officer": Yes, sir.

刻雷乌斯：农庄交给你。另外，把玛尔纱带上，她精通战斗和急救，你们可以互相掩护。
Creius: I want you on this village. Take Marsha with you. She's a skilled combatant as well as a medic. You can count on each other.

“警官”：明白。
"Officer": Yes, sir.

帕拉维扬离开了房间，但此刻还有最后一个没有被分配任何任务的人。
Paravyan exits, leaving one person remaining without orders.

年轻士兵睁大眼与长官对视，努力掩饰内心的庆幸与雀跃。
The young soldier locks eyes with her superior, an unspoken relief written on her face.

梅蕾尔：……也就是说，我留在蒙佩待命就好了，对吗？
Merel: So, does that mean I'll remain on standby in Montpaix?

刻雷乌斯：如果有重塑之手乘隙进攻蒙佩，你要负责守卫。
Creius: Yes. I need someone coordinating the defense of this town should the Manus attack.

梅蕾尔：啊……啊？
Merel: Oh. Uhm ...

年轻士兵垂下头颅，难过之情溢于言表。
Relief turns into dread.

“警官”：就是这里了？
"Officer": Is this it?

玛尔纱：应该没错，下车吧。
Marsha: I believe so. Let's get on with it.

村庄被一片繁茂的原野环绕。战争爆发前，这里的居民应该过着富庶而安宁的生活。
The village around them still carries the signs of lush wilderness and gentle fields. A place of abundance and safety, once.

“警官”：我走前面。
"Officer": Watch my six.

二人取出武器，从侧面进入村庄。
The two draw weapons and enter from the side.

调查者们没有遭到任何阻拦，如果不是得到了情报的指示，他们只会把这里当成一座孤零零的废墟。
The investigators are not stopped in any way, and if they hadn't been instructed to do so, they would have just treated this place as another forgotten remnant of better days.

玛尔纱：一个人也没有……真是一场灾难。
Marsha: This place is empty. It's heartbreaking to see it so quiet.

“警官”：时间还早，可以逐一检查一下房屋。
"Officer": We're ahead of schedule. Let's start by checking the houses one by one.

玛尔纱：没问题。
Marsha: Good.

玛尔纱：……找到什么了吗？
Marsha: Find anything?

“警官”：没有，我在一个房间里发现了一些写着字的纸张，但应该只是当地人没有寄出去的信件。
"Officer": Only some letters I can't read. I guess they didn't have time to post them before they left.

玛尔纱：我在一间地下室找到了一些枪械，不过是早就生锈的猎枪，火药也已经受潮。
Marsha: There were some small arms in the basement, all of them older models and rusty. The ammo was damp.

玛尔纱神情凝重地盯着一座空空如也的仓库。
Marsha holds her gaze on an empty warehouse.

玛尔纱：这里已经被废弃了很久，而且经历过掠夺。村子里的东西基本没有价值，或者不太好搬走。
Marsha: This place had to have been looted more than a few times. The only valuables left are the ones too heavy to move.

“警官”：那对重塑之手来说，这里有什么价值呢？
"Officer": So, basically, there's nothing here. What do the Manus want it for?

玛尔纱沮丧地摇摇头。
She shakes her head in frustration.

玛尔纱：我没有完整接受过调查员的训练，基金会很快就把我派到蒙佩来了。
Marsha: I was rushed through the investigator training before being sent to Montpaix.

玛尔纱：也许我会漏掉一些细节。
Marsha: It's possible I missed something.

青年想要给予宽慰，展露的笑容却显得有些生涩。
The young man tries to console her, but his smile is stiff.

“警官”：这一切都会逐渐熟练起来的，刻雷乌斯长官对我说，实战才是最好的训练。
"Officer": Don't worry. You're doing fine. Mr. Creius always says training is no match for experience.

“警官”：或许，这就像“乌鸫”——也就是梅蕾尔，你在蒙佩见过她的。
"Officer": Blackbird is a prime example, I mean Merel. You met her back in Montpaix.

“警官”：虽然她也接受过训练，但始终没能适应战争。其实我知道，她连在南极的时候都一直担惊受怕的。
"Officer": She's been through all the training the Foundation could throw at her, but she still isn't ready for the battlefield. I probably shouldn't say, but she nearly went mental during the Antarctic operation.

玛尔纱：战场的确十分残酷……三个星期的普通军事训练，是无法让人成为一名真正的士兵的。
Marsha: The battlefield is crueler than ordinary people can imagine. A few weeks of military training just isn't enough.

帕拉维扬顺着话题，试探性地提出了一个自己关心了很久的问题。
Paravyan follows the topic and broaches a question he's long been holding back.

“警官”：我听说……骑士团有一套独特的传统神秘术训练方法？
"Officer": So, what's your deal? I know you came from some Order with special arcane training.

“警官”：恐惧、痛苦，甚至是同理心，都能通过某种方法“冻结”起来，直到战斗结束之后再释放。
"Officer": You can "freeze" your fear and pain—emotional stuff—during battle until you feel safe?

“警官”：——这么说对吗？
"Officer": I only skimmed through the briefing. Is that right?

玛尔纱：差不太远了。但我想，现在不太适合谈这些。
Marsha: It's more complicated than that. But I'm not sure I'd like to get into it now.

“警官”：抱歉——我明白了。
"Officer": Yeah, sure. Sorry.

玛尔纱：不，没事……我们还漏掉了哪些地方吗？
Marsha: No need to apologize. Just ... do you think we missed anything?

“警官”：——让我想想……
"Officer": Well, let's take a minute.

“警官”：他们藏起来的东西会是什么呢？——枪械、化学武器、作战计划，还是某些不属于这个时代的装备？
"Officer": What could they even possibly hide here? Arms, chemical weapons, secret files, or gear smuggled back from the future?

玛尔纱：我对重塑之手的了解不太多，也不清楚你们所说的其他时代……
Marsha: I don't know much about Manus Vindictae or the future.

刺耳的爆裂声在耳畔炸响，一颗飞溅的石子在她的盔甲上敲出尖锐的声音。
There's a sudden ear-splitting pop, followed by a thundering explosion as rocks spatter across her armor.

玛尔纱：帕拉维扬——！
Marsha: Incoming!

“警官”：——装甲车，村庄西北面，200米！找掩护！
"Officer": Armored vehicle, 200 meters northwest of the village! Take cover!

11TH-10 不洁之路 / Devil's Work

装甲车的残骸中喷涌出浓烈刺鼻的烟雾。
Thick, acrid smoke billows from the wreckage of the armored vehicle.

玛尔纱：——咳咳。
Marsha: *cough*

玛尔纱从一堆碎石中撑起身子，肩头出现了轻微的撕裂感。
Marsha braces herself on a pile of debris, all at once letting herself feel the sharp tearing pain in her shoulder.

玛尔纱：结束了……似乎是谁帮了我们……
Marsha: It's over. Someone helped us.

玛尔纱：帕……帕拉维扬，你还好吗？
Marsha: Pa ... Paravyan, are you alright?

她望向道路另一头，不远处，青年被压在一块沉重的屋梁之下。
She looks across the road. Just ahead, the young man is pinned under a heavy beam.

“警官”：不要乱动，玛尔纱——你的伤口还在流血。
"Officer": Stay put, Marsha. You're bleeding.

“警官”：我马上——马上就能出来。
"Officer": I can ... I can get myself out.

帕拉维扬费尽全身力气，也无法让粗大的木料移动半分。
Paravyan strains with all his strength but can't move the timber an inch.

玛尔纱：敌方……已无威胁，我可以来……帮你。
Marsha: We're all clear. Let me help you.

“警官”：没关系，我只是被压住了。你先别动——你的头和肩膀还在流血！
"Officer": Don't fuss over me. It's just a bit of wood. You need to stay put. Your head and shoulder are bleeding!

玛尔纱：嗯？我……受伤了吗？
Marsha: What? Am I hurt?

玛尔纱摇摇晃晃地站起身来。
Marsha staggers to her feet.

玛尔纱：唉，有些头晕，不会吧——
Marsha: Ugh, I'm feeling faint.

她伸手摸向自己的头顶。
She reaches for the top of her head.

玛尔纱：噢……果然，我在……我在流血——糟了，应该留下一点疼痛感……
Marsha: It seems you're right. I'm bleeding profusely from several wounds. That's what I get for suppressing all my pain.

玛尔纱：也许是一个……弹……弹片——没有关系，很快就能恢复……
Marsha: Ah so, just a little shrapnel. Nothing too serious.

“警官”：先为自己止血，玛尔纱。
"Officer": Treat your wounds first, Marsha.

玛尔纱：……好。
Marsha: Understood.

受伤的骑士坐在一块倒塌的墙砖上，低垂着眼，看向自己脚尖的那一小块地方。
She leans back on a pile of fallen bricks, her head swaying until it slumps.

玛尔纱：……我休息一会就好了。
Marsha: I'll be alright. I just need a little rest.

……
...

玛尔纱：……？
Marsha: ...?

她看见一双靴子。
Her gaze lifts up to a pair of boots.

接着，是一柄硕大的反坦克步枪。
Then, the sizeable barrel of an anti-tank rifle.

玛尔纱：这是——
Marsha: Who ...

她抬起头。
She looks up.

“哨兵”：……
Sentinel: ...

玛尔纱：……是你…………
Marsha: You again ...

她挣扎着想要站起来。
She struggles to her feet.

“哨兵”：坐好。
Sentinel: Sit.

玛尔纱：哦……
Marsha: Um ...

她跌落回去，仰着头，表情有些呆滞。
Her legs buckle, leaving her braced up against the debris.

玛尔纱：是你……救了我们，谢谢。
Marsha: You saved us. Thank you.

“哨兵”：为什么在这里。
Sentinel: What brought you here?

玛尔纱：重塑之手……我们在寻找踪迹……
Marsha: Collecting intel on Manus Vindictae.

“哨兵”：你知道自己会面对什么危险吗？
Sentinel: Have you no reckoning on the danger in this place?

玛尔纱：……
Marsha: ...

她摇晃着脑袋。
Marsha shakes her head.

“哨兵”：疯了。
简直就是来送死。
Sentinel: Idiot. You might well have breathed your last in that battle.

？？？：别缠着我！
???: Let go!

“哨兵”：——？
Sentinel: ...?

玛尔纱：还有人？
Marsha: Who's out there?

“哨兵”转过身，在装甲车留下的浓烟后看见一道黑影。
Sentinel turns, spotting a figure emerging from the armored vehicle's smoking shell.

？？？：放开——放开！你会害死我的！
???: Let me go! You're gonna get me killed!

在他脚边，躺着一名和他穿着相同制服的伤员。
At his feet lies a wounded soldier in the same black uniform.

伤员：不——施特林……求求你——
Wounded Soldier: No! Sterling ... Please ...

伤员：——！
Wounded Soldier: ...!

伤员被杀死在原地，不再哀嚎。施特林抬起满是血丝的眼睛，与摧毁了坦克的狙击手对上目光。
The wounded man's cries are cut short. Sterling turns two manic bloodshot eyes toward the advancing sniper.

施特林：该死的！
Sterling: F**k!

“哨兵”：……
Sentinel: ...

一颗子弹击中石像鬼的腹部。中弹者身躯轻颤，弹着点崩出一缕伴着碎石的烟尘，却没有流出鲜血。
A bullet strikes the Gargoyle clean through her abdomen, but it draws no blood. Instead, chips of stony debris fall out from the wound.

施特林：妈的——他妈的，怪物！
Sterling: What the hell? You goddamn monster!

施特林转过身，向着村庄外亡命奔逃。
The man's eyes go wider still as he turns to flee.

“哨兵”：呵。
Sentinel: Heh.

“哨兵”没有急于追逐，她先是走向帕拉维扬，掀开压住他的屋梁。
She does not give chase. She walks to Paravyan and lifts the beam from his body.

“警官”：咳……咳咳——
"Officer": *cough*

“警官”：……谢谢你，请问我该怎么……称呼？
"Officer": Thanks. Who are you? Are you with the Foundation?

青年抬起头，看见浓重的阴云在女人的眉间凑集。
The young man finds his answer in her grim and stony face.

“哨兵”：你留下来，替玛尔纱止血。
Sentinel: Stay here and tend to your comrade.

“哨兵”：我去解决重塑之手。
Sentinel: I will tend to our enemies.

施特林：呼……呼！
Sterling: *panting*

欧根：只有我们逃——逃出来了吗？科尔腾呢，你没有把他带出来？
Eugen: Are we the only ones left? Where's Kolten?

施特林：别管他！他死了！
Sterling: Dead! Now get the lead out and run!

施特林：她出现了，她来了——朝她开枪！欧根！
Sterling: She's coming at us! She's coming! Shoot her, Eugen, shoot her!

欧根：我——我看不见她——我们到底在往哪里跑？！
Eugen: I ... I can't see her. Where are we running?

施特林：前面有座风车，我们躲进去截住她——别停下，蠢猪！
Sterling: Look, there's an old mill ahead! We'll regroup there to intercept her—keep running, you idiot!

欧根：我看见她了，看见她了——
Eugen: I see her now. She's there.

欧根：去……去死！
Eugen: Die!

欧根：呃——！
Eugen: Ugh!

施特林：白痴……白痴！
Sterling: You idiot!

施特林：啊……啊啊——！我的手——
Sterling: Ugh. Ahhhh! My hand!

逃亡者距离风车的掩护只有数步之遥。
An old windmill lies just ahead—refuge, in his panicked mind.

施特林：……呃——嗬……嗬……
Sterling: Urgh ... Huff ...

“哨兵”：你无路可走了。
Sentinel: For the wicked flee, and I pursueth.

施特林：——！
Sterling: ...!

子弹射向她的肩膀，再次无力地弹开。
Another bullet strikes her shoulder and glances off in another spray of stone.

施特林：为什么，杀不死你——你这个……怪物、恶魔……
Sterling: Why won't you die? You devil!

“哨兵”：我？
Sentinel: A devil, you call me?

“哨兵”：那你又是什么？
Sentinel: What are you, then?

难道他们不是我们的兄弟、姐妹吗？
What hast thou done? The voice of thy brother's blood crieth unto me from the ground.

“哨兵”：图谋奸恶，播散纷争——你又是什么呢？
Sentinel: You who discord between nations and plot schemes for the undoing of man. Who then is your master?

她逼近一步。
She steps closer.

“哨兵”：也许我们没有多大区别。所以，我会给你忏悔的机会。
Sentinel: For if you do the devil's work, are you not a devil like me? I pity you. Repent and you may yet find mercy in the judgment of the Lord.

土地从我们的手中接受亲族的血。
And now art thou cursed from the earth,

施特林：退、退后——！
Sterling: What the hell do you want? Back off!

“哨兵”：……我不是为了杀戮而来。施特林是你的名字，对吗？
Sentinel: Sterling, isn't it? You need not fear me. You still have time.

施特林：啊啊啊——！
Sterling: Ahhhhh!

从现在起，你要受到永远的诅咒。
Which hath opened her mouth to receive thy brother's blood from thy hand.

“哨兵”：可你必须要先忏悔……告诉我……
Sentinel: Repent, and you may yet be saved. Speak.

施特林：你在说什么——你想干什么？！
Sterling: What are you talking about? What do you want from me?

土地不再为我们效力。
When thou tillest the ground, it shall not henceforth yield unto thee her strength.

“哨兵”：咳……
Sentinel: *coughing*

施特林：……
Sterling: ...

终于，追随重塑之手的士兵绝望地跪倒在地。
The soldier tumbles to the ground; as he scrambles, he launches into a desperate prayer.

“哨兵”：告诉我……重塑之手究竟为何想要世界陷入——战火。
Sentinel: Answer me. For what purpose does Manus Vindictae drive the world to war and ruin?

施特林：复苏之母，引导之人……
Sterling: Mother of Resurrection, the Guiding One ...

“哨兵”：……？
Sentinel: ...?

怪异的名讳。
The prayer follows a pattern she knows by heart, yet the name he speaks is strange.

施特林：……请求您垂怜卑微的仆从，我向您祈求奇迹，赐我永恒的生命——
Sterling: Please have mercy on your humble servant. I pray for a miracle—a ladder into your eternal kingdom.

施特林：我将绝望的生命……献与您……永恒的国度，美好的时代——
Sterling: I hereby offer my life to you. Please save me from desperation and take me to the golden era.

我们终身操劳，终生流离飘荡在世上……
A fugitive and a vagabond shalt thou be in the earth.

他将最后一颗子弹留给了自己。
He saves the last bullet for himself.

“哨兵”：——！
Sentinel: ...!

...

Sentinel: ...

“哨兵”：无可救药的……

玛尔纱：——哨兵！
Marsha: Ms. Sentinel!

11TH-11 血污与伤痕 / Wounds and Scars

上尉：上刺刀！
Captain: Fix bayonets!

上尉：为了胜利！
Captain: For Victory!

上尉：跑起来——冲锋！
Captain: Charge!

上尉：他妈的，骑士团杀回来了。
Captain: Damn! Their cavalry's returned!

上尉：守住战壕——不准后退！我会亲自枪毙逃兵。
Captain: Hold the line! I'll shoot any coward that runs!

上尉：你是圣路连的神秘学家？那就快去，干掉那怪物！
Captain: You, you're from the Arcane Support Company? Go get that monster!

骑士团士兵：——
Knight: ...

她不记得自己是怎么做到的——也许是反扑的敌军也太过劳累，也许是受到上天的眷顾。
She can't remember how she did it—perhaps her enemies were as exhausted as she was, or perhaps it was just the devil's luck.

圣路连士兵：呃——
Arcane Support Soldier: Ugh!

在几乎是出自本能的搏斗之后，她终于将身披沉重甲胄的敌人抵在身下。
Struggling, fighting purely by instinct, she holds her heavily armored foe at bay.

骑士团士兵：……咳。
Knight: *cough*

……战斗僵持在最后一刻，只差最后一厘米的距离。抵抗者紧紧扣住刺刀的双手没有护具保护，此刻血流不止。
Time crawls to a standstill; her bayonet is stopped mere centimeters from her foe's throat by two armored fists.

……你还记得，在很小的时候，我们为争夺一棵野外的苹果树而吵了起来。
Dost thou recall when once, in our youth, we fought over an apple tree?

圣路连士兵：松手，该死的！
Arcane Support Soldier: Let go of me!

骑士团士兵：不——
Knight: No, damn it!

你想砍下一些枝条，尝尝用果木烤出来的鸡肉是什么味道。
Thou wished to cut its wood and make us a fire to roast a chicken.

骑士团士兵：呃……
Knight: Umm ...

而我隐隐觉得它是一棵该结果的树，第二年一定会有许多味道奇特的野苹果。
But I rebuked thee. For I believed the tree would bear fruit, and it would be the sweeter bounty of the two.

圣路连士兵：嗬……嗬……
Arcane Support Soldier: *panting*

你钻进浆果丛，朝我扔出几颗树莓。你说要保卫你的烤鸡，而我也捡起你扔过来的果子当作武器。
Thou didst find a bush with over-ripened berries and hurled them at me, crying that they should serve as my supper, while the chicken would be for thee alone. And I retaliated in kind.

圣路连士兵：可是……！
Arcane Support Soldier: But ...!

最后，我们浑身都是紫色与红色的浆果汁。
Ere long, we were painted red with juice.

骑士团士兵：嘶——
Knight: Ah!

你说，这真是一场血战，然后放下了手中最后的果子，举手投降……过去总是有这样快乐的日子。
"What a bloody melee we fight!" We laughed as we laid down our arms. What fun we had that day.

圣路连士兵：不——我……不想——
Arcane Support Soldier: No. I don't want to ...

但人为了争夺什么，才必须要把另一个人杀死……那也许是比苹果树更重要的东西，可是……
But the battle thou fightest now shall not end in the gentle smears of red berries. What drives humanity to war? Could it be so different from what drove us to it beneath that apple tree?

骑士团士兵：……
Knight: ...

我无法想象战争是什么样子，无法想象两百万人抱着杀死对方的心冲向彼此。
I dare not imagine how a slaughter that has claimed the lives of millions could be waged for so small a cause.

……我们是否真的能凭借仇恨，就将素不相识的人置于死地？
That we should be brought to bloodshed, driven only by the fear of those whom we were taught to despise.

可说到底，这场战争，究竟是为了争夺什么？
What immortal hand or eye could frame the cause behind these deadly ends?

你比我更勇敢，玛丽，永远知道自己在做什么，从不心生疑虑。那么，你能不能告诉我……
Thou art more courageous than I, Marie. Never hast thou doubted thy conviction. So tell me, I pray ...

如果命运皆有其意义……
Is there some purpose in the war they now fight?

那一个人杀死另一个人的意义究竟是什么？
For I see no divine meaning to be found in this killing and dying.

“哨兵”：……
Sentinel: ...

伤口的疼痛还在延续——幸运的是，小口径的手枪弹不至于给岩石化的身体留下致命伤口。
Small-caliber rounds pose no real threat to her rocky exterior, but that does little to reduce the pain.

但距离枪伤完全愈合，仍然需要不少时间。
And healing comes slowly.

“哨兵”：——艾格尼丝？
Sentinel: Agnès?

没有得到回应，但她已经习惯了。她站起来，才发现自己并非孤身一人。
No response. That was expected. But what she had not expected was the next voice.

玛尔纱：你在叫谁？
Marsha: Who's Agnès?

“哨兵”：……别在意。你在这里做什么？
Sentinel: She ... Matters not. But what brings you here?

玛尔纱：我得把你带到安全的地方。帕拉维扬——就是和我一起来的那个年轻人，留在村庄里搜查线索。
Marsha: I'm taking you somewhere safe. Paravyan—that young man who came with me—is back at the village. He'll continue with our search.

玛尔纱：至于我……和你一样，没那么容易死。
Marsha: Before you ask, I'm doing fine. Like you, I'm made of sterner stuff.

骑士活动了一下手臂，从她的动作来看，确实并无大碍。
She rotates her arm, looking as if her wounds had all but disappeared.

玛尔纱：我粗略检查了一下你的伤口，可我不太明白怎么处理……石像鬼的伤口，那里都是一些碎石块。
Marsha: I checked over your wounds, but I have no earthly idea what to do with this gravel. I know how to treat flesh, not stone.

玛尔纱：这对你来说应该不是太严重的问题，对吧？
Marsha: But that wound won't be a problem for you, will it?

“哨兵”：对……呃——
Sentinel: No. Ugh ...

即使肉体的疼痛可以忍受，惨烈梦境带来的精神痛苦仍然会令她忍不住皱眉。
Her physical pain is bearable. But the lingering echoes of her nightmare cause her to grit her teeth.

玛尔纱：很糟糕的梦？
Marsha: Were you dreaming? It seemed like a nightmare.

“哨兵”：……
Sentinel: ...

仍然受噩梦困扰的人双眼直直地看向前方。战地医生对这种精神上的苦楚无能为力。
She locks her stare forward and away. There's field dressing for the wounds that truly pain her.

玛尔纱：我不知道这样能不能让你好过一些……
Marsha: I don't know if this will help.

她干脆利落地脱下手套，将双手摊开在胸前。
She removes her gloves. It's a brisk and almost tender motion,

一道刺目的刀痕横贯掌心。
revealing deep slashing cuts across her palms.

“哨兵”：——！
Sentinel: ...!

“哨兵”：不，难道……真的是你——
Sentinel: Could it be ... Are you ...

玛尔纱：……是的，我们之间的战争已经结束了，你我不再是敌人。
Marsha: I am. But that battle is long over. You and I are no longer enemies.

殊死相搏的叫喊声汇聚成一阵嗡鸣。
The howls of their deadly melee still ring in her ears.

“哨兵”：玛尔纱……那是一场——毫无意义的自相残杀……
Sentinel: It was a senseless fight. I hurt you.

玛尔纱：这不是我们任何人的错。
Marsha: It wasn't your fault.

玛尔纱：其实，正因为有那场战斗，我才能被认定为阵亡——后来我想办法活了下来。
Marsha: In fact, I thank you for it. They thought I died fighting you—I used that as my opportunity to leave.

玛尔纱：我加入了一支民间组建的无国界救援队，之后，是一场重塑之手的袭击……最后，我被一支基金会小队救下。
Marsha: For some time after that, I was with an international rescue team. We came under attack by the Manus for our efforts, but the Foundation intervened.

“哨兵”：……你记得我？
Sentinel: Wait, then you remember me?

玛尔纱平静地点头，有如在病床前安抚伤员，一切并无大碍。
Marsha nods, a gentle, graceful motion, carrying the reassurance of a doctor at her patient's bedside.

玛尔纱：毕竟你不像我一样把整张脸都遮住了呀。
Marsha: And you didn't. I was wearing a helmet. But you don't have a face one forgets.

“哨兵”：……
Sentinel: ...

玛丽安娜：……玛丽安娜。
Sentinel: Marianne.

玛尔纱：嗯？
Marsha: Hm?

玛尔纱：……哦，我明白了。
Marsha: Oh, that's your name?

玛尔纱：玛丽安……安娜。
Marsha: Marianne. It's lovely.

她带着蹩脚的口音，重复着这个名字。
She repeats it, stressing the syllables as if to remember it.

玛丽安娜：基金会对重塑之手了解多少？
Sentinel: Tell me, then, what do you know about Manus Vindictae?

玛尔纱：他们是一支由纯血神秘学家组成的秘密团体，企图摧毁人类和神秘学家共同组成的社会。
Marsha: They are a secret organization open to only pure-blooded arcanists. Simply put, their goal is to cause as much chaos as possible and eventually destroy all of human society.

玛丽安娜：……复苏之母是他们敬奉的神灵吗？
Sentinel: And this "Mother of Resurrection" is like a god to them?

玛尔纱：没错，这个名字是阿尔卡纳的称谓之一。祂曾被杀死过一次，却通过某种仪式再次复活。
Marsha: Something like that, yes. She died once, but they managed to resurrect her through some awful ritual.

玛丽安娜：——复活？
Sentinel: A resurrected madwoman?

她的不屑演化为憎恶。她五指紧握，仿佛在空气中抓住了什么东西。
Her disdain curdles into hatred. Fingers clench, like she's trying to crush something in midair.

玛丽安娜：……可耻的模仿者。
Sentinel: Then she is a false prophet, an imposter of the true resurrection.

玛尔纱抓住机会，向她凑得更近一些。
Marsha seizes the opportunity to move to her side.

玛尔纱：基金会和重塑之手之间已经经历了相当漫长的战争——可能比这场大战本身还要久。
Marsha: The war between the Foundation and Manus Vindictae has lasted ages—longer, even, than this war.

玛尔纱：你和我们有一样的目标，而且此时此刻，你掌握的情报会给基金会带来巨大的帮助。
Marsha: You and the Foundation share the same goals, and the intelligence you gathered may prove crucial for us.

玛尔纱：如果你愿意共享关于重塑之手的情报，基金会也许能在一周之内促成停火，请你认真考虑这个可能性。
Marsha: If you would be willing to share it, we may be able to reach a truce sooner. So, please mull it over.

石像鬼低下头，相当粗略地对手中的步枪做了一番检查。
Sentinel bows her head, giving her rifle a rough once-over.

她擦去一些溅入枪机结构中的血液和泥土，随后向弹仓中塞入几颗新的子弹。
She wipes away some of the blood and dirt that cakes the receiver, then one by one slots new rounds into its magazine.

玛丽安娜：……1918年，我开始追查重塑之手的线索。人员、物品、信件……前线散落着各式各样的信息。
Sentinel: My search into Manus Vindictae began at the turn of 1918. Their documents, personal belongings, letters ... I sought and scrounged for every clue that might be found.

玛丽安娜：我得知他们不加区分地为交战双方提供援助，出于我不理解的目的，用尽一切手段延续这场战争。
Sentinel: From these, I learned of their mission to prolong this bloodshed, supplying both sides with arms of dreadful artifice. Then as now, I still do not understand why.

玛丽安娜：最初，我以为政府会重视重塑之手的阴谋，可无论是匿名举报信还是公开抗议，最终都毫无作用。
Sentinel: I brought my evidence before the powers of my nation, but they cared not. So, I spoke out against them, still hoping they might awaken to this madness.

玛丽安娜：所有信件和出版物都会遭受严格审查，任何谈论和平与重塑之手的信息都不允许出现。
Sentinel: But my words went unheeded. Worse, they turned against me, hiding even the very name of Manus Vindicate from all their publications and letters.

玛丽安娜：这是战争的第六年，报纸上唯一会出现的内容，就是鼓动开战时还只有十二岁的孩子上前线。
Sentinel: There is no longer any truth in the words they print; only lies meant to stir the pride of youth to deadly, pointless slaughter ... youths who were but children when the war began.

玛丽安娜：……我唯一能做的只有尽可能地消灭这些战争的煽动者。
Sentinel: That is why I have turned to this—to killing the ones who incited this war. It was the only choice I had left.

玛丽安娜：当我经历我所说的这一切的时候，基金会又在哪里？
Sentinel: Perhaps it has all been for naught, but at least I have put deeds to words. What has the Foundation done?

面对这番控诉，基金会职员顿时陷入手足无措的境地。
The accusation forces her into a stammering defense.

玛尔纱：根、根据规定，我没有权限向基金会之外的人告知……某些信息。
Marsha: We have done more than you know. But I'm not authorized to tell you.

玛丽安娜：基金会不信任我，却让我无偿提供所有的情报。
Sentinel: You expect me to offer all I know to you, yet still withhold your trust.

玛尔纱：我确实没有想过这一点，对不起。如果你想要一场交易，我会……
Marsha: I'm sorry. No, I suppose that isn't fair of us. If there is anything we can offer in exchange to make a deal, I'll ...

辩驳的言语逐渐失去了力量。
But her efforts lose steam.

玛尔纱：……我会尽可能为你申请足够好的条件，但我不确定……
Marsha: I'll try my best to honor it. But I can't guarantee anything.

她安静下来，即将入冬的冷风在二人之间吹过。
A cold breeze cuts the stillness between them.

玛丽安娜缓慢地叹出一口气。
Sentinel lets out a slow and labored breath.

玛丽安娜：我不会和基金会合作，这不是一场交易。
Sentinel: I will give nothing to the Foundation, neither freely nor for any bargain.

玛尔纱：……
Marsha: ...

玛丽安娜：但是，我可以为你个人提供帮助。
Sentinel: But you, Marsha—you have my trust.

玛尔纱：——！
Marsha: ...!

骑士难掩内心的欣喜。
Marsha lights up at her patient's declaration.

玛丽安娜：——走吧，跟我来。
Sentinel: Follow me.

玛尔纱：好、好的！
Marsha: Oh. Of course!

11TH-12 破碎的尖拱 / A Fractured Sanctuary

佩德拉：装甲车？
Pedra: An armored vehicle?

刻雷乌斯：是。驾驶员是重塑之手的人，他们从军队里窃取了装备和资源。
Creius: The driver was a Manus. They're not just supplying the war anymore.

通讯另一头沉吟片刻，接着，属于“鹰派”党魁的声音从听筒中传出。
There's a pause before the Hawks' leader speaks through the receiver.

伊里内伊：——刻雷乌斯，你有什么猜想？
Irinei: What do you think that means, Creius?

显然，各派委员们正身处一室，共同听取前线的汇报。
Both sides are gathered in the same room, listening to the reports from the front lines.

刻雷乌斯无声地发出轻笑，语调却仍然保持着严肃。
Creius lets out a soft, rueful chuckle, though he does not let it betray the seriousness of his words.

刻雷乌斯：重塑之手也许组建了一支属于自己的军队。
Creius: That the Manus have decided to build themselves an army.

伊里内伊：我持相同看法。
Irinei: That seems likely.

伊里内伊：我们要为这种情况早做打算。芝诺主力目前仍在东边，如果西线有变，他们短时间内无法增员。
Irinei: In that case, we must prepare immediately for a response. Zeno's main force is still at the eastern front. They won't be able to reinforce us if anything happens here.

伊里内伊：基金会应当在西线招募一支属于自己的军队。
Irinei: The Foundation will need an army of its own.

佩德拉：这不可能。
Pedra: That's completely irresponsible.

稳重的声音打断了过于夸张的猜想。
A calm voice cuts through the speculation.

佩德拉：——扩充军队会向外投射紧张情绪，不符合我们的和平政策。
Pedra: It will only increase the tension on this front, and it directly violates our peace policy.

佩德拉：而且，重塑之手只接受纯血神秘学家，他们不可能真正拥有一支足以形成战斗力的军队。
Pedra: Manus Vindictae takes in only pure-blooded arcanists. That doesn't make for a large recruitment pool. It won't be much of an army, really.

佩德拉：神秘学家缺乏纪律和组织必备的理智，如果没有人类领导，他们注定无法成为一支真正的军队。
Pedra: To say nothing of the fact that they lack the organization or discipline that is needed for a true large-scale military operation. Armies need human leadership.

伊里内伊：你忽视了阿尔卡纳，佩德拉，你不知道祂会给信徒带来怎样的影响。
Irinei: You forgot to take Arcana into consideration, Pedra. You don't know what she can do to her followers with her new power.

伊里内伊：基金会需要一支新的军队，尽早组织力量对重塑之手发动袭击。这样一来，也许我们还有先发制人的机会。
Irinei: Whatever the case, we cannot take anything for granted. The Foundation will need the strength to defend itself from future attacks by the Manus. If we act quickly, we may even get ahead of things.

佩德拉：委员会绝不会同意如此不顾后果的策略——
Pedra: I'd like to see what the Committee will think of this plan. I hope they'll have a better grasp of the consequences.

伊里内伊：你根本看不清形势，佩德拉——
Irinei: You're not seeing the board, Pedra.

通讯器已经无法清晰地捕捉到两派领袖的争吵。
The communicator struggles to transmit the two leaders' heated exchange.

刻雷乌斯在另一头秉持着一贯顺从的沉默。
Creius, on the other end, stays quiet, professional, obedient.

等待未久，调停人接管了通讯。
Before long, the mediator takes over the line.

康斯坦丁：我们不排除爆发大规模冲突的可能，但是，在没有绝对可信的证据之前，委员会仍将维持原本的策略。
Constantine: We can't rule out the possibility of a large-scale conflict. However, the Committee will maintain its peace policy until we have reliable evidence.

刻雷乌斯：如果更坏的情况发生了呢？
Creius: And if the worst happens?

康斯坦丁：——整个时代都将化为战场。
Constantine: Then we'll do what we must to survive, even if that means igniting a worldwide war.

玛丽安娜：到了。
Sentinel: We have arrived.

玛尔纱：喔……
Marsha: I see ...

神秘术的余辉逐渐消散，一方宁静的避难所出现在林间空地中。
The glow of arcane skills fades as they approach, revealing their hidden sanctuary.

教堂的穹顶虽然已经倒塌，但雕饰繁复的主体外墙仍然屹立不倒。
It is or was an abbey, appropriately gothic, with ornate stone walls rising up to meet the air—its dome long collapsed.

玛尔纱：这座教堂……是本来就建造在这里的吗？
Marsha: This monastery ... It's not an arcane creation, is it?

玛丽安娜：嗯。石像鬼的神秘术在这片废墟上能发挥很好的效果。
Sentinel: No. It has only been enchanted with our arcane skill "Carthusians."

玛丽安娜：在“加尔都西”神秘术的保护下，教堂和石像鬼都不会被过路的人关注。
Sentinel: Beneath its protection, those that dwell here will go unnoticed by any who pass near.

石像鬼修士：……
Gargoyle Friar: ...

一位身穿修士长袍的石像鬼在草地上赤足行走，意识到访客的到来后，他从书本中抬起头。
A Gargoyle dressed in friar's robes walks barefoot on the grass. He looks up from his book to meet the new arrivals.

玛尔纱：你好，我是基金会的调查员玛尔纱。
Marsha: Greetings. I'm Marsha, Investigator of the St. Pavlov Foundation.

修士轻轻点头，笑容柔和而友善。他伸出一根手指，压在嘴唇上。
The friar nods, offering a smile soft and friendly, then extends a finger and presses it to his lips.

玛尔纱：这是……某种缄默修行吗？
Marsha: Oh, I see. Have you made a vow of silence?

“喀喀——”
"Kra-ka—"

尚未得到回答，骑士又被另一侧岩石碎裂的铿锵声所吸引。
The sound of breaking rock draws her eyes away.

玛尔纱：……？
Marsha: ...?

一扇破损的窄窗下，一座女性雕塑突然活动起来，石质的表面逐渐化为柔软的皮肤。
Beneath a broken narrow window, a stone statue of a woman begins to stir, its surface softening into flesh.

一位满面愁容的妇人出现在玛尔纱眼前，她以夸张的步态向玛丽安娜走去。
Her face is marked by twisted sorrow as she walks toward Sentinel with an exaggerated gait.

石像鬼妇人：玛丽，我的好侄女，你终于回来了！看看你都消瘦成什么样子了。
Female Gargoyle: Marie, my sweetie, thou hast returned to us again! But oh! Child, thou needest rest.

她二话不说，就将玛丽安娜死死搂在怀里，又在她的面颊上留下一个深刻的吻。
She just pulls Marianne into a tight embrace and plants a series of deep kisses on her cheeks.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

玛丽安娜已经习惯了这份沉重的亲族之爱，面不改色地接受了一切。
Sentinel endures the affection with as much grit as she did the bullets.

石像鬼妇人：这是你的朋友吗？
Female Gargoyle: And this is a friend?

妇人转而看向玛尔纱，眼角上更是聚了更多悲伤，几乎要流下泪来。
The woman turns to Marsha, her eyes now pooling with greater sadness.

石像鬼妇人：可怜……可怜的孩子！
Female Gargoyle: Oh, poor child.

她以无可抗拒的力量把骑士拉到自己身边，照例给了她一个令人窒息的拥抱。
The hug comes too quick to dodge and too sturdy to resist, pulling Marsha into a breathtaking embrace.

玛尔纱：唔——
Marsha: Ugh ...

一秒。两秒。三秒——
One second. Two seconds. Three seconds—

——她终于挣脱热情的待客之道。玛尔纱猛吸一口新鲜空气，青草的芬芳浸透了她的肺腔。
The smothering hospitality at last abates, and Marsha takes a deep breath of fresh air, taking in the pleasant scent of grass and wildflowers.

玛尔纱：——呼……嗬……
Marsha: *panting*

石像鬼妇人：你们一定有还有事，可我从来都帮不上忙呢……玛丽总是说我老啦。
Female Gargoyle: Our Marie hast ever been tireless in her toils. 'Tis a shame that she never permits us to aid her. Am I truly too aged to be of service?

石像鬼妇人：哎呀，我居然连一杯茶水都没有准备，这像什么话。
Female Gargoyle: Oh, but perhaps my age hath eclipsed my wisdom. For I have thus far been an unwelcoming host. Allow me to brew you some tea.

她急匆匆地走开了。
She leaves with singular purpose and surprising speed.

玛丽安娜：……她是我姨妈，一年前自顾自地跑到这种危险的地方来，说这个家里的人都不能离开她的照顾。
Sentinel: My aunt is a gentle soul. She came by here one year ago, not fearing the danger, saying she must take care of everyone left in the family.

玛丽安娜：刚才和你打招呼的修士，在去年受伤之后就和他的兄弟一起到这里避难，却不知为何发誓保持静默。
Sentinel: That old lump of stone that greeted us came here to take refuge with his brother after they were injured last year.

她不解地摇了摇头。
She hangs her head with resignation.

玛丽安娜：留在这里的同族不算多。我还有一些家人分散在其他地方，也许只有在战争结束之后才有机会重聚。
Sentinel: Only a small number of my kind dwell here. Many of us remain divided by the war.

玛丽安娜：……你可以在这等着，玛德琳姨妈会给你端来茶水。我去拿你需要的东西。
Sentinel: Enjoy my aunt's hospitality. I shall go now to collect what you seek.

玛尔纱：好，我就在这儿等着。
Marsha: I'll be here then.

玛尔纱：……
Marsha: ...

玛尔纱：等等……
Marsha: Hold on.

她忽然想起来，自己身旁的雕塑也许都是活生生的石像鬼。
She lets herself relax only a moment before noticing the stone-faced Gargoyles that look down at her from a dozen perches.

意识到这一点后，不自在的感觉像蚂蚁一样爬上她的身体。
A thought crawls under her skin.

玛尔纱：……你们好？
Marsha: Hello?

她在原地转了一圈，目光停留在一尊掩面哭泣的少女雕塑身上。
She spins around in place, meeting the unblinking eyes of each statue, stopping on the figure of a young girl.

少女悲惨而哀恸的姿态与其他的雕塑截然不同，很长一段时间内，玛尔纱的注意力都被她吸引。
The girl's hands cover her face in a mournful pose—the silent tragedy of an endless moment of loss.

玛尔纱：这是……
Marsha: This is ...

？？？：为什么玛丽安娜会把你带进来？
???: Why hath my cousin brought you here?

身后传来一声几乎有些无礼的提问。
A voice calls out behind her, rigid and almost rude.

玛尔纱：——？
Marsha: Huh?

一位清瘦高挑的修士出现在露天教堂的庭院中。
A tall, gaunt monk stands in the courtyard.

？？？：你不是我们中的一员，却把战争带到这一片静修之地。基金会又想达成怎样的目的？
???: You are not one of us. You are a bringer of war in our house of peace. What dost your Foundation seek from our quiet halls?

他的声音如同卵石在沙地上摩挲，话语中的指责意味清晰可闻。
There's accusation in the gravelly tone of his voice.

玛尔纱：我不会带来争斗，我只是想帮助你们结束这场战争。
Marsha: You misunderstand. The Foundation isn't bringing war. We're trying to end it.

？？？：战争不需要我们，也不需要你来结束。
???: This war is neither yours nor ours to end.

玛尔纱：你说……什么？
Marsha: What are you saying?

？？？：……
???: ...

男人先是沉默着，似乎在犹豫是否要开口解释。
The monk falls silent, as if debating whether his next words are worth the effort.

随后，他的五官绷成一幅过度揉捏的肖像画。
His face contorts, becoming an exaggeration of self-righteousness.

？？？：这场大战是一次天罚，抛弃信仰的人必然要经受苦难方可获得拯救——战争只会在文明彻底灭亡之日终结。
???: It has come as a divine punishment for the faithless who have turned from God. Its end will come only with the extinction of civilization.

玛尔纱：难道……你希望看到人类和神秘学家走向灭亡？
Marsha: Sounds like you want everyone—humans and arcanists alike—to suffer and die.

？？？：你在曲解我的观念，我又何以憎恶世人——这些受苦受难的灵魂？不，我会为每一个受到伤害的人祈祷。
???: You twist my words, knight. I do not seek this end—this path of suffering—out of hatred for humanity. No, I do so because I pray fervently for their deliverance.

？？？：我说的是“文明”。人们将在这场战争中尝尽“文明”的苦果，而“文明”亦将倾覆其自身。
???: But deliverance waits for the last edifices of this sinful world to crumble. When the faithless nations, as a fire consuming its last embers, burn themselves to ash.

？？？：工厂会被拆毁，以“进步”为名的奇谈怪论会被抛弃，人们会离开如同索多玛一般罪恶的都市。
???: Soon the artifices of modernity, their factories of war and death, will crumble, as Babel before them had; their lies of "advancement" and "revolution" dying with them.

？？？：——我们要回到一个纯洁而朴实的昨日世界。
???: We must return to the innocence of the past, as Nineveh did, heeding the word of God.

玛丽安娜：别再搬出你那一套说教，拉蒂斯。
Sentinel: Enough, cousin.

拉蒂斯：——！
Ladislas: ...!

逐渐沉溺的宣教者被一声呵斥惊醒。
The rebuke breaks his rhythm.

玛丽安娜拦在玛尔纱与拉蒂斯之间。她先与堂兄对视一眼，后者不自觉地向后退了小半步。
Sentinel steps between Marsha and Ladislas, forcing her cousin to take a step away.

玛丽安娜：你让玛德琳姨妈没能端上给客人的茶水。
Sentinel: Your prophecies have kept our guest from her tea.

拉蒂斯：……
Ladislas: ...

玛丽安娜转过身，将一只沉重的军用帆布包递给玛尔纱。
Sentinel turns and hands Marsha a heavy canvas military bag.

玛尔纱：好沉——
Marsha: Um!

玛丽安娜：拿得动吗？
Sentinel: Are you able to lift it?

玛尔纱：完全没问题，我的体力还相当够用。
Marsha: No problem. I can handle it.

拉蒂斯见证这一幕，疑云满面。
Ladislas watches the exchange with abject curiosity.

拉蒂斯：这又是在干什么，玛丽安娜。你刚在蒙佩杀死了基金会的合作人，现在转过头又和基金会站到一起了？
Ladislas: Marianne, is she not of the very Foundation thou sayest lacketh the will to end this war? What fruitless endeavor dost thou now pursue?

玛丽安娜：这是个人交往。从今天起，教堂不再对她隐匿。
Sentinel: She's my friend, Ladislas. I shall grant her the freedom to come and go from here as she wills.

拉蒂斯：可她并不是……
Ladislas: But she is not a ...

玛丽安娜：这里我说了算。
Sentinel: It is my right to do this, is it not?

拉蒂斯：……是。
Ladislas: Yes.

拉蒂斯顺从地低下头，完全失去了一分钟前高高在上的气度。
He lowers his head without protest.

处理完家务事的玛丽安娜再次转向玛尔纱。此时，误入家族纠纷的玛尔纱揣着包裹，已被吓退到五步之外。
Sentinel turns from her kin back to Marsha, who has by now taken several steps away.

玛丽安娜：从1918年开始，我找到过的重要线索都在这，其中包括了与重塑之手有明确合作的军队高层名单。
Sentinel: You will find here all that I've collected since 1918; most useful to you may be a list of those in each military who have made contact with the Manus.

玛丽安娜：如果基金会真的像你说的那样能让这些东西发挥价值，那你就先带它们离开吧。
Sentinel: Take them from here to your Foundation and make of them what you will. I hope they will serve you better than they did me.

玛尔纱：我、我知道了。
Marsha: I will. Thank you.

骑士以惊人的速度撤离了战场。
Marsha seems more than eager to retreat.

玛德琳姨妈立在一根石柱下，手中端着茶水，自责地颔首垂目。
Aunt Madeleine stands at the foot of a stone pillar, tea in her hand, and nods in self-reproach.

石像鬼妇人：……
Female Gargoyle: ...

露天教堂的庭院中安静了一会儿。
The courtyard falls still.

拉蒂斯沉寂良久，终于板起他那张枯瘦的脸，再度开口。
Ladislas breaks his silence with a withering glare.

拉蒂斯：堂亲……为什么你总是如此执着地走入纷争？我们本可以避开这一切。
Ladislas: Cousin, why hast thou concerned thyself with the affairs of this sinful world? We are involved now at our peril.

玛丽安娜：即使这场战争真的是一场天罚，那世人受的苦难也已经够多。
Sentinel: Even if this war was, as you believe, a divine punishment, the people have suffered enough.

拉蒂斯：——可人们并不知悔改！
Ladislas: Have they? I see no sackcloth, only ashes!

拉蒂斯弓着背，靠近教堂角落中掩面哭泣的少女。
He motions to the weeping girl tucked in the sanctuary niche.

拉蒂斯：难道艾格尼丝的现状还不能令你有所觉悟吗？
Ladislas: Hast thou learned nothing from our dear Agnès?

玛丽安娜：别把她牵扯进来。
Sentinel: Leave her out of this.

拉蒂斯：可正是艾格尼丝带来了有关战争的预兆……
Ladislas: It was she who prophesied this war ...

男人遁入一场回忆。
He drags up the memory with sharp intention.

拉蒂斯：在战争爆发之后，艾格尼丝陷入了长久石化的沉眠中。
Ladislas: And whose body turned to stone as it came to pass.

拉蒂斯：她是我们之中最接近圣洁的人，命运本不应该如此，这一定是她通过自我牺牲的方式为我们带来征兆……
Ladislas: Was she not the closest of us all to the ear of our Lord? Then I can see only one reason for her sacrifice. It is a warning to us.

玛丽安娜：如果艾格尼丝“雕塑化”真的是一种预兆，为什么老天不把话说得更明白些？
Sentinel: Tell me, if that is so, why God would choose such a warning?

拉蒂斯：因为这是神圣的隐秘——如同古老时代的书卷，总是把真理与奥秘隐藏在最晦涩的文字中。
Ladislas: Revelation and prophecy oft appear inscrutable to those that disbelieve them, until their truth is made manifest.

拉蒂斯的声音颤抖起来，喉头演奏出集谦卑与骄傲于一体的宣道式嗓音。
Ladislas's voice trembles, a practiced tension of humility and pride.

拉蒂斯：而我，解读了这份隐秘——它警醒我们避开战争，保持隐匿。
Ladislas: But I do believe, and I see clearly what thou hast not—that our Lord bids us to neither fight nor end this war.

拉蒂斯：我向你预言，战争绝不可能在灭尽一切罪恶之前结束，艾格尼丝只会在一个纯洁的世界与我们相见。
Ladislas: Because it hath come as the next great deluge to sweep this sinful world away. Agnès will return to us again as our past innocence is found and rebuilt from their ruins.

拉蒂斯：到那时，必然要有虔敬之人来重建新世界的信仰。而我们的族裔担负着的就是这样的使命。
Ladislas: But the faith must be preserved if it is to be rebuilt, and these labors will be the task of the faithful—of we, the Gargoyles.

拉蒂斯：不要再涉身于杀戮之中，不要再呼唤血液中的恶魔，玷污本就有罪的灵魂。你理应听从我的教诲，堂亲。
Ladislas: I pray thee heed my words, cousin: Lay down thy sword of vengeance. Do not answer to the whispering demon in thy blood, nor stain thy soul already so burdened with sin!

他以尊长般的威严结束了最后一句话，嘴角保持着长时间的颤抖。
He lets his words cling to his lips with solemn weight.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

已经听惯了的玛丽安娜未能受到鼓舞，反倒是哀伤漫上了她的双眼。
His cousin, however, has never been easy to preach to. She stiffens, sorrow and purpose welling in her eyes.

玛丽安娜：机枪，火炮，坦克，飞机……
Sentinel: Guns, cannons, tanks, bombs ...

玛丽安娜：如果你记得这些机器如何将我们毁灭，又如何变得越来越强大，你就应该明白——
Sentinel: You do remember how these devices have destroyed our lives, do you not? Then surely you already know ...

玛丽安娜：昨日的世界已经被彻底毁灭，我们永远也回不到过去。
Sentinel: That the innocence of the past does not simply lie buried for us to rebuild. It is dead and gone.

玛丽安娜：如果背负罪孽就能结束这场战争……这个代价对我来说，实在是微不足道。
Sentinel: If a stain on my soul is what it takes to end this war, then I shall not hesitate to stain it so.

拉蒂斯惊骇不已，眼中闪着泪花。他背过身，面向祭坛，瘦长的身躯隐藏在高大花窗投下的阴影中。
Ladislas is stunned. He fights back tears and turns to face the altar. The light from the stained glass windows wreathes him like a mourner's cloak.

拉蒂斯：你的发言令我惊恐，堂亲，我必须提醒你，我们的祖先中出现过真正堕落的恶魔。
Ladislas: Hast thou forgotten our ancestral peril? Or the manifold names we have stricken from our line when they turned from the righteous path? The demon blood hath overtaken our kin before, as I fear it soon will overtake thee.

拉蒂斯：而我……不希望“玛丽安娜”也成为必须被从谱系中抹去的一个名字。
Ladislas: I do not wish to blot out thy name as well ... Marianne.

11TH-13 和平的价码 / Concessions for Peace

梅蕾尔：嗯……
Merel: *sigh*

留在安全区内待命的“Ⅻ”小队成员百无聊赖地执行着烦琐的指令。
The bored and idle remnant of Squad "XII" carries out her as yet tedious orders.

她在一扇窗前驻足，眯着眼向室内看去。
She stops by a window, squinting inside.

梅蕾尔：……
Merel: ...

视线所及之处，只有破损的家具残骸。几盏打碎的瓷器上已结成蛛网。
Broken furniture and cobwebs woven between cracked and forgotten china.

一台造型独特的反制神秘术监测设备正立在未经清理的地面上。
A uniquely shaped counter-arcanum monitoring device disrupts the decaying scene.

梅蕾尔：——完全没有打扫过嘛。
Merel: Clearly no one's bothered to do any cleanup, then.

护卫兵打开窗，将身子探进去，面罩帮助她隔绝了大多数灰尘。
She opens the window and leans in, her mask blocking out the sudden puff of dust.

按照长官的指示，她拿出一张透明的布条，放置在神秘学设备边。
Following her officer's instructions, she pulls out a transparent strip of cloth and places it by the device.

布条很快显露出颜色，一行小字在其上浮现。
The cloth changes color rapidly, and a line of neat letters appears on its surface.

梅蕾尔：“反制设备运行正常”——看来没有我的事了。
Merel: "Counter-arcanum device operating normally." Looks like I'm not needed here either.

她翻窗而出。
She climbs back out the window.

梅蕾尔：唔，嘿——嗯？
Merel: Hmph. Hmm? Aren't you ...?

玛尔纱：……梅蕾尔。
Marsha: Merel.

梅蕾尔：玛尔纱？
Merel: Marsha?

年轻士兵噌的一下站起来上前迎接，她长出一口气，看起来如释重负。
The young soldier springs up to greet her, visibly relieved.

梅蕾尔：你终于……回来了！
Merel: It really is you! You're back finally!

玛尔纱：帕拉维扬还好吗？
Marsha: Is Paravyan alright?

梅蕾尔：病床上躺着呢，累得够呛，但至少没有缺胳膊少腿，应该很快就能恢复了。
Merel: Oh, poor guy's had a hard time of it, but at least he's still in one piece. He's lying in a sickbed as we speak. He should recover soon.

梅蕾尔：他说农庄那边收获不算太大，帕拉维扬带人去检查了一番，除了装甲车之外，没有特别多的重要信息。
Merel: It's too bad he didn't find anything too useful in the village, well, aside from that armored vehicle.

玛尔纱：幸好，玛丽安娜和我们去了同一个地方。
Marsha: Fortunately, Sentinel happened to be there at the same time.

梅蕾尔：所以，真的是她——刺杀希施费尔德上校的凶手？
Merel: So it really was her, the one who assassinated Colonel Hirschfelder?

玛尔纱：对，她给了我一大批有关重塑之手的情报，我已经送给刻雷乌斯长官了。
Marsha: Yes. She'd collected a wealth of evidence concerning Manus Vindictae. I've already delivered it to Commander Creius.

玛尔纱：至于刺杀事件，是一场误会。
Marsha: As for the assassination, it turns out her actions weren't entirely unjustifiable. Let's just consider it a misunderstanding.

梅蕾尔：误会？——可她……杀了人……
Merel: Misunderstanding? She literally killed a guy.

玛尔纱：说到这个，我也一样。
Marsha: She's not the only one.

骑士无意识地用拇指揉搓着掌心的缺口——旧伤已经很久没有痒过了。
Marsha unconsciously rubs the old scars on her palms, feeling them itch like never before.

梅蕾尔：……
Merel: ...

她抿着嘴唇，连带着在面罩上挤出一条扭曲的细缝。
Merel presses her lips together, creating a twisted crease in her mask.

梅蕾尔：好吧，我……总之，我担心你会出什么事，就像……
Merel: Well, I ... Anyway, I was just worried that something bad might've happened to you, like what happened to ...

玛尔纱：就像？
Marsha: To whom?

梅蕾尔：就像查尔斯和阿曼达。4个小时前，他们和安全区失去了联系，已经好一阵子没有收到他们的回报。
Merel: Charles and Amanda. We haven't heard from them in over four hours now.

玛尔纱：……是去299高地侦查的小队？派出救援了吗？
Marsha: They were dispatched to investigate Hill 299, correct? Has any help been sent their way?

梅蕾尔：刻雷乌斯长官已经派人去打探情况了，应该很快就会有结果。
Merel: Commander Creius sent some men to look for them. Hopefully, we'll hear some good news soon.

梅蕾尔：至于其他的调查员小队，大多数都有了消息，还有几个已经带着不少线索回到安全区了。
Merel: Most of the other teams have finished their investigations. A few of them are already in the safe zone, actually. Apparently, they've found a lot of useful info.

梅蕾尔：我们应该……不用再出任务了吧？
Merel: So, we won't have to head back out again, right?

年轻士兵小心翼翼地看着玛尔纱，像是在等她说出一个肯定的答案。
Merel watches Marsha carefully, as if waiting for her to confirm something.

梅蕾尔：前线每天都在被炮火轰炸，如果一不小心……
Merel: The front's getting shelled to hell and back. I mean, chances are we'll ...

玛尔纱拍了拍她的肩膀。
Marsha pats her on the shoulder.

玛尔纱：玛丽安娜分享的线索非常充分，等到联系上299高地的小队，我们差不多能收工了。
Marsha: The evidence Sentinel provided is quite damning. Our job here will be over just as soon as we can get ahold of the team at Hill 299.

玛尔纱：别太害怕了。
Marsha: Don't worry.

玛尔纱递交来的证物照片副本在桌面上排开。
Copies of the evidence Marsha submitted have been spread across the table.

私人信件、带有标记的军用地图、作战计划书、工程蓝图，以及被污损与篡改的证件……
Personal letters, marked military maps, battle plans, engineering blueprints, defaced and altered documents ...

格奥尔格：……
Georg: ...

一同被放在桌面上的，还有来自其他调查员从前线各地找回的物证。它们按照从1918年开始的时间顺序粗略排列着。
Along with them on the table are exhibits recovered by other investigators from across the front line, arranged in rough chronological order starting from 1918.

格奥尔格：不……难以置信。
Georg: This is unbelievable!

议员代表紧盯着桌面的众多图片，洪水般涌来的信息在一瞬间击溃了他的理解能力。
He stares at the pile, the sheer flood of information overwhelming him.

格奥尔格：这些资料中的内容竟与最荒唐的阴谋论调完全吻合……之前的多次和谈确实是在重塑之手的计划下破产的。
Georg: These documents ... The evidence is undeniable. Every one of those absurd conspiracy theories was true. The 1918 peace negotiations really were sabotaged by Manus Vindictae!

格奥尔格：在这之后的战争……双方都不断陷入明显的陷阱……1919年末的那场惨败之后，获胜方也意外地没有扩大战果……
Georg: The nations on both sides of this war have been under the deception of an invisible enemy. It is no wonder that even the victors of the 1919 offensive gained no real advantage.

格奥尔格：我的老天……这意味着，重塑之手在向双方提供援助和情报，以此不让任何一方取胜。
Georg: My God. To think Manus Vindictae has been sharing war secrets with both sides to ensure neither can win this war.

格奥尔格：——合谋。战争不过是重塑之手在控制军队之后展开的屠杀。我如何才能想象到这么荒唐的事！
Georg: That they have used our commanders as tools for their massacre. It is nigh on unimaginable!

政客猛地抬头。
He looks up with sudden realization.

格奥尔格：这不是一个国家的事，在如此充分的证据面前，大半个欧洲的军队高层都要倒台。
Georg: This does not simply concern one nation. These documents could topple nearly all of Europe's military leaders.

格奥尔格：我们甚至已经有了一份足够详尽的名单，只要动作够快，我们有希望将这些出卖国家的叛徒全部逮捕。
Georg: With this list of Manus defectors in our hands, and if we act with haste, we may finally put every one of them behind bars.

等到格奥尔格的情绪相对稳定，刻雷乌斯才补上一句建议。
Waiting for Georg's mood to stabilize, Creius adds a word of advice.

刻雷乌斯：受到精神影响的军官和士兵，可以交由科算中心治疗。艾伯哈特的例子证明这种影响是可以被消除的。
Creius: Let me remind you that Laplace may be able to heal these so-called "defectors." Eberhard's case proved that the Manus's mental influence can be purged.

格奥尔格：没错，没错——不能再等了。现在是行动的时刻，首相与议会已经做好了发动致命一击的准备。
Georg: Yes, yes, of course. Whatever the case, we must act as soon as possible. The chancellor and the parliament are prepared to strike.

在宏伟前景的光照下，议员代表的双手开始颤抖，几乎无法抓稳手中的纸张。
Finding light in a once grim future, he starts to shake, sending ripples through the papers in his hands.

刻雷乌斯：证据已经足够，我们的确没有必要再等。
Creius: Agreed. The evidence is sufficient. There is no need to delay.

格奥尔格：当然，这很好……！重返家园的士兵们会感谢我们的。
Georg: Wonderful! Just think of the soldiers finally making their way home.

格奥尔格：我们将为欧洲留下一个世纪的和平！
Georg: This is the day we secure a century of peace for Europe!

刻雷乌斯：不错，这听起来像是一句能够被历史铭记的名言。
Creius: Hmph. Sounds like a line for the history books.

议员代表没有心思在乎刻雷乌斯最后这句有些辛辣味的评论，他将所有文件都塞进公文包，匆匆离去。
He has no mind to react to Creius's parting jab. Stuffing all the documents into his briefcase, he rushes out.

刻雷乌斯将桌上剩余的凌散文件整理好，从桌面下方拿出一台通讯器。
Straightening the remaining mess on his desk, Creius retrieves a hidden communicator.

它已经被接通了很长一段时间。
It's been connected the entire time.

刻雷乌斯：……一切都在按计划进行。
Creius: Everything's going according to plan.

康斯坦丁：很好，其他地区的负责人也已经通过相同的方式，向主和派政要分享了情报。
Constantine: Good. The other teams have shared the same intelligence with the pacifist political leaders in their respective regions.

康斯坦丁：基金会现在只需留意是否有重塑之手的人员出面干预。
Constantine: All the Foundation has to do now is watch for any interference from Manus Vindictae.

维尔汀：可是……用这种方式推动和谈是否会带来更大的动荡？
Vertin: But, won't this approach cause even more turbulence?

刻雷乌斯：司辰？
Creius: Timekeeper?

这一次，身处副会长办公室的不再是两位立场相悖的委员。
He had been expecting the faction leaders, making this an unexpected relief.

维尔汀：我只是恰好在旁听，刻雷乌斯。
Vertin: Oh, yes, Creius. I was just listening in.

刻雷乌斯：原来如此……这个结局不会比我们眼下经历的战争更糟了，司辰。
Creius: I see. In any case, the outcome can't be worse than the war we're living through, Timekeeper.

刻雷乌斯：拿真实历史的记载来说，这场大战曾造成千万名士兵的死亡。
Creius: As I'm sure you learned in your history studies, this war claimed tens of millions of soldiers' lives.

刻雷乌斯：受战争直接或间接影响而死亡的平民人数也与之相当。
Creius: Not to mention the equally massive number of civilian casualties, whether direct or otherwise.

刻雷乌斯：现在，我们处在错谬历史之下的1920年，死亡数字也许只会有增无减。
Creius: We are now two years on from what should've been the end of this war. The death toll has already climbed much higher, and it will only continue to rise if we don't put an end to it soon.

刻雷乌斯：——我们已经促成了一个相对较好的结局。
Creius: At least our efforts have won us a marginally better outcome.

维尔汀：……我能理解。
Vertin: I see.

康斯坦丁：总之，战争结束了。
Constantine: In short, the war is already over.

康斯坦丁：主和派上台之后，蒙佩会成为下一次停火协定的签订地点。
Constantine: Once the pacifist political parties take power, an armistice will surely be signed in Montpaix.

刻雷乌斯：也许现在说这个有些不合时宜，不过，我想问……
Creius: This may not be the time, but I have a question to ask.

刻雷乌斯：如果基金会最终没能阻止重塑之手的谋划，委员会有没有商讨出可以执行的备选方案？
Creius: Does the Foundation Committee have any contingency plans should things take a turn for the worse?

房间中的沉默印证了通讯另一头的猜想。
The silence in the room confirms the suspicions of the voice on the other end.

维尔汀：……你发现什么异常了吗？
Vertin: Did you notice something suspicious?

前执夜人尽可能地从回忆中捞起一些可疑的细节。
The former vigil officer fishes out as many suspicious details from his memories as he can.

刻雷乌斯：这要回到希施费尔德的问题上。
Creius: It's about Hirschfelder's assassination ...

刻雷乌斯：你们是否记得玛尔纱提交报告的一处细节……
Creius: Do you remember a certain detail from Marsha's report?

玛丽安娜：也许在你们看来，他的死导致前线战火重燃，可是……即使我不杀他，谈判也注定会失败。
Sentinel: You think his death to be the spark of a reignited war, but, even if I had stayed my hand from him, your plans would have been for naught.

刻雷乌斯：如果这是一场注定失败的谈判，重塑之手又为何让希施费尔德冒着暴露的风险，同意与基金会的人员在蒙佩接触？
Creius: If that were so, why would the Manus risk exposing Hirschfelder? Why would they allow him to meet with the Foundation in Montpaix?

刻雷乌斯：换句话说，如果希施费尔德不被刺杀，这场停火谈判是否会成为一场漫长而无果的交涉拉锯战？
Creius: If Hirschfelder hadn't been killed, would the negotiations have become a fruitless tug-of-war?

维尔汀：重塑之手在配合基金会做一件注定失败的事。
Vertin: Manus Vindictae would only cooperate with the Foundation on something that was sure to fail.

凭借与重塑之手接触的经验，一种直觉式的猜想很快被构建起来。
An intuitive guess is assembled, drawing on the experience of prior contact with Manus Vindictae.

维尔汀：……他们在吸引基金会的注意力？
Vertin: Could it be that they're purposely diverting our attention?

刻雷乌斯：这也是我的猜测，司辰。
Creius: My thoughts exactly, Timekeeper.

刻雷乌斯：不过……现在没有任何事情，比即将到来的和平还要重要。
Creius: That said, securing peace is our top priority at the moment.

11TH-14 两磅糖 / Two Pounds of Sugar

格奥尔格：……过去六年的战争，几乎要将我们民族积攒的信念摧毁殆尽，有明见之人早已知晓，战争不应该继续进行下去。
Georg: 6 years of war have deeply shaken the resolve and faith of our nation. It is clear to all that this war cannot continue any longer.

格奥尔格：将军们害怕和平会让他们失去权势，竟不惜与重塑之手这样的邪教团体合作，好让更多年轻人毫无价值地失去生命。
Georg: Afraid of the loss of power that peace may bring to them, leaders across Europe elected to collaborate with the evil cult, Manus Vindictae, sacrificing countless young lives in meaningless carnage.

格奥尔格：可重塑之手唯一的目的就是让战争带来更多杀戮，他们阴谋的触手早已秘密地伸向了所有交战国的高层。
Georg: But carnage is precisely what Manus Vindictae desires. Unseen by all, their wicked influence has long wormed its way into the leadership of every warring nation.

格奥尔格：但是，这一切已经结束了，所有涉嫌叛国的将领都已遭到逮捕，很快，法庭将对他们做出公正的审判。
Georg: But worry not. Their conspiracy has been thwarted. Every treasonous general has been arrested and will soon face a fair court-martial.

格奥尔格：为国家浴血奋战的英雄们即将踏上返乡的旅程，祖国将以无比的热情和感激迎接他们的归来。
Georg: The heroes who bled for the fatherland are finally returning home, where we will welcome them with smiles on our faces and gratitude in our hearts.

格奥尔格：西线的战事，将于1920年11月11日上午11时正式结束。
Georg: On the eleventh hour of the eleventh day of the eleventh month of the year 1920, this war will come to an end.

刺杀事件过去数周之后，几近荒芜的蒙佩街道再度变得拥挤。
Weeks have passed since the assassination, and the desolate streets of Montpaix have sprung to life again.

来自各个交战国的代表们聚集在道路两旁，头戴柔软礼帽的人占据了主导，只有少数军帽掺杂其中。
Delegates from the belligerent nations gather on opposite sides of the road. Soft bowler hats and ties decorate the event, mixed with occasional peaked caps and military epaulettes, though now precious few.

刻雷乌斯：……
Creius: ...

更多的政要，意味着更严苛的安保。
More dignitaries demand tighter security.

即使各国都派遣了安保力量在周边警戒，行动队长仍然以相当坚定的态度向基金会请求了额外增援。
Each nation came with their own detail, but the operations commander insists on further reinforcements from the Foundation.

基金会安保Ⅰ：……第三次常规巡逻已完成，没有发现异常情况，长官。
Foundation Security Staff I: Third routine patrol complete. No anomalies detected, sir.

基金会安保Ⅱ：神秘术侦测小组未提供新的警告，是否降低监视等级？
Foundation Security Staff II: No further warnings from the arcanum detection group. Should we lower the alert level?

刻雷乌斯：保持原有戒备模式不变，指挥所内至少要常驻两个小队的安保力量。
Creius: Maintain the current level. I need at least two squads on standby at the command post at all times.

基金会安保们：明白，长官。
Foundation Security Staff: Yes, sir.

身穿白衣的基金会安保尽职尽责地执行下一轮指令。
Clad in white, Foundation security diligently carry out their orders.

在熙来攘往的小镇道路上，行动队长突兀地立在原地，闭目凝神片刻，耳中只有嘈杂而难以分辨的噪音。
On the busy town road, the commander suddenly stops. Eyes shut, he focuses, trying to sift through the din of stuffy conversation.

刻雷乌斯：……
Creius: ...

他打开通讯器，另一端立刻响应了接入请求。
He activates his communicator. The line sparks to life instantly.

刻雷乌斯：联系上查尔斯和阿曼达了吗？
Creius: Any response from Charles and Amanda?

？？？：——没有，自他们抵达299高地之后就再没有回应，呼出去的信号像掉进了山洞里。
???: Negative. They've been silent since they reached Hill 299. It's like we're calling into the abyss.

？？？：也许他们没有其他调查员那么幸运，已经被重塑之手杀害。
???: Chances are, they got snuffed out by the Manus. Luck can't be on everyone's side.

刻雷乌斯：至少要找到他们的尸体……
Creius: Even so, we need to recover the bodies.

？？？：让他们带着功勋章下葬吗？
???: What, so they can be buried with shiny medals? Tch.

通讯器另一头的声音带着明目张胆的嗤笑。
The voice on the other end bites back with a sneer.

？？？：这些铁片片说不定我在战场上就能捡到一大堆。
???: A couple minutes' walk on the battlefield, and I'll find you a whole pile of that scrap metal.

刻雷乌斯：……还有重塑之手活动的迹象吗？
Creius: Any other signs of enemy activity?

？？？：我连一个重塑之手的黑点也找不见了，也许军队倒台确实挫败了他们原本的计划。
???: Nope, not a single trace of the Manus scum. Maybe all this military and political turmoil messed up their plans after all.

刻雷乌斯：……我希望如此。
Creius: Let's hope so.

刻雷乌斯：299高地的事情要查清楚，我不希望有任何从眼皮底下溜走的东西。
Creius: Whatever the case, we need to get to the bottom of what happened at Hill 299. We can't afford to let any potential threats slip past us.

？？？：我已经在路上了。
???: Already on my way there.

？？？：不过，这事儿结束之后我建议你去找个心理医生，治疗一下你的“重塑之手恐惧症”。
???: How about seeing a psychologist when all this is all over, Creius? Maybe they'll finally cure your Manus Vindictae paranoia.

刻雷乌斯：保持警惕。
Creius: Keep your eyes and ears open.

他切断了通讯。
He ends the call.

在街道一处无人在意的角落，收尸人踽踽独行。
In an unnoticed corner of the street, a grim figure walks alone.

卡戎：……
Charon: ...

他在蒙佩的事务也已结束，在停火前夕，前线还有更多等待他收集的尸体。
Charon's work in Montpaix is over, and even now, on the eve of a ceasefire, there are many corpses on the front line waiting for him.

收尸人想念起陪伴自己的马儿。
His disjointed thoughts dwell on the horse that once accompanied him.

卡戎：不知道安德烈森还会不会回来。
Charon: Will Andreas ever return?

但遗失对他来说是一件已经习惯的事。他慢悠悠地转身，走向通往蒙佩之外的小路。
But loss has ever been his first companion. Resigned, he shuffles down the road away from Montpaix.

梅蕾尔：嘿——先生，请等一等！卡戎先生！
Merel: Hey, sir! Mr. Charon!

卡戎：……？
Charon: ...?

“Ⅻ”小队队员气喘吁吁地跑到他身边。
Merel runs up to him, arriving out of breath.

梅蕾尔：呼……你要走了吗？玛尔纱和我说你要回前线了。
Merel: *pant* You leaving already? Marsha told me you're heading back to the front.

卡戎：我正准备出发，请问你是？
Charon: She speaks the truth. And you are ...?

梅蕾尔：噢——对了，你不认识我。但是玛尔纱和我提起过你——玛尔纱，你认识吗？
Merel: Oh right, you don't know me. But Marsha told me loads about you. You know Marsha, don't you?

卡戎努力回忆着，在破碎的记忆中拼凑出了玛尔纱的样貌。
Charon struggles to remember, piecing together Marsha's appearance from his shattered memories.

卡戎：是那位骑士，我记得。
Charon: Yes. The knight. I ... remember.

梅蕾尔：那就好，我也得去一趟前线，要不要和我们车队一起走？
Merel: Great. I'm heading to the front as well. Do you want to, or, er, I mean, could you please join our convoy?

卡戎：一起？
Charon: You wish for me to join you?

梅蕾尔：你比我更清楚前线的情况。
Merel: You know the front better than anyone.

年轻士兵掏了掏口袋，摸出半块被细心重新封好包装的巧克力，塞到了卡戎手里。
Merel digs into her pocket, fishing out half a bar of chocolate that has been carefully resealed and wrapped, and slips it into Charon's hand.

梅蕾尔：拜托了，卡戎先生，和我们一起去吧。
Merel: Please, Mr. Charon. Come with us. We could really use your help.

前线安静得不可思议。
The front is still as death.

埃里希：……
Erich: ...

罗尔夫：……有些奇怪……
Rudolph: This quiet feels strange.

埃里希：闭嘴，罗尔夫。该死的，这真是……
Erich: Shut up, Rudolph! Why, damn it.

壕沟内的士兵们仰头看向天空。
Soldiers in the trenches gaze up at the empty sky.

停火协定尚未签订，但前线的军事活动已经全部中止。士兵们只是在壕沟内蹲守最后数日，就可以启程返回家乡。
The ceasefire has not yet been signed, but all military activity on the front line has been suspended. Yet the soldiers still man their trenches, hoping desperately to go home.

埃里希：噢……威利，弗兰兹……
Erich: Ugh, why did Willi and Franz have to ...

埃里希用粗糙的手指把五官揉得一片扭曲。
Erich rubs his face, his calloused fingers twisting his features with stress.

距离他们最后一次听见炮弹炸裂与机枪嘶鸣已经过去了六个小时。
6 hours have now passed since the last time a shell exploded or a machine gun rattled.

奇异的寂静落在硝烟未尽的漫长防线上，士兵们甚至能隐约听见铁丝网被风吹动的声音。
Yet the quiet has a strangeness of its own. The faint cold wind shivers the lines of barbed wire with audible tensile contractions.

罗尔夫：所以，到底谁赢了？
Rudolph: So, who won in the end?

埃里希：谁还在乎呢？
Erich: Does it matter?

罗尔夫点点头。
Rudolph's head sways between a nod and a shake.

罗尔夫：我们是不是该收拾东西了？
Rudolph: Then, uh, sh-should we start packing up?

埃里希：是啊，把你那些笔记本都带回去吧。你回去之后不是要把他们编成书吗？
Erich: Sure. You can finally take all those notebooks of yours back home. Weren't you planning to turn them into a book?

罗尔夫：也许回去之后，我再也不想写任何字了。你呢，埃里希，你回去之后打算做什么？
Rudolph: Yeah, but I don't know. Maybe once I stop being a soldier, my motivation to write will stop too. What about you, Erich? What will you do?

埃里希：做面包，我家就是干这个的。我老爹要见我回去了，一定会高兴得发疯。他会开一瓶红酒……
Erich: Make bread, I think. My family runs a bakery. I can already see it: my old man cracking open his finest bottle of Pinot Noir when I arrive.

埃里希心生一计。
An idea crosses Erich's mind.

埃里希：说起红酒……我们能到对面去要点吃的吗？他们有红酒，还有柔软的白面包，上次那个俘虏就是这么说的。
Erich: Speaking of which, I bet we can go and ask the boys on the other side for some food and drinks. They've got wine and soft white bread. At least, that's what POW said.

罗尔夫：我想吃桃子罐头……
Rudolph: I wouldn't mind some canned peaches.

埃里希：我都给你带来，谁叫我他妈真当上了连长呢？
Erich: Fine, I'll get you your peaches. Hmph. I guess I really am your captain, huh?

说来也巧，埃里希身旁刚好有一块碎布。他拿起来，绑在步枪上，打算当作一面和平的旗帜。
He scrounges around for a bit of scrap cloth, then ties it to his rifle, intending it to be a peace flag.

卡戎：埃里希——不要离开战壕，请保持一些耐心。
Charon: Erich, do not hurry to leave the trenches. Have patience.

士官不知何时进入了战壕。
Charon slinks back into the trench without a word.

埃里希扔下绑着旗帜的步枪，靠近卡戎身前。
Erich drops his rifle for now and steps toward Charon.

埃里希：噢——你回来了。有什么新消息吗？
Erich: Oh, Charon, you're back. Any news?

卡戎：代表团都抵达了蒙佩，距离停火协定签订还有48小时，在这期间不要让自己置身险境。
Charon: The delegations from various nations have arrived in Montpaix. The armistice will be signed in 48 hours. It is best to avoid any unnecessary danger until then.

罗尔夫：可是，我很饿，卡戎。你有没有带一点吃的回来。
Rudolph: But I'm starving, Charon. You didn't bring any food, did you?

梅蕾尔：——我这儿有吃的！
Merel: I did!

基金会成员出人意料地出现在士兵们的视野中。
The new voice catches Erich off guard.

埃里希：你是什么人？
Erich: Who are you?

卡戎：基金会为前线士兵提供了一些食物和饮料，她会负责为你们分发这些物资。
Charon: The Foundation has issued food and drinks to be brought to the soldiers on the front. She is responsible for distributing them.

梅蕾尔：没错，差不多就是这样。
Merel: Yeah, more or less what he said.

梅蕾尔：还有几箱啤酒没来得及卸货，谁和我一起去？
Merel: Right, I need a hand unloading these crates of beer. Any volunteers?

士兵：——有啤酒！
Soldier: There's beer?!

士兵们应声而起，还有不少人从地下掩体中钻出来。
The troops all rise at once, climbing over themselves to get out from the dugouts below.

狭窄的壕沟内一瞬间被挤得水泄不通。
In an instant, the trench is packed wall to wall.

梅蕾尔：别——别急啊，东西很多的。
Merel: Hey, easy there! There's plenty to go around.

埃里希：停下——停下！除了我叫到名字的，都给我回去！
Erich: Boys, boys! You're humiliating yourselves! Get in line, and I'll choose a few of you to help out.

埃里希喊出几个名字，随后，他转向卡戎。
Erich calls out a few names, then turns to Charon.

埃里希：布劳恩少校呢？
Erich: Where's Major Braun?

卡戎：他仍然被留在蒙佩。
Charon: He is needed in Montpaix.

埃里希：好吧，那还挺可惜的。
Erich: Ah, that's a shame.

埃里希：虽然他是个王八蛋，但是……管他呢，战争已经结束了。就这样吧。
Erich: Yeah, he's got a slap-worthy face, but, ugh, who cares? The war's over. Forget it.

埃里希：你、你，还有你，都过来，跟我去帮基金会的人把东西搬进来。
Erich: You, you, and you, come here and unload the crates for the nice Foundation girl.

食物很快被分发到每一位士兵手上。
The food is passed from hand to hand until it reaches every soldier.

战壕内依旧弥漫着那一股令人难以忍受的腐烂气味，但这丝毫没有影响士兵们的食欲。
Rot and despair still hang over the trenches, but they do nothing to dampen their appetites.

罗尔夫：……
Rudolph: ...

罗尔夫捧着手中的黄油蛋糕，生怕一不小心将它揉碎——他已经很久没有见过这么柔软和明亮的食物了。
Rudolph cups a butter cake in his hands, desperately afraid of crumbling it. He hasn't seen such soft and bright food in a long time.

他一口吞下，不自觉闭着眼仔细咀嚼。
Then all at once, he stuffs it into his mouth.

埃里希来到他面前，拉开罗尔夫的眼皮，将一只装满金黄色啤酒的铝杯塞到他手上。
Erich hurries to his side, shoving a mug of golden lager into his hands.

埃里希：来，喝一杯。
Erich: Come on, cheers.

罗尔夫：……好的。
Rudolph: Fine.

梅蕾尔：算我一个，干杯！
Merel: Count me in! Cheers!

士兵们：干杯！
Soldiers: Cheers!

金属杯不断地互相敲击，蹦出清脆明亮的杂乱乐曲。
The metal cups tap rhythmically, shaping into a joyful and bright tune.

一阵飘渺的合唱声远远地飘了过来。
From far across the field, their clinking percussion is met with raucous singing voices.

埃里希：什么？你们听到有人在唱歌吗？
