Erich: What's that? Do you boys hear singing?

罗尔夫：我也听见了，是……在对面？他们在唱什么？
Rudolph: I hear it, too, from the other side. Why are they singing?

梅蕾尔：噢……这些算是人道主义物资，对面战壕也有份。
Merel: Oh right, these are humanitarian rations. They've been given to the other side too.

梅蕾尔：也许他们也在庆祝吧。
Merel: They're probably celebrating.

埃里希跳起来，重新拿起绑好“和平旗帜”的步枪，探出战壕不断挥舞。
Erich jumps over the top, waving his whitish flag toward the other side.

埃里希：他妈的，那就干脆再弄点噪音出来吧。
Erich: Hell yeah! Come on, boys, let's make some noise ourselves!

埃里希：干杯，对面的坏东西，听得懂吗？——干杯！
Erich: Cheers to you bastards over there! You understand what I'm saying? Cheers!

对面的士兵：——干杯！
Soldiers on the Other Side: Cheers!

士兵们：停火——万岁！！
Soldiers: To peace!

士兵们：万岁！！！
Soldiers: To life!

士兵们庆祝停火的情绪将持续到深夜。
The ceasefire celebration stretches late into the night.

重回战壕的卡戎一直蹲坐在角落里，以过分宁静的态度注视着眼前的一切。
Charon watches the festivities crouched in a dim corner of the trench.

梅蕾尔：哎，你怎么一直在这里躲着？
Merel: Hey, what are you doing holed up here alone?

还是有人注意到了他。
Despite his best efforts, he is noticed.

士官抬起头。
Charon lifts his head.

卡戎：我想我不太适合出现在那样的氛围中。
Charon: The presence of the dead is not fitting among such joy.

梅蕾尔：你当然可以。
Merel: What are you talking about? You fit in perfectly.

她摇晃着手中的香肠罐头与纸包软糖。
She waves a can of sausages and a paper-wrapped candy.

梅蕾尔：也许你不需要吃太多东西，但就连味道也不想尝试吗？
Merel: I mean, I know you don't exactly eat much, but you can still enjoy the taste of the stuff, right?

梅蕾尔：我认识一个脑袋是玻璃缸的家伙，就连它也会偶尔吃些什么……
Merel: I even know a guy with a fish tank for a head who eats every once in a while.

梅蕾尔：噢……我倒是没有真正见过它吃东西的场景……那些咖啡都被倒进玻璃缸里了吗？
Merel: That said, I've never actually seen him do it. Hmm, does he just pour the coffee straight into his fish tank, or what?

卡戎：感谢你分享的食物，它们对你一定意义重大，不必交给我。
Charon: The offer is heard but refused. Such things have better use to you.

梅蕾尔：你不饿吗？
Merel: Seriously? Aren't you ever hungry?

卡戎：我一直很饿……但这是一种常态。
Charon: There is always hunger within me.

卡戎：食物应该被尽量地留给生者，它们对我的价值不如对你的多。你应当多吃些东西，好让自己活着。
Charon: But food should be saved for the living. Eat well while you can. Stay alive.

梅蕾尔：呃……话确实是这么说。但听着确实有些奇怪。
Merel: Well, you're not wrong, but I wouldn't exactly put it like that.

梅蕾尔：收下吧，“猎犬”总说我吃得已经够多了。
Merel: Come on, take it. Hound's always poking fun at me for eating too much anyway.

卡戎：“猎犬”？
Charon: "Hound"?

梅蕾尔：啊，别在意——你还是拿着吧，趁着现在能吃的东西还不是那么紧缺。
Merel: Oh, never mind. Just take it, alright? It's not like it's easy to get a decent meal out here on the front.

年轻士兵不再执着于征询对方的意见，她把罐头塞进了对方的大衣口袋里，同时摸到了巧克力冰凉的塑料包装。
No longer insisting on soliciting Charon's opinion, Merel slips the cans into his coat pocket while touching the cold plastic wrapping of the chocolates.

梅蕾尔：至少记得尝尝巧克力！天气再暖和一点它就该融了，在前线可没法洗衣服。
Merel: Oh! At least try the chocolate in your pocket! It'll melt if you leave it in there much longer anyway.

卡戎没有抗拒，他点点头，迟缓地站起身。
Charon doesn't resist. He nods and slowly rises to his feet.

卡戎：……我该走了。
Charon: It is time I left.

梅蕾尔：好吧，不过我还走不了。
Merel: Alright, I still have some finishing up to do here.

梅蕾尔：我得去盯着他们发放物资，长官们希望每个人都能领到。你要去哪儿？
Merel: Won't be long. Just have to make sure everyone's got their supplies. Where are you heading anyway? If you wait a moment, I can come with you.

卡戎：这次我打算独自前往。
Charon: No. This must be done alone.

卡戎：我还有……一封信要送。
Charon: There is a message, one that must be sent off.

11TH-15 回信 / Send-off

保罗：你果然在这里，艾伯哈特。
Paul: Here you are, Eberhard.

艾伯哈特：你来了，保罗。前线如何？
Eberhard: Paul, it's good to see you, my friend. How's everyone holding up on the front?

保罗：他们昨晚在办宴会，一切都很好。
Paul: They are celebrating this war's end, singing songs and drinking beer. It's peaceful.

艾伯哈特：一切都很好。
Eberhard: Hm. Peaceful.

他满意地重复着。相比上一次相见，艾伯哈特的精神已经发生了显著的改变。
He repeats the words with satisfaction. Eberhard's spirit has changed significantly from the last time they met.

保罗：我以为基金会不会允许你自由活动。
Paul: It's unexpected that the Foundation would allow you to move so freely.

艾伯哈特：不，我的使命已经完成了。蒙佩我已经待不下去了，里面全都是西装革履的大人物。
Eberhard: Heh. No, my duty is done. I have no place in Montpaix—no place among suits and politics.

他长舒一口气，在清晨的空气中伸展四肢。
He exhales, stretching in the crisp morning air.

艾伯哈特：那个红头发的官员同意我出来走走，他说，“会有人看着我”——管他呢。
Eberhard: That red-haired official agreed to let me go for a walk every once in a while. He said, "Someone will keep an eye on you." Hah, whatever.

艾伯哈特：天又变冷了……但我也很喜欢这样清冷的早晨。它让我想起过去读书的日子。
Eberhard: It's getting cold, but I enjoy a crisp winter morning like this. It reminds me of our days as students.

艾伯哈特：在冬天的时候，天还没亮时就要起床。不过通常我会等到你骑着自行车，在我家楼下喊人的时候才睁眼。
Eberhard: Remember? We had to get up before dawn. I was lazier than you. I wouldn't wake up until you rode your bicycle to my window and shouted my name.

保罗：这样我们两个都会错过拉丁文课。还有瓦尔特。
Paul: Then, the two of us would miss Latin class. Just as Walter did.

艾伯哈特：哈哈哈，就是这样。拉丁文才是真正的地狱呢。
Eberhard: Hahaha, I don't blame him. Latin class was hell.

艾伯哈特：瓦尔特……我真为他惋惜。
Eberhard: Walter. He was a good lad.

保罗从外套内取出一只揉皱的信封。
Paul removes a crumpled envelope from inside his jacket.

保罗：这是我从蒙佩替你取来的包裹，还没有来得及给你，里面只有这一封信件。是穆伦贝格先生写给三班学生的。
Paul: This parcel is to be delivered to you. There's a letter within it from Mr. Mühlenberge, addressed to those of us in Class 3.

艾伯哈特：穆伦贝格……在假期里我准备去亲自探望他，但在家乡发生的事情，你也已经知道了。我没有来得及见他。
Eberhard: Mr. Mühlenberge ... I was planning to visit him during my home leave, but, well, you know what happened back home.

艾伯哈特：他从来不知道前线发生了什么，打下蒙佩之后，三班的学生只剩下你和我了。他还在给谁写信呢？
Eberhard: But he doesn't have a clue about what happened out here. What use is this letter? You and I are the only two class members left since the fall of Montpaix.

艾伯哈特：打开它吧，保罗，你念给我听。
Eberhard: *sigh* Alright, let's hear it, Paul.

保罗深沉地换了一口气，随后撕开信封。
Steadying his breath, Paul tears it open.

他展开信纸。
He unfolds the letter.

保罗：“同学们，及战士们：战争正进行到最关键的时刻。作为你们的老师，我有义务为各位提振信心。”
Paul: "My dear students and honorable soldiers! The war has reached a critical point, and, as your teacher, it is my duty to boost your morale."

保罗：“虽然你们身在前线，但不一定能将眼下的局势把握准确。我要告诉你们的是——胜利就在眼前。”
Paul: "I am aware that the vision of the war from the front lines may be more limited than for those of us in the fatherland. So, allow me to make things clear: victory is within our grasp."

保罗：“前线的日子虽然艰苦，但要考虑到，你们正在为更加伟大的事业献身。那么苦难也应当是甘甜的。”
Paul: "Though I'm certain life on the front is tough, remember, this is a sacrifice for a greater cause. Therefore, let your suffering be sweet!"

保罗：……
Paul: ...

保罗：“……这将是你们一生中最光荣的时刻，如同我教育过你们的，在未来，这些痛苦会成为回忆中的欢乐。”
Paul: "... This will be the most glorious moment of your lives. And, as I have taught you, perhaps it will please us one day to remember these things."

艾伯哈特：欢乐？你听听这，他一定是在抄袭卢坎……还是维吉尔？我有印象。
Eberhard: "Please us"? Ha. Listen to him. He's even quoted Lucan's poem, or was it Virgil?

保罗：也许是维吉尔。他在后面还引用了一个短句，命运眷顾勇者[Audentis Fortuna iuvat]。
Paul: It is most likely Virgil. He has quoted him below, "Fortune favors the bold."

艾伯哈特：那关于欢乐的那一句……Forsan……Haec……后面是什么？也许是……
Eberhard: The quote about remembering things, how do you say it in Latin again? Forsan ... haec ... and then what? Hmm ...

保罗：你弄丢了一个词，艾伯哈特。
Paul: The "et" is missing, Eberhard.

保罗：也许有一天，回忆这些痛苦也是一种快乐[Forsan et haec olim meminisse iuvabit]。
Paul: "And perhaps it will please us one day to remember these things."

艾伯哈特：没错，就是这一句！这个老东西被我们逮住了，这根本不是他自己说的。
Eberhard: Yes, that's it! Hah. That old fart ... He cheated. These aren't even his words.

艾伯哈特：总之，他就是个没脑筋的老头，根本不明白自己在说什么。
Eberhard: What a fool. He doesn't know what he's talking about.

保罗：哈哈……
Paul: Heh ...

苦涩的笑声过后，二人都沉默了一会儿。
After a bitter laugh, both are silent for a moment.

艾伯哈特：……保罗，我不会因为回想这一天而快乐的。
Eberhard: Paul, I'll never be "pleased" looking back on any of this.

艾伯哈特：如果我有孩子，我要怎么告诉他我年轻时的故事？
Eberhard: If I have children one day, how will I tell them about all this?

艾伯哈特：我让自己的同胞冒着机枪和炮火冲上必死的阵地，而我明明知道，敌人在几小时后就能夺回来。
Eberhard: I sent our fellow countrymen directly into the line of fire—a death trap—knowing full well that the enemy would retake the ground in mere hours.

艾伯哈特：他们白白送死，而这一切只是为了完成一个不知所云的命令。
Eberhard: Young lives, lost one after another, and for what? Some senseless orders?

艾伯哈特：……我听够了，把信收起来吧。
Eberhard: I've heard enough. Put the letter away.

保罗缓缓将信折起。艾伯哈特却一把夺过信纸，揉成一团，扔到纪念碑旁的杂草中。
Paul slowly folds up the letter. Eberhard, however, snatches up the letterhead, crumples it into a ball, and throws it into the weeds beside the monument.

前线已经停火，不再有轰鸣声从遥远的地方翻滚而来。
There is no more fighting, and for the first time in a long time, the day passes without the thunder of artillery.

阳光落在草叶、墓碑与鸟羽上，人们可以静静观赏。
The sunlight falls on blades of grass, tombstones, and birds in the air. Their songs finally can be heard once more.

艾伯哈特：你能懂吗，我从来没有这么好过，好像在这一刻，我能——或者我已经掌握了自己的命运。
Eberhard: This feeling ... I've never felt it before. It's as though, for this one moment, I can—no, I have already taken control of my future.

艾伯哈特：活着的感觉如此美好，我的胸中也不再有沉重的东西。
Eberhard: Haheh. I'd forgotten how good it feels to be alive. Heh. For the first time in a very long while, my heart feels light, my friend.

艾伯哈特：我犯下的错误也许无法洗清，我已经决定我唯一能走的那条道路。
Eberhard: The choices I've made may be irreversible, but I've made up my mind. There is only one path for me now.

他望向山坡的顶端，情不自禁地向上迈步。
He looks to the top of the hill and starts climbing.

保罗：……你应该回去读书，学校花名册上还留着你的名字，课本与笔记也寄存在了学校的仓库中。
Paul: Do you not wish to continue your studies? Your writings are surely safely stored in the school's archives.

艾伯哈特：你还会回学校吗，保罗？
Eberhard: Would you return to school, Paul?

保罗：我也许不会，但你还可以继续学业。
Paul: It is unlikely, but you still may.

艾伯哈特：他们还会教给我们更多的知识，我们还要经历更多的考试……我还需要一份中学毕业证书吗？
Eberhard: For what? For knowledge? A diploma? That might've mattered to the old me.

艾伯哈特：可我感觉我已经成为了另外一个人。
Eberhard: But I'm no longer that boy.

保罗：艾伯哈特——
Paul: Eberhard—

艾伯哈特：不行的，保罗。现在已经太迟了。
Eberhard: It's too late, my friend. Far too late.

艾伯哈特：接下来我要一个人去散个步，请你给穆伦贝格先生写一封回信吧。
Eberhard: I need some time alone. Please write the reply to Mr. Mühlenberge for both of us.

今日有十足的好天气，艾伯哈特开始像郊游登山的学生那样攀上山坡。
The weather is unseasonably mild, and Eberhard begins to climb the hill like a student on a field trip.

难得的明媚阳光与恰到好处的清冷令人神清气爽。
The sunshine and brisk air make the world feel new.

艾伯哈特：天很蓝……战争结束了，保罗。
Eberhard: The war is over, Paul. The sky is so blue.

保罗：就像过去一样。
Paul: Just as it always was.

艾伯哈特：就像过去一样……这话真好。再见。
Eberhard: Just as it always was, hmm. Well said. Farewell, my friend!

他挥舞手臂，转身离去。
He waves, turns, and walks away.

保罗立在原地，将笔记本摊开。
Paul stands and opens his notebook.

保罗：“穆伦贝格先生：您寄来的信件已由您的学生签收。”
Paul: "Dear Mr. Mühlenberge, your letter has been well received by your students."

保罗：“他们共同度过了最黑暗与困苦的时光，曾在悲苦中相拥而泣。而现在一切业已结束。”
Paul: "They have endured the darkest and hardest of times together. But now, the sorrow and pain have reached their end."

保罗：“他们是勇敢的人，忠诚的人……但是，这些品质在某些时刻变得过于沉重，并非他们年轻的肩膀所能承载。”
Paul: "They showed courage and loyalty, yet these virtues became a burden—one far too heavy for their young shoulders to bear."

保罗：“故而我不愿意用这些词来为他们增添更多荣耀。”
Paul: "Therefore, I will not pile any more empty words upon them."

保罗：“战火让年轻人变成另一副模样，您教授他们的知识不再有用武之地，而他们也无法再度聆听您的教诲。”
Paul: "War has shaped these young men into something else entirely. The knowledge you imparted is of no use to them now, nor will they ever again hear your teachings."

保罗：“此刻，我不得不用最沉重的心情告诉您——”
Paul: "At this time, I must inform you with the heaviest of hearts that ..."

保罗：……
Paul: ...

保罗：“十三年级三班的学生已经全部阵亡。”
Paul: "All of your students from Class 3 have fallen."

保罗：“——谨致敬意。一个已死之人。”
Paul: "With best regards. A dead man."

“这是关于士兵保罗·霍伊默尔的记录。”
This concludes the records of the soldier Paul Haumann.

11TH-16 未完成的布道 / An Unfulfilled Prophecy

自从停火的消息传到教堂，拉蒂斯就一直缄口不语。
Ladislas hasn't spoken a word since news of the ceasefire reached their sanctuary.

拉蒂斯：……
Ladislas: ...

他长久地跪在祭坛前，已经有好几日没有吃正餐，原本已足够瘦削的他此刻似乎已经变成了一座嶙峋的塔楼。
He's been kneeling at the altar for days, having eaten next to nothing. Always thin, he now looks more like a jagged stone obelisk than a man.

石像鬼妇人：玛丽，这可如何是好？他连我亲手给他做的饼干都不吃了，他以前可不是这样的。
Female Gargoyle: What am I to do, my sweetie? He will not so much as touch the biscuits I baked for him. Never have I seen him in such a state.

妇人担忧地将手怀抱在胸前，对此现状无可奈何。
The woman clasps her hands to her chest, worried but helpless.

玛丽安娜：……拉蒂斯。
Sentinel: Ladislas.

她发出试探性的呼唤。
She gently calls out to him.

拉蒂斯：…………
Ladislas: ...

玛丽安娜：战争没有以他所预言的方式结束。
Sentinel: The war has ended not as he foretold.

玛丽安娜：他要从错误地解读了预兆的罪恶感中走出来，这需要一些时间。
Sentinel: It may take some time ere he is able to free himself of his guilt.

石像鬼妇人：拉蒂斯，主会包容我们的愚昧和罪恶，只要你的心是向着主的……唉。
Female Gargoyle: Dear Ladislas, *sigh* keep thy heart in the Lord, for He shall forgive us, no matter how great our missteps.

好心而虔诚的女人止住自己说更多话的欲望，她知道自己绝无可能通过宗教论理说服比自己学识更加渊博的拉蒂斯。
The good and pious woman stops herself from saying more. There's no line of reasoning sufficient to break him from his watch.

石像鬼妇人：玛丽，无论他是怎么想的，再过几天，我们一定要一起回鲁昂。
Female Gargoyle: Marie, I beg thee do something. One way or another, we all must return to Rouen in the coming days.

妇人珊珊离去。
She leaves without another word.

玛丽安娜来到拉蒂斯身边，但无心打扰拉蒂斯的默祷。她转向一直坐在角落中掩面哭泣的少女雕塑。
Sentinel comes to Ladislas's side but has no desire to interrupt his silent prayers. Her focus instead is on the statue of the crying girl.

玛丽安娜：拉蒂斯，你告诉过我，在战争结束的时候，艾格尼丝会恢复原样。
Sentinel: Ladislas, you foretold that Agnès would return to herself come the end of the war.

她拿出一块手帕，在“雕塑”上轻轻擦拭。
She pulls out a handkerchief to softly clean the stone's unmoving face.

玛丽安娜：可是现在呢？我们还有什么办法带回共同的朋友……和亲人？
Sentinel: Yet she remains unchanged. Is there truly no way to revive our dear friend? Our family?

拉蒂斯：………………
Ladislas: ...

回应她的仍然只有谦卑与愧疚的沉默。
Once again, she receives only a humbling, guilt-ridden silence.

玛尔纱：……玛丽？
Marsha: Marie?

转过头，玛丽安娜看见教堂这几日的常客。与往常一样，她照例带来了不少食物——这次是一些腊肠与干奶酪。
She turns to the voice, finding it belongs to the woman that has become a regular visitor to their sanctuary. As usual, she brought food—this time some salami and dried cheese.

玛尔纱将补给品交给其他人后，径直朝玛丽安娜走来。
After handing off the supplies, Marsha marches straight toward her.

玛丽安娜：前线有什么新消息？
Sentinel: What news from the front?

玛尔纱：一部分军队已经撤离前线，还有一部分会在停火协定正式签订之后撤退。
Marsha: Some troops have already withdrawn. The rest will follow suit once the armistice is officially signed.

玛尔纱：拉蒂斯……他还是不吃东西吗？
Marsha: Ladislas ... He still won't eat?

玛丽安娜：不用管他。
Sentinel: Just leave him be.

她已经不打算在这件事上纠缠，她继续刚才的工作——为掩面哭泣的少女雕塑擦去灰尘。
She doesn't let Marsha dwell on the matter, returning to her work dusting the statue.

玛尔纱：其实……我不知道这么问是否礼貌——这是一个……真正的雕塑吗？
Marsha: If you don't mind me asking, is this statue real?

玛丽安娜：真正的雕塑？
Sentinel: What do you mean?

玛尔纱：我、我不知道该怎么说……只是，我从来没见她活动过……
Marsha: I-I'm not sure how to put this into words properly. It's just that I've never seen her move.

玛丽安娜：我明白你的意思。
Sentinel: Ah, now your words are clear.

她收起手帕，深吸一口气，湿冷的晨雾灌入肺腔。
She gathers her handkerchief and takes a deep breath, the cold, wet morning mist filling her lungs.

玛丽安娜：她是艾格尼丝，我的远房表妹，我们有同一个曾祖母。
Sentinel: This is Agnès, a distant cousin of mine. We share a great-grandmother.

她把手放在艾格尼丝石质的膝盖上。
She places her hand on Agnès's stone knee.

玛丽安娜：1914年之前，我们一直生活在一起。有时在鲁昂郊区的家族庄园里，有时她会来巴黎的出租屋看望我。
Sentinel: We took residence together until 1914—both at our clan estate in the suburbs of Rouen and in my rented apartment in Paris.

玛丽安娜：战争开始之后不久，我加入军队离开家乡。在第一次回到家时，我发现她化成了一座雕塑。
Sentinel: When the war broke out, I departed to join the army. Upon returning during my first leave, I found her in the cellar—it came to pass that, in my absence, she had turned herself to stone.

玛尔纱：她……一直如此？
Marsha: She can stay in this form as she pleases?

玛丽安娜：你必须要让你的心脏保持跳动……如果你从内到外都成为了石头，就无法凭自己的力量恢复肉身了。
Sentinel: Only so long as her heart yet beats. Were she to turn to stone from within, she would be unable to restore her body to flesh.

玛丽安娜：但拉蒂斯告诉我另外的可能。
Sentinel: But Ladislas informed me of another possibility.

玛丽安娜：按照拉蒂斯的说法，艾格尼丝的石化并非出于平凡的理由，而是她选择了一条自我牺牲的道路。
Sentinel: He said Agnès's petrification was an extraordinary act of self-sacrifice.

玛丽安娜：同时这也是一份预言——石像鬼应该在这场战争中置身事外。
Sentinel: And that this sacrifice was also a prophecy: Gargoyles were not to coexist with this war.

玛丽安娜：也许战争结束的那一天，会有奇迹降临在艾格尼丝身上。
Sentinel: He said that a miracle would occur—that Agnès would be freed from her petrification. I thought it might have been true.

她看向跪在地上的拉蒂斯。
She glances toward Ladislas, still kneeling.

玛丽安娜：现在看来，他的预言是错的。艾格尼丝还是没能复原。
Sentinel: But I suppose it was not. Agnès has shown no signs of recovery.

玛尔纱：那有没有什么别的办法……
Marsha: There must be another way.

年轻的石像鬼懊丧地摇头。
The Gargoyle shakes her head, disheartened.

玛丽安娜：我也不清楚让艾格尼丝复原的方法……我对血脉的了解甚至不比一个外人多多少。
Sentinel: If only there were—if only I knew of one. But there is very little I know of our bloodline.

玛丽安娜：我的大多数同族都会在成年前接受族内的传统教育，但祖母支持我在很小的时候就去世俗学校读书的愿望。
Sentinel: While the young of my kin generally receive a traditional education from within the clan, my grandmother supported my decision to attend a secular school in my youth.

玛丽安娜：直到战争爆发前，我都住在巴黎租的小房间里，准备申请巴黎装饰艺术学院。
Sentinel: I resided in a small rented apartment in Paris for some time, hoping to enroll at l'ENSAD—that was, until the war broke out.

玛丽安娜勉强自己看向玛尔纱的眼睛。
Sentinel forces herself to look into Marsha's eyes.

玛丽安娜：之后就是战争……战争，你也清楚。过去的记忆，还有许多生命，随着炮火声一起消失。我失去了很多朋友和亲人。
Sentinel: This war ... Well, you've seen the face of it. It takes but one shot to end a life, and this war has hurt millions. Friends, family, loved ones ... I have lost far too many.

玛尔纱：玛丽……
Marsha: Marie ...

玛丽安娜：算了。你有时间吗？
Sentinel: Forget it. Tell me, have you yet time today?

玛尔纱：你想做什么？
Marsha: What do you want to do?

玛丽安娜：……出去走走。我在教堂待太久了。
Sentinel: Take a stroll. I have spent far too much time in the monastery.

历经跋涉，她们回到了那一片曾被杀戮所扰的原野。
After a long journey, they return to the field once soaked in blood.

玛丽安娜：飞行员？
Sentinel: A pilot?

路途中谈及的话题仍在继续。
Their earlier conversation still lingers.

玛尔纱：——是的，我曾经想过要当飞行员。
Marsha: Yes, that's what I wanted to be.

玛丽安娜：为什么？
Sentinel: Why?

玛尔纱：当时有很多骑兵都加入了空军，他们认为，只有天上还保留有最后一丝骑士精神。
Marsha: Many knights joined the air force at the time. They believed the sky to be the only battlefield that still maintained at least some semblance of knightly chivalry.

玛尔纱：至于地面的部队，唯一能做的就是在泥泞中爬行，或者挖战壕。
Marsha: It had more than the ground, at least, crawling through mud and digging trenches.

玛丽安娜：我不喜欢飞机。在地面的人拿它们没有任何办法，还有那些该死的引擎声……
Sentinel: I loathe airplanes. They're exceedingly difficult to withstand from the ground, and the engine noise.

她咽下更多的抱怨，以免显得太过难堪。
She swallows the complaints, not wanting to sound bitter.

骑士轻轻拍了拍石像鬼的后背。
Marsha extends her arm over to her friend's back.

玛尔纱：你不需要再担心了，也许……你会喜欢上坐飞机旅行。
Marsha: Relax, you don't need to fight them anymore. In fact, I'd wager you'll come to like traveling by plane in time.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

她把目光转向如浪涌般的草地。
She turns to the sea of grass rippling in the wind.

玛丽安娜：你看见那些人的尸体了吗？
Sentinel: The corpses that lay yonder—did you see them earlier?

玛尔纱：没有，也许卡戎已经收走了他们。
Marsha: No. Perhaps Charon had already buried them.

玛丽安娜：哈……有可能。他倒确实是个有意思的怪人。
Sentinel: Hah, most likely. He is an interesting fellow, if not strange.

玛尔纱：还是个好人——在公墓的时候，我们差点又要打起来。
Marsha: And kind, too. Without him, you and I would certainly have fought again at the graveyard.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

玛尔纱：我想起来了——
Marsha: Oh, that reminds me!

她忽然低下身子，在路边摸索着什么。
Suddenly, she bends down, rummaging in the roadside dirt.

玛丽安娜：什么？
Sentinel: What?

玛尔纱：你用烟雾弹呛过我！
Marsha: You threw a smoke grenade at me!

玛丽安娜：嘿！
Sentinel: Hey!

玛尔纱：哈哈哈——
Marsha: Hahaha!

骑士笑着在土路上奔跑，石像鬼一边大步追赶，一边用雨披擦去脸上的土灰。
They laugh as they race down the dirt road, feeling more like children than soldiers for the moment, however brief.

——她们停在风车前，巨大的齿轮系统啮合转动，仿佛一位年迈巨人的呼吸。
They come to a halt before the windmill, its colossal gears interlocking and turning, like the breath of a slumbering ancient giant.

眼前的一切沉静在奇异的宁静中。
The slow creaking of the windmill becomes the only sound.

玛丽安娜：……玛尔纱。
Sentinel: Marsha.

玛尔纱：嗯？
Marsha: Hm?

玛丽安娜：你是不是该走了？
Sentinel: Are you leaving?

玛尔纱：不，今天我有很多空闲的时间。
Marsha: No. I have plenty of free time today.

玛丽安娜：我是说之后……我知道在和约签订之前，基金会需要你留在这里看住我的动向。
Sentinel: Not now, after the armistice. I know well that the Foundation has tasked you with keeping a watchful eye on me.

玛尔纱：也不完全是这样……
Marsha: It's not exactly like that.

玛丽安娜：没事。你留下吧。只要你不对我撒谎。
Sentinel: All is well. You may stay, so long as you do not lie.

玛丽安娜：你有需要的地方，我可以帮忙，但不要劝我加入基金会。我不能丢下我的家人。
Sentinel: I shall even aid you should you require it. But do not attempt to persuade me to join the Foundation. I cannot abandon my family.

玛尔纱：我知道……正式停火之后，我也要离开了。
Marsha: I know that. I'll be leaving after the armistice is officially signed.

玛丽安娜：嗯……
Sentinel: *sigh*

玛丽安娜：……？
Sentinel: ...?

玛丽安娜：有人在风车里。
Sentinel: It comes from the windmill.

玛尔纱：——我听着更像是马的声音。
Marsha: Sounds like a horse to me.

玛丽安娜：马……？
Sentinel: A horse?

二人取下武器，小心翼翼地向风车的入口接近。
They cautiously approach the windmill's entrance.

玛丽安娜靠在玛尔纱之前，让一边的身体石化，侧着身子打开风车的塔门。
Sentinel moves ahead of Marsha, turning her body sideways, and hardens into stone to give a weighty push on the door.

战马：咴咴——！
War Horse: Neigh!

玛尔纱：哇——好漂亮的小马！
Marsha: Wow, what a beauty!

玛丽安娜：这真是……一匹马？
Sentinel: A horse indeed. What brings it here?

11TH-17 沉默的风轮 / Serenity on the Wind

战马：咴。
War Horse: Neigh.

玛尔纱：出来，到我这儿来，好孩子。
Marsha: Here, come on out. That's a good boy.

也许是马儿天然更亲近一名骑士，它耷拉着脑袋，向玛尔纱蹭了过去。
The horse seems to naturally gravitate to the knight, drooping its head to brush up against her.

战马：咴……咴咴——
War Horse: Neigh ...

玛尔纱：哈哈——
Marsha: Haha.

玛尔纱：天呐，玛丽，这真是一匹马。看看它的毛色！上校都不会有这么漂亮的伙伴。
Marsha: Oh my, Marie, look at his beautiful coat! Not even the colonels have such handsome companions.

玛丽安娜：它很亲近你嘛……你会骑马吗？
Sentinel: He seems to have taken a liking to you. Can you ride?

玛尔纱：看看你在问什么，玛丽安娜，我可是一名骑士。
Marsha: What sort of question is that, Marianne? You're talking to a knight.

即使没有马鞍，训练有素的骑士仍然飞快地攀上了马背。
Even without a saddle, she mounts the horse with ease.

玛尔纱：抓住我的手，上来——我带你骑一段！
Marsha: Come on, take my hand. I'll give you a ride.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

犹豫片刻后，她握住了骑士向她递来的手。
After a moment's hesitation, Sentinel takes the offered hand and finds herself on the horse's back as well.

玛尔纱：这片原野太适合骑马狂奔了，可是我担心你会颠下去。
Marsha: This field is perfect for a gallop, but I'm worried you might fall.

玛丽安娜：那你自己骑就好。
Sentinel: Let me off, then. Enjoy it yourself.

玛尔纱：不，那有什么意思呢？——但你还是得抓紧我。
Marsha: What fun would that be? Come on, just hold on tight.

玛尔纱：驾——
Marsha: Giddy up!

玛丽安娜：嘿！
Sentinel: Hey!

玛尔纱：哈哈哈哈——
Marsha: Hahahaha!

玛尔纱：玛丽，我没想到你不会骑马。但我可以教你如何与马匹相处——只需要把它们想象成特大号的猎犬。
Marsha: I can't believe you don't know how to ride a horse. But I can teach you. Just think of them as oversized hunting dogs.

玛尔纱：等你回家之后，我会来找你，如何？——那个时候你会在哪里？
Marsha: I'll come find you after you move. How does that sound? Where will you be if you're not staying with your family?

玛丽安娜：巴黎？——也许不会。我也搞不明白。但我会试着开一家服装店。
Sentinel: Perhaps Paris? My mind is yet made. But, wherever I am, I should like to open a clothing store.

玛尔纱：那你要取一个我一眼就能认出来的店名……不，你一定会成为特别出名的设计师，都不需要我刻意去找。
Marsha: Then you'd better choose a store name I'll recognize right away. No, you'll become so famous that it'll take no work to find you.

玛尔纱：你能给我做一套游行礼服吗？
Marsha: Could you make a parade dress for me?

玛丽安娜：我不明白这该怎么做，但我想……我可以学。
Sentinel: I have never before made such a dress, but, I shall learn for you.

玛尔纱：天呐，我会拥有一套法国设计师量身定做的游行礼服，简直就像是在做梦。
Marsha: Wow, a parade dress tailor-made for me by a famous French fashion designer. It's like a dream come true.

玛丽安娜：哈哈……
Sentinel: Heh ...

自从战争降临以来，从未有过如此安然的时光可供消磨。
This might be the first moment of true peace they've felt since the war began.

她们都骑累了，就放走了驯顺的马儿，任它在草地中寻觅嫩叶。
The horse grows tired. They dismount to let it roam and feed on the tall meadow grass.

玛丽安娜：可是，我要如何知道你的下落呢？之后基金会应该还会把你派到其他地方。
Sentinel: What of you? How may I come into your contact? The Lord only knows where the Foundation will send you once this is ended.

玛尔纱：没错，我们和重塑之手之间的冲突还没有结束。但我总能想办法联系到你的。
Marsha: You may be right. The fight against Manus Vindictae isn't over. But don't worry. I'll always find a way to get in touch with you.

玛丽安娜：我不想评价你的选择，但……尽量活下去，玛尔纱，不要太勇敢。
Sentinel: I do not wish to judge your decision, but do all you can to stay alive, Marsha. Do not make a martyr of yourself.

玛尔纱：为什么要说这么奇怪的话，玛丽？
Marsha: Why the sudden sentimentality, Marie?

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

玛丽安娜：假如这一切都有结束的时候，到那一天，我希望……还能再见到你。
Sentinel: If all this—when all this—comes to an end one day, I hope ... I hope to see you again.

玛尔纱：我也是。
Marsha: Me too.

玛丽安娜：……我会为你祈祷，虽然我不太确定我的声音是否能被听见。
Sentinel: I will pray for you, though I am uncertain if my voice will be heard.

玛丽安娜：我不像她——艾格尼丝。她是从天堂来到人间的天使，至于我……
Sentinel: I am nothing like Agnès. She is an angel descended from heaven. And I am ...

石像鬼将眼神掩藏在阴影中。
The Gargoyle keeps her eyes hidden in the shadow.

玛丽安娜：算了。
Sentinel: Never mind.

玛尔纱：……
Marsha: ...

“哔哔——”
*beep-beep*

战马：咴咴——
War Horse: Neigh!

玛尔纱：诶——？
Marsha: Hmm?

通讯器的噪音惊扰了安静的马匹，它倏然抬头，奔向远处。
The communicator's noise startles the nibbling horse. It lifts its head and bolts into the distance.

玛尔纱：啊……它逃走了。
Marsha: Ah, there he goes.

她拿起通讯器，再次看见了未署名的呼叫人。
She picks up the device. Again, it's an anonymous caller.

？？？：玛尔纱，尽快到前线待命，具体坐标我已经发送给你了。
???: Marsha, we need you on the front immediately. I've already sent you the coordinates.

？？？：如果石像鬼愿意跟你走，最好把她也一起带上。
???: Bring the Gargoyle if she's willing.

玛尔纱：你到底是谁？
Marsha: Who are you?

？？？：——我们很快就会见面。
???: We'll meet soon enough.

11TH-18 停火协定 / The Armistice

半小时前。
Half an hour earlier.

格奥尔格：是的，首相，代表团都已经抵达蒙佩……今天晚餐前就会签字。
Georg: Yes, Mr. Chancellor. The delegations have arrived in Montpaix. The armistice will be signed before dinnertime.

格奥尔格：明白，我们会办一个体面的晚宴……朴素至上，当然，准许进入会场的记者会经过筛选。
Georg: Understood. We will be sure to serve a simple but delicious dinner. And of course, all journalists granted entry will be carefully selected.

近期跻身内阁的格奥尔格先生干脆利落地挂断电话，他怀着充分的信心，再次检查了一遍停火备忘录。
Mr. Georg hangs up the phone dryly and with full confidence before checking the ceasefire memorandum once again.

格奥尔格：……不算太差。
Georg: Phew. No problems so far.

他拿起一支盟国外交官赠送的钢笔，在一张稿纸上绘下几个签名。
He picks up a fountain pen and sketches out his signature over and over again.

在停火协定上签字是他今天最重要的工作，必须勤加练习。
Each loop of the pen is taken with utmost seriousness—aware of the gravity it will soon hold.

又一道急躁的铃响，格奥尔格部长笔尖一滑，让字母“o”的形状变得相当不美观。
Another impatient ring, and the tip of his pen slips, leaving the letter "o" in a rather unsightly shape.

格奥尔格：啧啧——
Georg: *tut*

不过，这次响铃的是助理桌上的那一台。
But the call isn't on his phone. It's the one on his assistant's desk.

这意味着，对他来说这不是一件需要亲自处理的事情。
Which, thankfully, means it isn't his concern.

格奥尔格：弗雷德里希，你在做什么呢？快接电话。
Georg: What are you waiting for, Friedrich? Pick up the phone already.

部长助理：……
Assistant: ...

助理埋首在一大堆文件中，不慌不忙地书写着什么，没有对响铃做出任何反应。
The assistant, buried in paperwork, fails to react to the ring.

格奥尔格：你耳聋了吗，嗯？
Georg: Pick up the phone, you hear?

格奥尔格：噢——我真不明白为什么他们要安排一只鼹鼠来当我的助理，回国之后，我一定让你滚蛋。
Georg: Damn it. I still fail to understand why they would assign me a deaf sloth as an assistant. I'll have you fired the moment I set foot on the fatherland!

格奥尔格气势汹汹地冲向助理的桌面，想要给他一个教训。
Georg storms over to the assistant's desk to scold him.

后者倏然惊觉，立刻伸手拿起了听筒。
Jolting alert, the assistant grabs the receiver.

格奥尔格：——这还差不多。
Georg: That's more like it.

格奥尔格：……？
Georg: ...?

令他没想到的是，助理原封不动地将听筒放了回去。
To Georg's surprise, his assistant then immediately puts the receiver down.

部长助理：实在是有些吵，部长先生。
Assistant: That was an awful racket, sir.

格奥尔格：你这是什么态度？
Georg: H-How dare you?!

助理从容不迫地看了一眼手表。
The man checks his watch, paying no mind to his superior.

部长助理：我有更要紧的事情要做……不过，也该到时候了。
Assistant: I have more pressing matters to attend to. Yes, it's about time.

他站起身，拿起听筒，故技重施地将其挂断。
He stands up, picks up the receiver again, and hangs it up once more without a word.

格奥尔格：你需要对你的行为做出解释！
Georg: Wh-What? Explain yourself this instant!

格奥尔格：——？
Georg: ...?

部长助理：我不需要再对你做出任何解释，议员先生。
Assistant: Oh, I owe you no explanation, sir.

格奥尔格：谁？
Georg: Who could that be?

部长助理：进来吧。
Assistant: Come in.

格奥尔格：你——？！
Georg: You—?!

向299高地调查员发送的呼叫仍然没有收到回信。
All attempts to reach the investigators sent to Hill 299 have failed.

刻雷乌斯：……
Creius: ...

刻雷乌斯放下通讯器，片刻后，再次抬手，向“猎犬”发出同样的呼叫。
Creius puts his communicator down, pauses, then tries again—this time calling Hound.

听筒中传来的仍然是杂音。
But only static replies.

刻雷乌斯：同样失联了……
Creius: No response, either.

“Ⅻ”小队队长以略有不安的目光审视着从身边经过的政要。
Creius watches the passing politicians with growing unease.

谈判代表：……
Negotiation Representative: ...

结伴而行的代表们并不为刻雷乌斯的目光而侧目。他们保持着体面，把有限的时间投入到国家大事的商讨中。
They don't flinch under Creius's gaze. In fact, they don't seem to pay him any mind at all. Their limited time is devoted to the pressing matters of peace.

帕拉维扬从一幢房屋内走出，快步来到刻雷乌斯身前。
Paravyan exits a nearby building and makes his way to Creius.

“警官”：按照你的要求，新抵达的一批神秘术反制设备已经部署完毕，长官。
"Officer": Sir, a new batch of counter-arcanum devices has been deployed as instructed.

刻雷乌斯：嗯。最近三个小时，你和梅蕾尔有过联系吗？
Creius: Good. Any contact from Merel in the past three hours?

“警官”：没有，她应该还在前线，那边现在有很多小型宴会。
"Officer": No. She's probably still on the front. There's a lot of celebrating going on out there.

刻雷乌斯第三次拿起通讯器，开始呼叫小队内的另一名成员。
Creius tries the communicator once more, this time calling a different squad member.

“沙沙——”
*beep—buzz*

回应他的同样是沙哑的电噪音。
Static.

刻雷乌斯：……这不太对。
Creius: Something's not right.

接着，是第一声枪响。
A shot rings out like a thunderbolt on a cloudless day.

刻雷乌斯：——！
Creius: ...!

警卫士兵Ⅰ：有袭击——！
Security Guard I: We're under attack!

负责保卫代表团的警卫力量很快汇入街道。
Security forces rush into the streets, drawing any wandering delegates inside to safety.

可他们面面相觑，不知道敌人的子弹是从哪里射出来的。
Steel-eyed veterans fan out, searching for the gunfire's source.

警卫士兵Ⅱ：敌人在哪里？
Security Guard II: What's their location?

警卫士兵Ⅰ：我看见了！在那幢房子里，黑色的——
Security Guard I: I saw them! In that house! They're wearing black—

警卫士兵Ⅰ：呃啊——
Security Guard I: Ugrrrgh!

“警官”：他们——
"Officer": I have to—

青年差点就要冲上前去。
The young man begins a charge, only to be held back.

刻雷乌斯：帕拉维扬——回来，和我回指挥所去！通知所有基金会安保，返回预定战斗位置。
Creius: Get back here, Paravyan! We need to get to the command post and inform all security staff to resume combat positions.

“警官”：——是，长官！
"Officer": Yes, sir!

基金会安保向着防备最严格的主要建筑靠拢。
Foundation security regroups around the most heavily guarded buildings.

街道另一边，身穿漆黑军服的人从格奥尔格部长的办公楼中走出。
Across the street, a man in a jet-black uniform exits Georg's makeshift office.

重塑军官：呵……
Manus Officer: Heh ...

他从容不迫地走入开阔地带，浑身漆黑的士兵不断从他的身后涌现。
As he walks into the open, he is flanked by soldiers covered in pitch black.

重塑军官：……终于——这一刻终于到来。
Manus Officer: Finally! No more hiding. The moment of truth has arrived.

他举起一只手，环绕着他的士兵即刻停止行动。
He raises a hand, and the soldiers around him stand at attention.

重塑军官：留下几个基金会的人，我还有话要对这些道貌岸然的哈巴狗说。
Manus Officer: Leave a few of the Foundation lapdogs alive. I have something to say to those sanctimonious hypocrites.

重塑军官：其他人——全部杀光。
Manus Officer: As for the rest, kill them all.

停火协定的签字仪式以一场血腥的屠杀告终。
The ceasefire's signing descends into a bloody firefight.

重塑军官：认真搜索每一座房屋。
Manus Officer: Search every room! Leave no stone unturned!

每隔数十秒，就有某种绵软重物从高处坠落地面的沉闷声响。
Every few seconds, a heavy, soft thud echoes as something limp crashes to the ground from above.

仅有基金会安保据守的房屋内还有抵抗的力量——部署在掩体内的神秘术反制设备为他们提供了片刻喘息之机。
Foundation security offer what resistance they can, the counter-arcanum devices they've deployed providing them with a moment's respite.

重塑军官：——噢，对了，不要破坏他们签字用的桌子，那些文件也最好原封不动地放在那里。
Manus Officer: Oh, but keep that signing desk and the documents on it intact.

重塑军官：那会成为一个绝佳的新闻镜头，我要让它出现在所有报纸的头版。
Manus Officer: It'll make for a great headline shot—perfect for the front page of the papers.

重塑军官：另外，把她带出来吧。
Manus Officer: Now, bring her out.

重塑士兵：……
Manus Soldier: ...

重塑之手的士兵无声地履行命令。在激烈的交火之后，地上也躺满了穿着黑色制服的尸体。
The soldiers of Manus Vindictae carry out their orders in wordless lockstep. Soon bodies in white and black riddle the streets.

片刻后，两名士兵押着人质来到空旷街道的正中央。她清晰地暴露在基金会所占据房屋的视野中。
Moments later, two soldiers march a hostage into the center of the empty street.

基金会安保Ⅱ：唔……
Foundation Security Staff II: Ah ...

重塑军官：安静。
Manus Officer: Quiet.

再一次，军官抬起手，从容不迫地看了一眼手表。
Once again, the assassin-turned-officer raises his hand and checks his watch.

重塑军官：有点晚了……但也不赖。
Manus Officer: Better late than never.

他同样来到主干道上，向前迈着步子，犹如在参与一场盛大的凯旋游行。
He strides forward as if he were participating in a triumphal parade.

军官走到了距离基金会的指挥所只有十步之遥的地方，几乎能听见洁白的旗帜在风中颤抖的声音。
Stopping only a few short paces from the Foundation command post—so near that he can hear the flag fluttering in the wind.

重塑军官：找啊……找啊——看，现在你们终于找到我们了。
Manus Officer: All that endless searching. Heh. Well, here we are—you've finally "caught" us.

他摊开双手，仿佛在展示一件奖品。
He spreads his arm wide like a showman.

重塑军官：为什么事情竟做到了这个地步？为什么我们非要彼此互相杀害不可？
Manus Officer: You might ask, why must things end like this? Why must we kill one another?

重塑军官：因为——我们的哀求、我们的痛苦，统统都被你们无视！
Manus Officer: Do you want to know why? Because our pleas, our pain, our suffering, were all ignored by you!

重塑军官：人类制造了战争，将神秘学家推向战壕与弹坑之中，仿佛我们只是最廉价的消耗品。
Manus Officer: Humans started this war, all these wars, and yet you hurled us—arcanists—onto the front lines like cheap cannon fodder.

重塑军官：人类鄙夷我们的血脉，却又在战争中，命令我们用神秘术去对抗那些钢铁巨兽。
Manus Officer: You have created a world that despises us for our bloodlines and mocks us for our arcane skills, yet you force us to use those very skills to fight the war machines you built.

重塑军官：人类让我们付出惨重的代价，可在战争结束之后，连哪怕一片面包都不肯赏赐给我们。
Manus Officer: You humans have sown untold horrors in the name of conflicts created by your own hand, and still, you refuse us even a single scrap of bread in reward.

重塑军官：这是历史告诉我们的事。所以，我们要终结这对神秘学家来说不太友善的历史。
Manus Officer: These are the lessons history has taught us—a history of arcanist suffering that must end.

他从腰间取出手枪，放在双手中把玩。
He draws a pistol from his waist and toys with it.

重塑军官：所以，当我听到……神秘学家能够联合起来——不再是那种孱弱的抱团取暖的社区团体，而是像军人一样的联合。
Manus Officer: So when I heard that arcanists were uniting—marching under the banner of a formidable army—

重塑军官：……我看到了多少过去不曾有过的希望。
Manus Officer: I caught a glimpse of hope. In fact, it shone like never before.

重塑军官：基金会，人类的走狗——听好了！
Manus Officer: Foundation lapdogs, human scum, mark my words!

重塑军官：这场战争只是一个开始，从今往后，每一个时代人类的秩序与强权都将被颠覆。
Manus Officer: This war has only just begun. From this era onward, the unjust reign of humanity shall be overturned.

重塑军官：每一个于时代受苦的神秘学家，都会团结在重塑之手的旗帜之下。
Manus Officer: All arcanists from every era shall march under the banner of Manus Vindictae.

重塑军官：直到最美好的那个时代降临——！
Manus Officer: Until the ultimate, most glorious era arriv—

一颗子弹穿透军官的太阳穴。
A bullet rips through his temple.

重塑士兵：——！
Manus Soldier: ...!

残余的士兵也应声而倒。
The remaining soldiers drop where they stand.

基金会安保Ⅱ：……是谁？
Foundation Security Staff II: Who did that?

……
...

？？？：……我不喜欢这些和狗有关的低劣比喻，它们实在是太泛滥、太缺乏尊重了。
???: "Lapdogs," eh? Couldn't come up with anything more original?

游荡在外的“猎犬”终于归来。
The stray Hound at last returns.

他来到基金会指挥所的正门前，一脚踢开碍事的军官尸体。
He marches straight through to the command post, kicking the fallen Manus Vindictae officer's corpse for good measure.

“猎犬”：区域安全。
Hound: Command post's clear now.

防备森严的大门敞开，刻雷乌斯出现在他的视线中。
The door swings open, security staff cautiously scanning for trouble. Creius stands inside, waiting.

刻雷乌斯：……你来得有些迟了，叶尔莫莱。
Creius: You're late, Yermolai.

“猎犬”：起码你还活着，不错了。
Hound: At least you're not dead.

他四下环顾，目光与语调一样，总是带着一丝轻佻的讽刺。
Yermolai balks. His voice, like his face, carries a permanent smirk.

“猎犬”：不会永远有人替你擦屁股，刻雷乌斯。
Hound: You won't always have someone around to cover your ass, Creius.

如同之前的大多数对话那般，长官照例无视了下属的挖苦。
As always, Creius finds it easier to simply sidestep his insubordination.

刻雷乌斯：外面发生了什么？
Creius: What have you found?

“猎犬”：简而言之，我们晚了一步。重塑之手的确组建了一支属于自己的军队，不仅是这里，整个前线都有他们的人。
Hound: Long story short, we're a step behind the Manus. They've got an army, launching an assault on the front lines as we speak.

“猎犬”：我们面对的是至少一个旅级的作战单位，甚至也有可能是两个旅。他们藏在299高地下面，全部都是神秘学家。
Hound: We're talking about a force the size of a traditional brigade—possibly even two. They're hiding out beneath Hill 299, and every one of their soldiers is an arcanist.

刻雷乌斯：299高地……查尔斯和阿曼达情况如何？
Creius: Hill 299. Any news on Charles and Amanda?

行动队员收起了部分吊儿郎当的态度。
He lets the swagger drop from his voice.

“猎犬”：我找到他们的时候，两个人都死了。
Hound: Yeah. They're both dead.

“猎犬”：但他们还是想办法留下了关键的调查结果。
Hound: But they did leave behind some critical info.

“猎犬”：重塑之手几乎把299高地给掏了个空，他们在山体内挖掘了一座巨大而完备的地下堡垒设施。
Hound: Turns out Manus Vindictae's built a colossal, full-fledged underground fortress inside Hill 299.

“猎犬”：袭击安全区的人就是从299高地出发的，还有一部分重塑之手的部队正在向前线人类士兵发动攻击。
Hound: That's where all these Manus troops have been coming from—the ones here in the safe zone and the ones sent to eliminate the human soldiers at the front.

刻雷乌斯：是否执行了第二方案？
Creius: Did you carry out the other order?

“猎犬”：求援信息和应急预案已经发给总部，所有我能联系上的在外基金会人员都在向前线指定位置转移。
Hound: Yeah. I've sent the request for reinforcements and your "frontline contingency plan" to headquarters. All available Foundation personnel in the region are moving towards the designated locations on the front.

“猎犬”：不过，我没能联系上梅蕾尔。
Hound: All except Merel. I haven't been able to make contact with her.

刻雷乌斯：……
Creius: ...

长官点头，投出克制的认可。
Creius nods—an understated gesture of approval.

他对梅蕾尔的失联未作评价，似乎这已在他的预料之中。
He says nothing about Merel's radio silence, as if he had anticipated it all along.

“猎犬”：……所以，你真的打算这么做？所谓的“前线应急预案”？
Hound: You're really gonna do this, huh? This so-called "frontline contingency plan"?

刻雷乌斯：我们没多少选择。
Creius: I don't think we have much choice.

“猎犬”：那299高地怎么解决？——这不是预案中料想到的问题。
Hound: How're we gonna deal with Hill 299? It came out of nowhere.

刻雷乌斯：解决意外是执行计划的一部分。
Creius: Every plan has its surprises. We'll deal with it.

刻雷乌斯：……和我到前线去，在路上向我说明详细情况。
Creius: Follow me. We're going to the front lines. You can fill me in on the details on the way.

11TH-19 未至的终结 / A False Dawn

罗尔夫：那是什么？
Rudolph: What's that sound?

罗尔夫放下装满破旧衣物、纪念品与肉罐头的包裹，在胸前，还怀抱着这几年留下来的手稿与笔记。
Rudolph has set about packing his things. Like many in the trenches, he doesn't have much, but his greatest treasure is a pile of manuscripts and notes.

他仰起头，以费解的神色望向火炮声传来的方向。
He lifts his head. A pale look glints behind his glasses.

埃里希：你在这里站着干嘛，罗尔夫。
Erich: What are you standing there for?

罗尔夫：有人开炮……
Rudolph: They're firing again.

埃里希：难道你还没有听习惯吗？
Erich: So? Surely you're used to it by now.

对长期生存在前线的士兵来说，火炮声已经成为一种几近无害的噪音，他们已经能就着这种声音安然入眠。
The rumble of artillery had become so familiar to them that its return is barely noticed.

罗尔夫：可是……不是要停火了吗？就算没有到正式的停火时间，但是……再开炮也没有意义了。
Rudolph: But, isn't there supposed to be a ceasefire? I know it isn't official yet, but there's no point in firing now, is there?

埃里希：嘶——
Erich: Ah!

埃里希倒抽一口气。
Erich draws in a sharp breath.

随之而来的是一声低沉的呼啸。
A low, ominous whistle follows.

埃里希：操！——躲掩体里去！
Erich: S**t! Take cover!

宁静的前线被重新点燃。
All at once, the quiet of the front erupts into fire and fury.

罗尔夫：唔——咳咳——
Rudolph: Ugh ... *cough*

饱受摧残的土地在爆炸的冲击中摇晃，堑壕化为一艘随时将在海浪中倾覆的脆弱航船。
The impact of the explosions shakes the trench lines in unyielding waves, the blasts spraying mud and earth in every direction.

埃里希：他妈的，都疯了？！那帮老东西不是正在谈判吗？
Erich: Damn it! Has everyone gone mad?! Those old farts! I thought they were supposed to be negotiating peace?

罗尔夫：为、为什么——又……又开战了？
Rudolph: Why? Why are we fighting again?

趴在地上的罗尔夫四肢并用，想要抢救被一阵气浪掀飞的行李。
Rudolph sprawls out on the ground, trying to find his baggage, which has been scattered in the blast.

衣服、笔记与罐头……将要带回家乡的一切，化作碎片飞溅而起。
Clothes, notes, and cans are buried in loose dirt or carried off in the air.

罗尔夫：不——
Rudolph: No!

埃里希：别管那些没用的玩意儿了，躲进来！
Erich: Forget that rubbish! Get inside!

埃里希将瘦小的罗尔夫塞进地下掩体内，随后抄起一把潜望镜贴在战壕一侧向外观察。
Erich forces the bespectacled soldier into a dugout, then forces himself up to the parapet, peering over with his periscope.

埃里希：这他妈的……到底是什么人打过来了？
Erich: St! St! Who in the hell is attacking us?

罗尔夫：他们的衣服……不是蓝色，全都是黑色。
Rudolph: I-I don't know. They're not even wearing blue. They're in all black.

埃里希：见鬼的，他们脸上的面具又是怎么回事？他们能看清东西吗？
Erich: Right. Are they wearing masks? Can they even see through them?

观察员：侧翼——
Spotter: *pant* The flank! *pant*

观察员从通向右翼的交通壕中冲出来，不断向各个战壕传递最新的情况。
Scouts and messengers dash in every direction, alerting everyone they can reach of the attack.

观察员：这些人是从侧翼高地冲过来的，不知道是什么鬼东西——
Spotter: I don't know who or what they are, *pant* but they're coming from our flank! *pant*

埃里希：靠！
Erich: Damn it all to hell!

一颗流弹打碎了镜筒，埃里希咒骂着将破损的潜望镜扔到脚边。
A stray bullet shatters his periscope. He tosses the device down with a stream of curses.

他一把抓住路过的观察员。
He grabs a messenger by the collar.

埃里希：把2连的人找来——朝那些黑衣服的东西开火！
Erich: All men from the 2nd Company, assemble! Focus fire on enemies in black uniforms!

进攻暂时停歇了。
Their first assault breaks against the renewed defenses.

大多数身穿黑色制服的士兵将尸体留在了无人区。
But the black-clad soldiers seem numb to their losses; they advance in rigid order, stepping over the dead and dying.

埃里希：这些人都丧失神智了？……一个劲儿地往枪口上撞。
Erich: Have they lost their minds? They just keep charging right into our gunfire.

转过身，谨慎而迅速地越过身旁受伤的战友，在更远处，他能听见受伤士兵们哀嚎的声音。
Erich steps down from the parapet to relay orders; in every direction he sees his comrades lying wounded.

他们都没有想到还要再经受如昨日般炮火的折磨。而这一次，他们仍然不理解战争的含义。
Only yesterday they had begun to believe their fight was over, but the rattling barrage has shattered their dreams—a new war has begun.

埃里希：……天呐，这到底发生了什么？
Erich: Damn it. What the hell is going on?

他在昏暗的壕沟中寻找罗尔夫的下落，却猛然撞上一道高大而醒目的白色身影。
Rudolph hasn't reported back. Concerned, Erich begins to search the dim trenches for his friend, only to bump into a striking figure in a white uniform.

刻雷乌斯：你是2连的连长，对吗？
Creius: Are you the captain of the 2nd Company?

男子提问时不失长官的威严，埃里希一时之间有些不知如何应对。
The man speaks with a gravity of command that Erich still has yet to find.

埃里希：我是。你是……基金会的？
Erich: I am. You're ... with the Foundation?

红发男子点点头，有条不紊地阐明眼下的战况。
Creius nods, articulating the battle at hand in an organized manner.

刻雷乌斯：我是基金会在蒙佩的指挥官，刻雷乌斯，目前我们都遭遇了紧急情况。
Creius: I am Creius, the commander of the Foundation personnel stationed in Montpaix. This is an emergency situation.

刻雷乌斯：重塑之手的军队袭击了安全区，还准备将前线的人类军队一同剿灭。
Creius: Manus Vindictae invaded the safe zone. We neutralized the threat there, but now they're on a mission to kill every human soldier on the front lines.

埃里希：……人类？包括对面的……我们全部人？
Erich: Every human soldier? You-You mean, including those on the other side?

他一时之间有些不明白自己听到了什么。
He struggles to find sense in the words.

刻雷乌斯拍了拍连长的肩膀。
Creius pats the soldier-turned-captain with a firm and steady grip.

刻雷乌斯：如果你们愿意放弃这片阵地的话，可以跟我走。
Creius: If you're willing to give up this position, follow me.

埃里希：我不在乎这该死的阵地，只不过……你想带我们去哪儿？
Erich: I couldn't give less of a damn about positions, but where are we going?

相距不远的另一段战壕。
In a nearby section of trench.

玛尔纱：还有能动的人吗？——来搭把手，我们把这块掩体清理出来。
Marsha: Anyone still standing? Help me clear this bunker!

战地医生几乎是与基金会的队伍一同抵达战壕的。
The field medic arrives in sync with the rest of the Foundation's team.

士兵：医生——医生！有伤兵，快救救他！
Soldier: Doctor! Doctor! My brother—he's wounded! Please!

玛尔纱：医生在这儿——把人送过来！
Marsha: Bring him to me!

士兵拖着受伤的战友来到充做临时急救点的掩体旁。他身下的伤兵拖着一条失去知觉、浸满暗红血液的大腿。
The soldier hauls his wounded comrade to the makeshift aid station. The man's leg hangs limp, soaked in dark red blood.

罗尔夫：……呃——
Rudolph: Urgh ...

玛尔纱：把他放下，好，不要动了——另外，你看到基金会的其他人了吗？
Marsha: Easy. Put him down here. I'll patch him up. Have you seen any other Foundation personnel?

士兵：看、看到过一个红头发的。
Soldier: I-I think I saw one—a redhead.

玛尔纱：好，告诉他让人把急救品都拉到这儿来。他们应该从蒙佩带了不少东西过来。
Marsha: Good. Go tell him we need medical supplies. They should've brought plenty from Montpaix.

士兵：这、这就去！
Soldier: R-Right away!

在他身旁，受伤的士兵正捂着大腿，喘出沉重的呼吸。
Next to them, another soldier clutches his thigh, gasping for breath.

恰在此时，又有一位伤兵被放在临时急救点。玛尔纱略作检查，又回到了大腿受伤的士兵身边。
Only a moment passes before yet another man is carried in. Marsha makes a brief inspection and returns to the soldier with the injured thigh.

玛尔纱：我先给你止血。
Marsha: I'll stop the bleeding first.

罗尔夫：他、他怎么了？
Rudolph: W-What about him?

玛尔纱：他死了。松手，忍住——
Marsha: He's dead. Now relax, and try to stay with me.

罗尔夫：他死——不——
Rudolph: He's dead? No!

罗尔夫：啊啊啊啊——
Rudolph: Ahhhhh!

罗尔夫：我的老天，我要死了，我就要死了——
Rudolph: Good heavens! It's over. I'm dead. I'm dead.

罗尔夫：呃……呃啊……！
Rudolph: Urgh ...

玛尔纱：好，你这会儿死不了了。
Marsha: No, you're not. Not today, anyway.

罗尔夫：呼……呼——
Rudolph: Huff ...

他的视线逐渐模糊，几乎出现了幻觉——他竟然看见一名身穿灰蓝制服的士兵，和自己出现在同一条战壕中。
His vision blurs—for a moment he thinks he sees a soldier in a gray and blue uniform.

罗尔夫：这、这是……
Rudolph: Is-Is that ...?

他昏了过去。
Then he blacks out.

玛丽安娜：怎样，找到刻雷乌斯了吗？
Sentinel: Update? Have you located Creius?

玛尔纱：他已经到战壕了，应该就在不远的地方。
Marsha: He's somewhere in the trench. A soldier spotted him.

男人很快出现在她们面前。
The man soon appears before them.

他以带有敬重的审慎姿态向曾追查过的狙击手点头致意。
With solemn deference, he nods to the sniper he once pursued.

刻雷乌斯：没想到会在这里见——
Creius: I didn't expect to run into—

玛丽安娜：别废话。
Sentinel: Save the pleasantries.

她直截了当地打断对方的客套话。
The response is blunt.

玛丽安娜：情况我听玛尔纱说了。基金会把我叫来，最好是已经有了打算。
Sentinel: Marsha made known to me the situation. The Foundation ought to have a sure plan, having requested me to join her.

玛丽安娜：告诉我，你想让我干什么？
Sentinel: Speak then, what would you have me do?

行动队长很快调整了语气。
Creius adjusts his tone to match.

刻雷乌斯：留在前线的士兵缺乏应对神秘术的武器和训练，无法与重塑之手的部队作战。
Creius: The frontline soldiers have little experience fighting enemies with arcane skills.

刻雷乌斯：我打算把他们带去更安全的战略位置，以免这些毫无准备的人被重塑之手全部歼灭。
Creius: If they stay here, it's only a matter of time until they fall to the Manus. I'm going to move them to a safer strategic position.

刻雷乌斯：但是，299高地把至少8个师钉死在战壕里。重塑之手在山体内修建了地下堡垒，差不多有一万人藏在里面，另外——
Creius: However, enemy forces on Hill 299 have us pinned down in the trenches. Manus Vindictae has turned it into an underground fortress, housing an estimated ten thousand troops. They've even—

刻雷乌斯：——另外还有隐藏在混凝土工事下的火炮阵地。士兵们不能顶着炮火撤退。
Creius: They've even positioned artillery on the hillside. Retreating under that kind of fire would be a death sentence.

玛丽安娜：消除来自高地的威胁，然后把前线的部队撤走，这就是基金会的计划？
Sentinel: Eliminate the threat from Hill 299, then withdraw the troops from the front—this is the Foundation's plan?

刻雷乌斯：不，至少现在还不是。
Creius: Not the Foundation's plan. Not yet, at least.

男人热切的眼神中忽然凝出冰冷的克制。
An icy restraint condenses in the man's eager eyes.

刻雷乌斯：这是我的决定。
Creius: This is my course of action.

玛丽安娜：那你打算怎么摧毁地下堡垒？——就算你能让十万人去送死，也不一定能拿下一座设防的高地。
Sentinel: How do you intend to do this? Even with an army of a hundred thousand at your command, to take a fortified high ground under artillery fire is no surety.

刻雷乌斯：我明白，所以我只能请求你的帮助。
Creius: I know. That's why I need your help.

刻雷乌斯的态度近乎肃穆，他知道自己的请求有多么荒诞。
Creius stands solemn and sure, though he knows how absurd his request sounds.

玛丽安娜：我看不出这项自杀行动有多大的收益。
Sentinel: Such an act is to walk into the valley of the shadow of death. What difference would be made if I lent my aid or withheld it?

刻雷乌斯：如果我没记错的话，石像鬼不容易受到毒气的伤害。
Creius: If I recall correctly, Gargoyles are insusceptible to poison gas.

玛丽安娜：确有此事，你想表达什么？
Sentinel: That's correct. So?

刻雷乌斯：这样的话，我们有其他更安全、代价更小的方式摧毁地堡。请跟我来，我的部下会为你做详细的解释。
Creius: So, we may be able to take a subtler approach. Please, come with me; my subordinate will give you the details.

11TH-20 地狱之门 / Gates of Hell

他们在泥泞中飞速穿梭。
They race through the mud and debris.

玛丽安娜：……还有多远？
Sentinel: How much longer?

“猎犬”：保持速度，十分钟。
Hound: About ten more minutes at this pace.

“猎犬”：如果没有人阻拦，也许不用十分钟。
Hound: Maybe less if there are no interruptions.

玛丽安娜：你很乐观。
Sentinel: Hmph. What an optimist.

“猎犬”：……
Hound: ...

他们不再说话，继续向前。
There isn't anything more to say. They just keep moving.

腐烂与衰败的一切在不断后退。
Until they leave the trench behind.

……
...

玛丽安娜：隐蔽。
Sentinel: Take cover.

他们躲进一处弹坑，一颗子弹落在他们眼前，溅起不少泥点。
They dive into a shell crater. A bullet skips off the lip of earth in front of them, kicking up wet clods of dirt.

玛丽安娜：你来压制他。
Sentinel: Pin them down.

“喀锵——”
*clang*

一颗滚烫的弹壳从机匣中蹦出。
A searing-hot shell casing ejects from the chamber.

玛丽安娜：……解决了。
Sentinel: Threat neutralized.

“猎犬”：枪法不错……事实上，我们到了。
Hound: Nice shot. Right, we've arrived.

叶尔莫莱走向一侧，翻下一截被废弃的战壕。
Yermolai veers off to the side and drops into a stretch of abandoned trench.

石像鬼尾随其后。
Sentinel follows close behind.

他们站在一处紧闭的地下掩体门前。
They stand before a sealed underground bunker.

叶尔莫莱站在距离掩体入口较远的位置上，从外套中取出一捆炸药与一张潦草的地图。
Yermolai stops a short distance from the entrance, pulling from his coat a bundle of explosives and a hastily drawn map.

“猎犬”：拿着它。
Hound: Take these.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

她不发一言地取走“自杀行动”的关键物品。
Without a word, she takes the key items for this suicide mission.

“猎犬”：我很惊讶——你愿意帮这样的忙。
Hound: I'm surprised you'd agree to this.

玛丽安娜：我不会解释我的理由。
Sentinel: I have my reasons.

“猎犬”：那么，再重复一遍计划。
Hound: Sure. Let's go over the plan one more time.

“猎犬”：两位基金会调查员发现299高地堡垒与很多地下通道相连，我们眼下的这条直通重塑之手的弹药库。
Hound: Two of our investigators discovered a number of tunnels running under Hill 299. The one we've just arrived at leads directly to the Manus's ammunition depot.

“猎犬”：开战之后，重塑之手用毒气封锁了所有地下通道，从我找到的尸体判断，这些毒气能穿透现有的防毒面具。
Hound: After the war broke out, the Manus sealed all accessible tunnels with poison gas. Judging by the bodies I found earlier, this gas can penetrate all existing gas masks.

“猎犬”：好处是，因为这些毒气的存在，通道中或许没有多少重塑之手的守军。
Hound: On the bright side, that means there aren't many guards in the tunnels—at least, that's what we think.

“猎犬”：抵达弹药库，引爆炸药，摧毁地堡。然后，基金会将带着士兵撤离。这就是全部的计划。
Hound: Your goal is simple: reach the ammunition depot, detonate the explosives, and destroy the fortress. After that, the Foundation will evacuate with the soldiers.

玛丽安娜：……至少基金会的调查不是一无所获。
Sentinel: Good to know the Foundation's investigation bore some fruit.

“猎犬”：299高地实在是太显眼，以至于容易忽视。
Hound: Hill 299 is so conspicuous that everyone just unconsciously overlooked it.

玛丽安娜：够了。你回去吧。
Sentinel: I'm prepared. You may leave now.

“猎犬”：那么，祝你好运。
Hound: Alright. Good luck.

男人挥手告别。
The man offers a wave.

等到叶尔莫莱离去的声音完全消失之后，玛丽安娜才拉开地下掩体的大门。
Only once Yermolai's footsteps have faded into the distance does Sentinel open the bunker door.

紫红色的毒雾翻涌而出。
Violet-red mist billows out.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

她紧皱着眉，轻嗅一口。
She furrows her brow and takes a cautious sniff.

所幸，和以往一样，她未能感到任何不适。
Thankfully, as before, it has no effect on her.

玛丽安娜听见掩体内传来拖行声，她警觉地守在门边，随后，一道阴影沉默地出现在视野中。
Yet from within, she can hear something dragging. Sentinel holds position at the door, waiting as a shadow shuffles into view.

卡戎：……
Charon: ...

亡者从毒雾中缓缓走出。
A grim figure emerges from the toxic mist.

玛丽安娜：——你怎么在这里？
Sentinel: What are you doing here?

卡戎沉默地将一具尸体拖出掩体，在门外暂时停驻。
Charon drags a corpse out of the shelter and halts outside.

卡戎：一场战争结束，又一场战争爆发……更多人将死于同类之手。
Charon: One war ends, and another begins. More lives will be claimed by their own kind.

卡戎：我仍然做着和以前一样的事。
Charon: I am simply doing what I always do.

玛丽安娜：你早就知道这条路？
Sentinel: You knew of this tunnel?

卡戎：这条……路？我不知道它通向哪里。我看见死亡的阴云笼罩在这片土地上，所以我来到了这里。
Charon: Tunnel? I know nothing of it. The cloud of death hanging above this place—that is what led me here.

亡者不会撒谎。
She knows better than to suspect him.

玛丽安娜：阴云？
Sentinel: Cloud of death?

卡戎：一种模糊的征兆。
Charon: An ambiguous omen.

玛丽安娜：……征兆。那你能否告诉我，这份死亡属于谁？
Sentinel: An omen, hmm. Tell me then, who will this cloud of death fall upon?

卡戎：死亡是平等的，我无法区分不同人的死亡。
Charon: Death is impartial. It doesn't decide who will live and who will die.

玛丽安娜：但我可以。
Sentinel: But I can.

她无所顾忌地在毒雾中深呼吸一口气。
She breathes in the toxic air without concern.

玛丽安娜：我劝你尽快离开这里。如果死的不是我，那么299高地会有一场爆炸。
Sentinel: I suggest you leave. Should this cloud not fall upon me, an explosion will soon obliterate Hill 299.

卡戎：你要杀死高地上重塑之手的驻军吗？
Charon: Do you intend to claim the lives of all the Manus Vindictae troops here?

玛丽安娜：……你想阻止我？
Sentinel: Do you intend to stop me?

卡戎：……
Charon: ...

亡魂无法用言语来回应，他只是静默地沉思着。
He broods for a moment, as a silent war is waged behind his mask.

玛丽安娜：……我该走了，时间不多。
Sentinel: I should leave. Time is pressing.

在她转身的那一刻，卡戎的声音再度在身后响起，他刚刚似乎只是在思索如何回答。
But as she turns, Charon's voice breaks through with sudden clarity.

卡戎：我不希望看见这样的杀戮，但也没有能力阻止。
Charon: I do not wish for such carnage to occur, yet I am powerless to prevent it.

卡戎：不过，在你离开之前，我想要提醒你……
Charon: But before you go, a word of warning ...

卡戎：……你的战争事实上已经结束，你将走向的是另一场争端，另一条更加残酷的道路。
Charon: The war you've been fighting is, in fact, over. What lies before you is a conflict all its own—a much harsher path.

卡戎：你可以转身离去，用一些时间卸下迄今为止积累的负担。
Charon: You still have a chance to turn away from this and relieve yourself of the burdens placed upon you.

玛丽安娜：比起战争中的人们遭受的苦难，我所负担的重量不值一提。
Sentinel: In view of the sufferers of this war, my burden is light.

玛丽安娜：……而我也不会在我选择的道路上迷失。
Sentinel: Harsh or not, I shall not waver from the path I have chosen.

卡戎：你在五年前踏上了战场，这一天与过往的那一日又有什么不同？
Charon: You first set foot on the battlefield five years ago. What makes today different from that day?

玛丽安娜：我知道战争因何而起，也看清楚了敌人的样貌。
Sentinel: I now know the true cause of the conflict, and I have seen the face of the true enemy.

玛丽安娜：……我知道罪恶的道路能完成我的牺牲。
Sentinel: If I must sin to fulfill my sacrifice, then so be it.

卡戎：我不能理解牺牲，以及你执意受苦的意志……但是，作为不凡的生者，你也许拥有不凡的智慧。
Charon: Your willingness to suffer, your passion for sacrifice ... it is beyond me. Perhaps you possess a wisdom beyond my comprehension.

卡戎：而我……只是为你感到悲哀。
Charon: Yet, still, I feel a deep sadness for you.

卡戎：我没有资格阻拦你前进……此处即是地狱之门。
Charon: I am in no position to stop you from walking through the gates of hell.

11TH-21 一小时的政治 / 1-Hour Politics

地下深处，黑暗统治着一切。
Deep underground, darkness reigns.

起初，她在逼仄无光的泥土甬道中穿行，直到跨过一道水泥浇筑的门框。
At first, she travels through cramped, unlit dirt tunnels until she reaches a poured concrete doorframe.

一阵冰冷的回声激荡着，她意识到此刻所处的是一处较为开阔的空间。
Its cold echo tells her she's entered a wider space.

玛丽安娜：行于黑暗之人得见光亮，死荫之地亦有光明照耀。
Sentinel: The people that walked in darkness have seen a great light: they that dwell in the land of the shadow of death, upon them hath the light shined.

她以血脉赐予的力量窥破黑暗，却也因此被迫见证黑暗中所有的秘密与污秽。
She taps into the power of her ancient bloodline, her eyes adjusting rapidly to the pitch black. Yet she finds no comfort in seeing what surrounds her.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

暗沉而黏腻的物质在甬道的壁上流淌，仿佛某种不定形的生物在蠕动。
Dark and viscous substances flow through the walls of the tunnel, like an endless mass of writhing insects.

它们恍惚间构成某种难以辨认的符号，转瞬间又化作混乱不堪的图形。
In their trance, they form some kind of unrecognizable symbols, shifting back and forth into chaotic shapes.

玛丽安娜：亵渎。
Sentinel: Blasphemy.

眼前的一切不足以令她止步——她早已见过更险恶的深渊。
But she has seen far more sinister abysses in her time.

玛丽安娜：高地据点的核心区应该在更靠近山顶的位置。但……这条路似乎是在向下延伸。
Sentinel: The fortress's center ought to be closer to the peak, but this path appears to be extending downward.

她展开叶尔莫莱交给她的地图资料。
She unrolls the map and reads the included intel.

玛丽安娜：不过根据基金会提供的地图，路线并没有出错。
Sentinel: The Foundation's map says this is the route.

暗紫色的气体因闯入者的动作而翻滚着，刺激性的气味持续侵入她的鼻腔。
Plumes of gas tumble with the intruder's movements, stinging her nostrils.

玛丽安娜：不像发霉的干草味，也不是大蒜和芥末的味道。新的毒气。
Sentinel: Not the stench of rotting hay, not garlic or onion, either. This is a new kind of poison gas.

玛丽安娜：不过，对我也没有效用。
Sentinel: Still, it has no effect on me.

你在哪里？
Where art thou?

空灵的呼唤声悠然落下。
An ethereal voice drifts down.

玛丽安娜：——艾格尼丝。
Sentinel: Agnès.

玛丽，你听得到吗？——我听不见你的声音。
Dost thou hear me, Marie? I heareth naught from thee.

玛丽安娜：你……听不见？
Sentinel: You hear me not?

她仰起头，只看见向下压迫着的沉重穹顶。
She looks up, seeing nothing but the vaulted ceiling.

艾格尼丝的声音溶解在致死的毒雾中，在耳旁如同蜂鸣。
Agnès's voice is like a biting acid in her ears.

你到哪里去了，玛丽？你在很深很深的地方，被我所不能看清的东西包围。
Where hast thou gone, Marie? I sense thou art somewhere deep below the earth, surrounded by that which I cannot clearly see.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

玛丽安娜：地上有很多尸体，艾格尼丝，他们倒在金属残骸与水泥块之间。
Sentinel: Bodies lay scattered around me, Agnès. Many of them.

玛丽安娜：杀死他们的是毒气，也许在一小时前，他们正准备逃离这座坑洞。
Sentinel: They're Manus soldiers. It appears they attempted to flee through this tunnel but an hour ago.

她越过一道残骸。
She steps over debris.

玛丽安娜：可他们都是重塑之手的士兵……他们的长官为了堵住道路，释放了可以杀死自己人的毒气。
Sentinel: Their superior blocked their way and loosed upon them this poison gas, killing his own men.

她跨过一双圆睁的眼。
Bodies stare up at her from unblinking eyes.

玛丽安娜：我在面对的究竟是怎样的敌人，艾格尼丝？
Sentinel: What kind of enemy am I soon to face, Agnès?

……你害怕吗？
Art thou afraid?

玛丽安娜：——
Sentinel: ...

你一定对我说了很多话，玛丽。我没有离开，我在等你说完。
Thou must have spoken much, Marie. I shall not leave thee. I am listening.

只是……我仍然听不见你的声音。
Only I yet hear not thy voice.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

我记得我们一起躲在庄园的地下墓穴，你告诉我你才不会害怕奶奶说过的鬼怪故事。
Dost thou recall the day we hid together in the catacombs of the manor? Thou said unto me thou feared not the ghostly tales thy grandmother once spake.

你说，你是比它们更可怕的魔鬼。但那天夜里，我注意到你的呼吸，在颤抖。
Thou saidst thou bore a devil more terrifying than any tale. But on that night, thy breath did tremble—thou wert afraid.

她停在继续向下的阶梯入口。
She halts at the descending stairway.

玛丽安娜：不是这样的，艾格尼丝。
Sentinel: That was not the thing of which I was afraid, Agnès.

又一次，她意识到头顶厚重的岩层隔断了她想传递的话语。
Once again, she realizes her words cannot reach beyond the heavy rock above.

在黢黑深邃的另一端，仿佛有什么东西正在等待。它伸出黑色的尖爪。
From the depths of that pitch-black void, something waits, stretching out sharp, black claws.

我在害怕，玛丽，你面前的道路已经没有亮光，你离我越来越远。
I worry for thee, Marie. The path that thou dost walk holdeth no light. I can feel thee growing ever more distant from me.

有时我不懂你要做什么，但我会相信你。只是，记得回来好吗？
Whatsoever it is—whatever thou dost wish to do, I know thou art determined to see it to its end. But I pray thee, make haste and come unto us soon, wilt thou?

……我将为你的灵魂祈祷。
Until that time, I shall pray for thy soul.

石化的浪潮在她身上蔓延。
Waves of cold stone scrape over her skin as she readies herself for battle.

她向下，迈入无光的黑暗。
Then begins her journey down.

在火力稍微停歇的间隙，叶尔莫莱回到了战壕。
In a brief lull between volleys, Yermolai returns to the trenches.

他很快在众多灰色军装中找到了自己的长官。
It's little trouble to find his commander in the sea of gray uniforms.

刻雷乌斯：……机枪火力点必须留在原地，我们已经和对面的守军取得联系，他们会在下次攻势中与我们共同组成火力网。
Creius: To summarize, your troops must stay in place for the time being. We've made contact with the other side. They'll cooperate with you to create a fire network against the enemy.

埃里希：但愿他们真的会配合。
Erich: Let's hope they do cooperate.

刻雷乌斯：重塑之手对人类发动了战争，我们必须共渡难关。
Creius: Manus Vindictae has waged war against all humankind. We must work together if we're to get through this.

失去长官的新任连长烦闷地敲了敲钢盔，咬着嘴唇，从基金会行动队长面前离开。
Erich knocks his helmet with frustration as he leaves, chafing against his orders, burdened by the lives placed in his care. Wishing now, more than ever, that he was just a soldier again.

叶尔莫莱迎上去。
Yermolai steps forward.

“猎犬”：这会儿由你来当军官了？
Hound: So you're their commander too now, huh?

刻雷乌斯：我已经说服部分士兵与基金会合作。
Creius: All I did was convince them to work with the Foundation.

“猎犬”：你不能代表基金会，基金会还没有通过你的方案，给你授权。
Hound: But you don't represent the Foundation—not without proper authorization for your plan.

刻雷乌斯：此时此刻，在这些绝望的士兵面前，我可以代表基金会。
你的任务完成没有？
Creius: The soldiers are desperate. I won't hesitate to do what I must to restore their hope. What's the status on your mission?

“猎犬”：石像鬼已经在向目标地点出发了，保守估计还要再等一个小时。
Hound: The Gargoyle's en route to the target location as we speak. Conservative estimate says she'll take another hour to get there.

“猎犬”的语调变得暗哑。
Hound's voice comes out low and hoarse.

“猎犬”：……但我们不知道地下到底有什么，她可能会死。
Hound: But who knows what she'll come up against? She might not make it.

刻雷乌斯：我没想到你在这个时候会心生怜悯。
Creius: Unusual for you to show compassion in such a moment.

“猎犬”：我只是想起一些令人生厌的事，刻雷乌斯。
Hound: It just brings back unpleasant memories. You know what I'm talking about, Creius.

下属的嘴角勾起一丝毫不掩饰的嘲讽，而长官只是面不改色地无视了这支小插曲。
That wolfish grin returns to Hound's face, and Creius ignores it once more.

刻雷乌斯：那就再等一个小时。
Creius: Then we'll wait one more hour.

刻雷乌斯：那时基金会的援军应该也快到了……我们可以再想办法。
Creius: The Foundation's reinforcements will likely have arrived by then. Should it come to it, we will regroup and consider our next steps with them.

“猎犬”：呵——如果真有支援的话。
Hound: Heh, if there really are reinforcements, that is.

刻雷乌斯：新的攻势来了，准备防御。
Creius: They're launching a second offensive! Hold your ground!

燃烧的微粒被热浪掀上半空，随后化为灰烬，如雪花般纷纷洒落战场。
Charred earth splinters in the air, falling like black snow over the battlefield.

士兵们经受了又一次冲击。他们散在战壕中，神色木然地紧紧抱着胸前的武器。
The soldiers reel from another shockwave. Scattered across the trenches, they grip their weapons tight, certain only of the coming battle.

刻雷乌斯：……
Creius: ...

男人的食指在枪机上敲出微弱的声响。
His index finger taps his rifle's receiver with anticipation.

他再一次拿出通讯器，等待着。
He pulls out his communicator again and waits.

“哔哔——”
*beep-beep*

刻雷乌斯：……终于。
Creius: Finally ...

“鹰派”领袖伊里内伊的名字出现在屏幕上。
The name Irinei appears on screen.

伊里内伊：——刻雷乌斯，你还在前线吗？
Irinei: Creius, are you still on the front?

刻雷乌斯：是，伊里内伊委员。我能坚守的时间不多了。
Creius: Yes, Mr. Irinei, but I don't think we can hold out much longer.

刻雷乌斯：委员会有决定了吗？
Creius: Has the Committee reached a decision?

伊里内伊：他们仍在争吵不休，你的“前线应急预案”对“鸽派”来说太过荒唐，他们不愿意接受接管军队带来的政治风险。
Irinei: Not yet; the debate is still ongoing. The Doves find your "frontline contingency plan" absurd. They disapprove of the political risks involved in taking control of various nations' armies.

伊里内伊：不过……就我个人而言，我想问，你是否明确地知道自己想要达成什么目的？
Irinei: But I personally find it feasible. Just to be sure, do you have a clear understanding of your ultimate goal?

刻雷乌斯无声地深吸一口气。
He takes a deep, silent breath.

刻雷乌斯：重塑之手对基金会发动了一场跨时代的战争，它必然要进行到其中的一方彻底灭亡为止。
Creius: This war between Manus Vindictae and the Foundation will only end once one of the two parties is completely destroyed.

刻雷乌斯：而我不希望基金会成为失败的那一方。
Creius: And I refuse to let it be the Foundation.

刻雷乌斯：如今的芝诺不足以应对这场战争，基金会需要扩充兵力。目前仍然留在前线的士兵是我们最直接的希望。
Creius: If we're to prevail, the Foundation cannot rely on Zeno alone. We need more capable soldiers—soldiers like these on the front lines.

刻雷乌斯：他们中的一些人也许会同意加入基金会，继续与重塑之手作战。
Creius: With the proper arrangements, we may be able to recruit them to our cause. We'd have a whole new army to fight Manus Vindictae.

伊里内伊：即使如此，你能带回来的人数也相当有限。十万人不足以维持一场现代战争。
Irinei: But even if you manage to bring them all—say, one hundred thousand soldiers—on board, it still won't be enough to sustain modern warfare.

刻雷乌斯：我提出的不是一个局部战术，它需要在战略层面上执行。基金会应该派人收拢所有遭到重塑之手攻击的人类军队。
Creius: This is about the bigger strategic picture, not just a single recruitment effort. I'm suggesting that the Foundation start canvassing all human armies, especially those under attack by the Manus.

伊里内伊：战略层面……你考虑过这些军队所属的国家会做出什么反应吗？
Irinei: Bigger strategic picture. What about the governments behind these armies? Have you considered how they might react?

刻雷乌斯：重塑之手的进攻会让人类国家意识到，基金会是他们最后的依靠。
Creius: It's about time they realized that the Foundation is their only hope—the last bastion for humanity to unite against their shared enemy.

刻雷乌斯：何况……我们无法为一个错谬的时代负责。下一次“暴雨”降临时，这个时代的一切都会消逝。
Creius: The Foundation cannot take responsibility for all the lives in this era or in any other. The "Storm" is a near inevitability, and so too is the loss of many.

刻雷乌斯：但重塑之手一定会把战争带向新的时代。基金会必须要保有一支能够跨越“暴雨”的军队。
Creius: Once it does come, the Manus won't hesitate to drag war into that new era—into any new era. It's time the Foundation took action and built an army capable of crossing the "Storm."

伊里内伊：……
Irinei: ...

通讯另一头的政客陷入了长时间的沉默。
The politician on the other end falls into a long silence.

伊里内伊：按你的想法去做，刻雷乌斯。
Irinei: Enact your plan, Creius.

伊里内伊：只要你能先取得成功，那么……
Irinei: As long as you're successful on your end ...

伊里内伊：……我会解决政治问题。
Irinei: I will deal with the political obstacles in your way.

通讯被挂断。
The call is cut.

男人长舒一口气。
Creius exhales.

“警官”：下一步怎么做，长官？
"Officer": What next, sir?

青年注视着刻雷乌斯，忠诚地等待新的指令。
The young soldier watches Creius, waiting for orders with a dutiful stare.

刻雷乌斯：……
Creius: ...

他望向299高地，除了持续不断的炮火声外，重塑之手的阵地仍然没有任何动静。
He casts a look toward Hill 299. The Manus Vindictae stronghold bristles with flashes of gunfire, yet to him it looks as if it were a slumbering beast.

刻雷乌斯：……再坚持一个小时。
Creius: We stand our ground for an hour.

11TH-22 硫磺火 / Brimstone and Fire

艾格尼丝的声音已经消散无踪，耳畔只有难以辨认的嗡鸣。
Though Agnès's voice has vanished, the sharp ringing in her ears remains.

玛丽安娜：……什么声音？
Sentinel: What's that sound?

她将更多的注意力投向声音来源的方向，黑暗如帷幕般被切开——本不该出现的阴影正潜伏在一块残骸之后。
She casts more attention in the direction of the source of the sound, and the darkness is sliced like a curtain—a shadow that shouldn't be there is lurking behind a piece of wreckage.

？？？：……咳咳——呃——呃……
???: *cough* Ugh ...

他趴在地上，用淌着鲜血的手指在地面绘出杂乱无章的印记。
He lies prone, using bloodied fingers to scrawl erratic symbols across the ground.

？？？：……
???: ...

当闯入者接近时，他缓缓抬起头。
As the intruder draws near, he slowly raises his head.

玛丽安娜：又是你。
Sentinel: Oh. It's you.

施特林：凶手，恶鬼！你害死了我，害死了科尔腾，欧根……欧根也被你杀了。
Sterling: You! You murderer! You murdered me. You murdered Kolten. *cough* You murdered Eugen too!

施特林：可恨的魔鬼，杀人魔……
Sterling: You devil! You murderous demon—

施特林：啊——
Sterling: Aaagghh!

玛丽安娜：我不介意再来一次。
Sentinel: I have no qualms in doing so again.

近乎凝固的黑色“血液”在地面漫延。
Thick, congealed black blood spreads across the ground.

玛丽安娜：幻觉……可悲的把戏。
Sentinel: Pathetic illusions.

玛丽安娜：还有人。
Sentinel: Incoming attack.

玛丽安娜：身后。
Sentinel: From behind.

玛丽安娜：右前。
Sentinel: From the right.

玛丽安娜：脚下。
Sentinel: From below.

玛丽安娜：就在眼前——
Sentinel: Right before me!

士兵？：——！
Soldier?: ...!

石化的尖爪迅速而精准地钳住了柔软的脖颈，敌人被拎到半空中，双手徒劳地抓挠着石像鬼粗硬的手臂。
Petrified claws clamp down on his soft neck with precision, pulling him up into mid-air, his hands clawing against the chokehold.

士兵？：呃——放了我……求——你——
Soldier?: Ghk ... Let me go, please.

她不断施加的力量停顿了一秒，在仅有一个喘息的间隙，渴望摆脱钳制的士兵从腰间抽出一把尖锐的匕首。
She eases her grip if only for the length of a breath, yet the soldier seizes the moment for all he's worth, drawing a blade from his belt.

士兵？：……咕唔！
Soldier?: Urgh!

她来到了绽放死亡之花的苦难之地。
She arrives at the land where the flower of death blooms.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

尸横遍野。
Corpses are strewn across the ground.

一个身影在那尽头等待她的到来。
A figure waits at the far end.

重塑军官？：你究竟杀了多少人？——这些死于你之手的人都是神秘学家，你的同胞。
Manus Officer?: How many have you killed? Do you even keep count? Remember, they were all arcanists like you.

玛丽安娜：这与种族无关。
Sentinel: Race is of no matter.

重塑军官？：我喜欢这个回答。杀戮只是杀戮，与弱者毫无关系。
Manus Officer?: Hm. So the killer does the killing, and the dead have no say at all. I like it.

一颗子弹穿透了军官的心脏。石像鬼没有费神去反驳他的话。
A bullet rips through the officer's heart. A simple, blunt retort.

她前进一步，发现同样的人站在自己面前。
She steps forward, only to find the figure standing before her once again.

重塑军官？：还要往前走吗？
Manus Officer?: Haven't had enough?

玛丽安娜：让开。
Sentinel: Begone.

玛丽安娜：终有一日，我会亲手将你送回地狱，永堕烈焰与熔岩之所。
Sentinel: One day, I shall personally deliver you to the fires of hell where you belong.

重塑军官？：看来你知晓我的身份。
Manus Officer?: Oh. It sounds like you know who I am.

玛丽安娜：不要以为我会被你借用的外表所蒙蔽，我知道你一直都缠绕在我的家族之血中——
Sentinel: Do not think me deceived by your disguise. I am well aware that your taint has long been tangled in the blood of my family.

石像鬼们：——恶魔。
Gargoyles: Demon.

玛丽安娜：拉蒂斯？
Sentinel: Ladislas?

她虔诚的堂兄出现在地狱之中。
Her devout cousin appears in the midst of this strange hell.

拉蒂斯：堂亲，我为你带来最后的警告……你与堕落的距离不远了，过去数年的杀戮已经让你站在地狱深渊的边缘。
Ladislas: Dear cousin, I bring thee a final warning. Thou art but a step away from utter corruption. Thou hast killed many in the years past, and now thou dost stand at the edge of the abyss.

拉蒂斯：你也许不了解那些堕落的先祖经历了怎样的折磨，他们的良知和信仰全都被摧毁，只留下永不停止的嗜血欲望。
Ladislas: Hast thou not understood the suffering endured by our fallen ancestors? Their conscience crumbled, their faith shattered, leaving naught but an insatiable thirst for blood.

拉蒂斯：我不希望你也走上一样的道路。
Ladislas: It paineth me to see thee walk that same wretched path.

“恶魔”彬彬有礼地站在远处，等到教士说完之后才再度开口。
The demon stands to the side with unhinged politesse, waiting until Ladislas has finished speaking before speaking again.

“恶魔”：我从不引诱任何人。
The Demon: Well, don't blame me. I did nothing to entice her.

它的声音仿佛不再是从眼前的这一具身躯中发出，而是来自黑暗天空的遥远尽头。
Its voice no longer seems to come from the body before her but from some faraway place in the darkened sky.

“恶魔”：是玛丽安娜自己做出的选择，她的双手早已浸在血泊之中。
The Demon: Marianne made this choice herself. Her hands have long been soaked in blood.

“恶魔”：可她自始至终都没有被所谓的负罪感所困，这是我钟爱她的理由。
The Demon: And yet, she has never been troubled by that so-called "guilt" of yours. I've come to adore her for that.

拉蒂斯：也许你选的道路能拯救泥淖中的人们，但这个人不能是你，堂亲。
Ladislas: Perhaps it is true that this path of carnage shall save many lives, but why, I pray, must it be thee who walkest it?

拉蒂斯：我们流淌着不洁的血液，太多的杀戮注定会让灵魂落入万劫不复的深渊。
Ladislas: Our blood beareth an impurity like no other. To kill so many is to will thyself to the bottom of the abyss, never to return.

拉蒂斯：这一次你将带走的是上万人的生命，他们中有多少误入歧途的无辜者？
Ladislas: The ten thousand thou art soon to kill—consider, I pray—how many among them are innocent victims of deception and coercion?

拉蒂斯：杀死他们的罪孽，会比你过去所积累的还要多。
Ladislas: The weight of so many lives shall weigh upon thee in far greater measure than any sin thou hast yet borne. What good shall it profit thee to gain the whole world, yet forfeit thy soul?

“恶魔”：你也在计算生命的数量吗，拉蒂斯？
The Demon: Did I hear that right? Are you also calculating the lives, Ladislas?

拉蒂斯：——！
Ladislas: ...!

拉蒂斯：停、停止你的污言秽语！
Ladislas: Speak no more of thy filthy words!

“恶魔”：我愚昧的孩子……
The Demon: Oh, you silly, stubborn child.

“恶魔”以优雅的步态接近拉蒂斯。
The demon approaches Ladislas with sharp, graceful steps.

拉蒂斯：你想做什么，邪恶的——呃——！
Ladislas: What art thou ... O wicked dem—Rrghk!

教士的喉咙被一双手死死掐住。
His throat is seized in both hands.

拉蒂斯：唔——你——玛丽安……
Ladislas: Urggh ... Thou ... Marie ...

拉蒂斯：……
Ladislas: ...

“恶魔”松开手，拉蒂斯的躯体倒在地上的众多尸体之间。
The demon releases its grip. Ladislas's body collapses among the other corpses.

玛丽安娜以审视的目光看着眼前的这一幕。
Sentinel watches the scene with a probing gaze.

“恶魔”：——还是我来帮你做这件事吧，玛丽安娜。这个疯子，实在是太吵闹了。
The Demon: There, I silenced the noisy fool for you, Marianne.

玛丽安娜：你的表演毫无意义。
Sentinel: Such pantomime shall not move me.

玛丽安娜：他只是一个有形无实的幻影，残留在我脑海中的声音。
Sentinel: This "Ladislas" was naught but an echo lingering in my mind. An illusion.

“恶魔”：可我不是，我是永远与你共生的本性。
The Demon: Oh, but I'm not. I am your very nature. The core of your being.

大地在颤动，打破了血腥而短暂的宁静。
The ground shakes, and their bloody silence is shattered.

“恶魔”毕恭毕敬地后退一步让出道路，它先向石像鬼投去一抹阴沉的微笑，随后扭头张望。
The demon makes way for her, casting a grim smile at the Gargoyle before turning its head to look around.

在它身后，一支庞大的军团正轰鸣着赶赴战场。
As an army rumbles into view.

先头的装甲部队碾过残破的尸体，怪异的引擎声愈发清晰。
The strange sound of engines grows clearer as the armored vanguard grinds over mangled corpses.

“恶魔”：看来重塑之手发现了你的到来。
The Demon: Oh, Manus Vindictae. They've finally noticed you.

恶魔转过身去，背向玛丽安娜。
The demon turns its back to Sentinel.

“恶魔”：——不过，这些可悲的敌人没有击败我们的力量。
The Demon: What a shame. They don't stand a chance against our ferocity, do they, Marianne?

玛丽安娜握紧手中的枪，未与“恶魔”同行，也没有转身离去。
She grips her gun, neither joining the demon, nor turning away.

她轻吻冰冷的枪机。
She presses a kiss to the cold receiver.

玛丽安娜：……我看见罪人将灵魂出卖给恶魔，他们行过的土地皆滋生恶果。
Sentinel: I have seen sinners forsake themselves in service of the devil. The land they trod upon yielded only bitter, cursed fruit.

“恶魔”：来吧——
The Demon: Come!

玛丽安娜：现在，忏悔的时间已过。
Sentinel: But the hour for repentance has long since passed.

“恶魔”：与我一起——
The Demon: Come with me!

玛丽安娜：天上——降下了硫磺与烈火！
Sentinel: Then the Lord rained upon them brimstone and fire!

“恶魔”：——毁灭他们！
The Demon: Let's kill them all—together!

玛尔纱：……
Marsha: ...

玛丽安娜：玛尔纱？
Sentinel: Marsha?

骑士站在风车下，黑色的战马在草地中悠然踱步。
Marsha stands beneath a windmill. Her black warhorse pacing idly in the grass.

玛尔纱：我总觉得，我永远不会忘记这座风车和原野。
Marsha: I don't think I'll ever forget this windmill—the calm of this field.

玛尔纱：第一次来的时候，我居然没有感到惊讶——战争中怎么会有这样一片宁静的土地。
Marsha: I can't believe I didn't appreciate how peaceful this place was the first time I came here.

她闭上眼，深吸一口饱含青草芬芳的空气。
She closes her eyes and breathes in the sweet scent of the meadow.

玛尔纱：也许是因为土地本身就是宁静的，人的生活也应该是……我们以为战争已经结束，一切都会重归安宁。
Marsha: Perhaps it's because the land was quiet, just like our lives once were. And back then, we thought everything would be peaceful again once the war was over.

玛丽安娜：对不起。
Sentinel: I'm sorry.

玛尔纱：你怎么又在道歉？
Marsha: Why? There's no need to apologize.

玛丽安娜：我差点杀了你……不，事实上，对我来说，我的确杀了你……和其他我杀害的人一样。
Sentinel: I was nigh on killing you. No, in a way, I did kill you, just as I have killed so many others.

玛尔纱：这不是我们任何人的错。
Marsha: It's not our fault. None of this is …

玛丽安娜：也许你能原谅我，可……那些永远失去生命的人，我没有机会，也没有资格得到他们的原谅。
Sentinel: You may have granted me your forgiveness, but those who have forever lost their lives due to my actions—I shall never have the chance, nor the right, to earn theirs.

玛尔纱：我们没有发动战争，却饱受战争带给我们的苦难。
Marsha: We didn't start this war. Yet, we have had to bear the brunt of the pain it has caused.

玛尔纱：如果战争中的这一切罪恶最终还要加在我们身上，这种不公……
Marsha: If all the sins of war are laid at our feet, where's the fairness in that?

玛尔纱：我不能接受。
Marsha: No. I refuse to accept it.

骑士为不公而愤懑。
Marsha seethes at injustice.

玛尔纱：玛丽，等真正的和平到来之后……
Marsha: Marie, perhaps when peace finally comes ...

一阵风卷走了她的声音。
A gust carries her voice away.

玛丽安娜：……？
Sentinel: ...?

风势越来越大，她能听见老旧风车发出的“吱嘎”声。
The wind howls, and in it she hears the creaking of the old windmill.

玛尔纱：……
Marsha: ...

玛丽安娜沿着小路向前走，想要与她站得更近些……
Sentinel walks along the path, wanting to stand closer to her.

——直到眼前的一切陡然被炮火撕裂。
—until the scene is torn apart by gunfire.

玛丽安娜：——玛尔纱！
Sentinel: Marsha!

士兵？：去死！
Soldier?: Die!

士兵？：啊……呃啊——
Soldier?: Arrgh ...

军团中的最后一人痛苦地倒下，残骸遍地的无人区在遥远的嗡鸣声中陷入寂静。
Wreckage is strewn over no man's land. The last of the assembled force falls with a gurgling scream that ushers in the silence of death.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

恶魔与石像鬼并肩而立，共同观望眼前遍布死亡的土地。
The demon and the Gargoyle stand side by side, looking over the destruction.

“恶魔”：鲜血汇为湖海，颅骨堆成山岳。一切憎恶的被灭绝，一切贪求的被夺取。
The Demon: Take it all in, Marianne—the pools of blood, the piled corpses, the lingering echoes of the dead, their whimpering, desperate cries.

“恶魔”：多少年过去了……我未能看见如此盛大的血祭。玛丽安娜，你已唤醒了最古老的本性。
The Demon: Aahh. How long has it been since I last witnessed such a beautifully gruesome massacre? The ancient bloodlust within you truly has awakened.

“恶魔”：你已经杀尽了阻拦你的敌人。来吧，把炸药交给我。
The Demon: You slaughtered every last one of them. Well done. Now, hand me the explosives. It's time to end them all.

“恶魔”伸出双手，讨要那件能夺走一万人生命的武器。
The demon holds out his hands, asking for the weapon that will take the lives of 10,000 men.

玛丽安娜：……可悲的东西。
Sentinel: Get thee behind me, Demon.

“恶魔”：你仍有权力二选其一。一个选择有一万条生命之重，而另一个的重量则有十倍胜之。
The Demon: I won't force you. The choice is still yours. So, which will it be? The weight of ten thousand lives, or one that is ten times harder to bear?

“恶魔”：当然，十万人的死亡并不与你直接相关，你无需为他们负责，只不过……
The Demon: Well? Their blood will be on your hands, that's for certain, but the responsibility won't rest on you alone. Your soon-to-be-blood-soaked hands have been forced.

“恶魔”：你、只能、二选其一。
The Demon: These are the only choices you have left.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

石像鬼取下那一捆沉重的炸药，握在手中。
The Gargoyle removes the bundle of heavy explosives and grasps them as tightly as if they were prayer beads.

玛丽安娜：……我没有能力洗净血液中的污秽，如同我无法卸下早已承受的罪孽。
Sentinel: I am powerless to cleanse the filth that muddies my blood, just as I am powerless to erase the sins I have already borne.

玛丽安娜：我知道我已经堕入地狱，古老的邪恶在我的灵魂中生长。
Sentinel: I have descended into the depths of hell—I know that. And this ancient darkness has already taken root in my soul.

玛丽安娜：可是，如果牺牲一人就可以拯救十人，牺牲一万人，可以拯救十万人……如果必须有人做出选择……
Sentinel: But if sacrificing one can save ten, if sacrificing ten thousand can save a hundred thousand, if someone must make that impossible choice ...

玛丽安娜：我可以背负选择的罪恶。
Sentinel: Then I am willing to bear that sin.

最终，炸药被交给“恶魔”。
She hands the explosives over to the demon.

“恶魔”：这就对了。从此以后，我会与你结伴而行，赐予你更强大的——
The Demon: That's the spirit. From now on, we will walk together, side by side, a greater power as one—

话音未落，刺刀捅穿了它的身体。
Before he can say anything, the bayonet stabs through his body.

“恶魔”：……？！
The Demon: …?!

玛丽安娜抽出刺刀，将“恶魔”推开，后者踉踉跄跄地退到更远的地方。
Sentinel pulls out her bayonet and pushes the demon away, who staggers further back.

“恶魔”：……
The Demon: ...

“恶魔”：真有意思……你知道这伤不了我，玛丽安娜，这一切又是为了什么？
The Demon: You are fascinating, Marianne. You know this won't harm me. So, why did you do it?

石像鬼发出沉重的喘息。
She lets out a heavy labored breath.

玛丽安娜：看清我，“恶魔”，我不是你熟悉的那些先祖，受到引诱而在嗜血的欲望中无法自拔。
Sentinel: Look upon me, Demon. I am not like my ancestors, to be led astray by their thirst for blood and your honeyed words.

玛丽安娜：无论我做出什么选择，都与你毫无关系，这一切都出自我自己的意志。
Sentinel: Whatever choice I make, I make of my own free will.

玛丽安娜：……我会夺取你的力量，而你，没有资格号令我的灵魂。
Sentinel: I will not let your taint spread within my soul, yet still, your power shall be mine to command.

“恶魔”：呵呵……
The Demon: Heh-heh ...

“恶魔”：哈哈……哈哈哈哈哈——
The Demon: Haha ... Hahahahaha!

伪造的“身体”消失了，恶魔在地狱中发出狂笑。
The figure vanishes, yet she can still feel the demon cackle madly from the depths of hell.

你是一个纯粹的天才，玛丽安娜。残酷的杀手，贪婪的魔鬼——
You truly are a genius, Marianne. A ruthless killer, a greedy devil ...

——我最钟爱的孩子！
And my most worthy child!

来吧，让我们在地狱中称王！
Join me! Let us reign together in hell!

玛丽安娜：艾格尼丝，小时候，我不明白你给我读的那些故事——为什么有人可以背负世人的一切罪孽？
Sentinel: Agnès, when I was young, I never truly understood the words you spake. Why would one man willingly bear the sins of all the world for the sake of others?

玛丽安娜：如果有人要将一切罪责与痛苦都交给我，那该是多么的不公与不幸……
Sentinel: I lingered on the thought of it—if all guilt and suffering were placed upon me, how cruel and unjust that would be.

玛丽安娜：但现在，我想……所幸它们最终也都交给了我。
Sentinel: But now I think, perhaps it is best that they are mine alone to bear.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

玛丽安娜：对不起，艾格尼丝。
Sentinel: I'm sorry, Agnès.

Wir kommen hier raus, Bruder! Komm schon!：<color=white>没事了，兄弟，快过来吧。 <color=white>106团第3营的的士兵，请到我这里来！Soldiers of the 3rd Battalion, 106th Regiment, with me! <color=white>我们……得救了？W-Wir sind gerettet? <color=white>没错，让我看看——还能站起来，好样的，我们快一起离开这鬼地方。Ganz genau. We have to get them to the dressing station! <color=white>你能站起来吗？Tu peux te lever ? <color=white>你是谁……我、我听不懂你在说什么。W-Wer bist du? I-Ich verstehe nicht, was du sagst. <color=white>小心穿越无人区——我们正在剪除铁丝网，请稍作等待！Tread carefully; we're crossing no man's land! Hold strong while we cut the barbed wire! <color=white>来，跟上基金会的人，我们走——快起来！Là, on peut suivre les gens de la Fondation. Allez, ressaisis-toi !
刻雷乌斯: ——所有行动人员：299高地已被摧毁，重塑之手的威胁已解除。刻雷乌斯: 按原定计划撤离。刻雷乌斯: 重塑之手的堡垒已被摧毁，我已成功带领部队向后方防线撤退。刻雷乌斯: 我明白……感谢您关键时刻的支持，伊里内伊先生。
<color=white>We're getting out of here, brother! Come on! <color=white>Soldiers of the 3rd Battalion, 106th Regiment, with me! <color=white>W-We're saved? <color=white>That's right. Alright, good, you can still stand. Let's leave these damn trenches behind. <color=white>I've found him! He's still alive! <color=white>Bring him with you! Hurry! <color=white>Multiple severely wounded over here! All available medics with me! We have to get them to the dressing station! <color=white>Can you stand? <color=white>Wh-Who are you? I-I don't understand what you're saying. <color=white>Tread carefully; we're crossing no man's land! Hold strong while we cut the barbed wire! <color=white>There, we can follow the Foundation's people. Come on, pull yourself together!
