Thank you for your support in this critical time, Mr. Irinei.

11TH-23 赦免令 / The Pardon

又一次月升月落之后，屹立不倒的教堂再次接纳白昼的光明。
After yet another night passes, the hidden chapel once again welcomes the light of day.

此时已接近正午，草被绵软的庭院内依旧保持惯有的静谧，只不过此刻多了一份因静候而生的肃穆。
Time passes, reaching near to midday, and the grassy courtyard holds its quiet with a patience born of humility.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

受企盼的人终于出现在林地边缘——她已经用一夜的时间处理好醒目的伤痕。
The awaited figure finally appears at the forest's edge. She's spent the night tending to her wounds.

石像鬼妇人：玛丽，你回来了。
Female Gargoyle: My, Marie, thou hast returned!

她按捺住上前拥抱的念头——因为此时她正用双手端着一只装着咖啡与茶点的银盘。
She holds back the urge to embrace her family—her arms are filled with a silver tray of coffee and pastries.

玛丽安娜：咖啡？
Sentinel: Coffee?

石像鬼妇人：没错，照你喜欢的——不加奶也不加糖。另外还有一些香草马卡龙和蒙布朗。
Female Gargoyle: Yes, just to thy liking—no milk, no sugar. There are also vanilla macarons and Mont Blanc besides.

对于刚从战场上退下的士兵来说，这些食物与器皿的色彩营造了一种不真实的氛围。
The bright colors of the pastries feel all the more surreal for the darkness she has gone through.

玛丽安娜从堂姨手中接过温热的咖啡，怀着不可思议的心情轻啜一口。当然，不及巴黎咖啡馆的出品，但此刻亦是珍馐美味。
Sentinel takes the warm coffee from her aunt's hands and takes a small sip in disbelief. Of course, it's far from the quality of a Parisian café, but at this moment, it is more than enough.

玛丽安娜：姨妈，这些是从哪里弄来的？
Sentinel: Where did you get these desserts?

妇人双手握在一起，展露出一道有些哀婉的苦笑。
The woman clasps her hands together, wearing a faint, bittersweet smile.

石像鬼妇人：看看谁来了，玛丽。
Female Gargoyle: Look, who is here, my sweetie.

她让出身子，玛丽安娜即刻注意到那久未得见的高大身影。
Sentinel takes notice of the tall figure stepping into view—a face she has not seen for a long time.

埃曼努埃尔：玛丽安娜。
Immanuel: Marianne.

玛丽安娜：……父亲。
Sentinel: Father.

玛丽安娜：你为什么过来了？
Sentinel: What brought you here?

埃曼努埃尔：总统已经为你签发了赦免令，你可以回后方了。
Immanuel: A pardon hath been issued by the president. Thou art free.

埃曼努埃尔：另外，拉蒂斯病得不轻，在信仰问题上，他太钻牛角尖，我虽然预料到了这一天……
Immanuel: As for Ladislas, he is gravely ill. His stubbornness was ever bound to lead to trouble.

他以略带不满的方式结束了话题。
He ends the topic with mild discontent.

埃曼努埃尔：总而言之，我是来接你们离开的。
Immanuel: Hmph. To answer thy question: I am here to gather ye. We are to depart.

玛丽安娜：这么说，现在家里是你在管事。
Sentinel: So, you are now the leader of the clan?

埃曼努埃尔：泰内布朗热家在战争中损失惨重，需要有人在战后领导家族的重建。我正在重新与失散的家族成员取得联系。
Immanuel: Verily. After all we have suffered under this war, someone must lead the Ténébrun family's reconstruction. I seek to re-establish contact with those of our kin with whom we have lost fellowship.

埃曼努埃尔：重塑之手尚未威胁到巴黎，我在蒙马特购置了几套房产，在重塑之手和基金会的冲突结束之前可供暂时居住。
Immanuel: The hand of Manus Vindictae has not yet fallen upon Paris. I have purchased a number of dwellings in Montmartre. They are to be our temporary homes until the conflict between the Manus and the Foundation reaches its end.

泰内布朗热先生以不容置喙的姿态转身，面向艾格尼丝。
The Ténébrun patriarch makes an imperturbable gesture as he turns to face Agnès.

埃曼努埃尔：艾格尼丝要送回鲁昂，安置在家族的墓地中。
Immanuel: Agnès shall be sent to our cemetery in Rouen.

玛丽安娜：……墓地？
Sentinel: Cemetery?

她不能理解这个词。
She cannot—or will not—accept the words.

玛丽安娜：艾格尼丝没有死，她只是……出于……拉蒂斯说的某些理由……
Sentinel: But Agnès is not dead; she's simply ... Ladislas said there was a reason behind her—

玛丽安娜抬起眼，对上父亲有些哀其不争的目光。
Marianne raises her eyes and meets her father's mournful gaze.

埃曼努埃尔：你从来都不尊重家族的传统，所以才会被拉蒂斯的疯言疯语所欺骗。
Immanuel: This is what comes of disrespecting tradition, Marianne. Thou wert too easily swayed by Ladislas's maddened words.

玛丽安娜：他撒谎了？
Sentinel: He lied to us?

埃曼努埃尔：不，我相信他不会撒谎，只是在对灵知的探索中太过偏狭。
Immanuel: Nay. I believe not that such was his intent. He was simply too fervent in his pursuit of Gnosis.

埃曼努埃尔：家族中没有任何记载表明，预兆会以这种奇怪的方式降临在我们的族人身上。
Immanuel: There is no record in the family archives that suggests any sort of prophecy should befall our kin in so strange a form.

埃曼努埃尔：艾格尼丝的“雕塑化”只是一个平凡的惨剧，没有任何隐秘或神圣的意味。
Immanuel: Agnès's condition is the result of a tragic accident, nothing more. There is no divine meaning behind it whatsoever.

埃曼努埃尔：她只是因为太过害怕落在头上的炮火，才在未成熟的神秘术上失手，在石化中没有留下任何一丝血肉。
Immanuel: Her fear of the war was too great. She simply faltered in the casting of her arcane skill and petrified her body to the core.

埃曼努埃尔：这就是全部的故事。
Immanuel: That is all.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

埃曼努埃尔：你和拉蒂斯都把她看得太重，可艾格尼丝终究只是一个普通的孩子，并非天上降下的天使。
Immanuel: I know well that Agnès meant a great deal to both Ladislas and thee, but she was only an ordinary child. She was not an angel descended from heaven.

埃曼努埃尔：我也为此难过，但你必须相信，不会再有任何奇迹降临到艾格尼丝身上。她永远都只能是一座雕塑。
Immanuel: Though it doth bring sorrow for me to say, we must all come to accept that no miracle shall ever come to Agnès—she will forever remain a statue.

父亲伸出手，轻轻拍了拍女儿已承担了许多重量的肩膀。
He reaches out to take his daughter's shoulder, already bearing too many burdens.

父女没有再交谈什么，只是在艾格尼丝的“雕塑”前戚然沉吟。
Their conversation falls away into a pensive silence before the "statue" of Agnès.

泰内布朗热先生率先离开了，他还有更重要的事情要处理——教堂外已经停着好几辆搬家用的卡车。
He is the first to leave, attending to more pressing matters—several moving trucks are already parked outside the church.

颤巍巍的锁链声刺破了空气。
Trembling chains pierce the air.

玛丽安娜：……？
Sentinel: ...?

拉蒂斯：玛丽安娜，你竟然回来了……
Ladislas: Marianne, thou hast returned. How ...?

教士步履蹒跚，似乎正在被什么无形的东西推搡着向玛丽安娜靠近。
He staggers forward, as if pushed by some invisible force, drawing closer to Sentinel.

他的手心捧着一串闪着寒光的锁链。
In his palm lies a chain that glints coldly in the sunlight.

玛丽安娜：该死的，我以为父亲只是——你真的生病了吗？
Sentinel: S**t, I thought Father was only ... Have you truly fallen ill?

拉蒂斯：我生了病，那你呢，玛丽安娜？——你竟不知道自己陷入了比罹患疾病更可悲的境地中了吗？
Ladislas: That I have. But what of thee, Marianne? Art thou not in a condition far graver than my own? Or art thou simply too blind to see it?

他吐出疯癫的言辞，完全失去了过往谨慎克制的谦逊。
He babbles on. With every word, his madness grows. There seems to be no trace of his old humility left.

拉蒂斯：我在你身上看见了多么沉重的罪孽，可悲的人！而我也一样……一样……天啊，我在你身上嗅到了地狱的气味……
Ladislas: Thy soul is stained with the wickedness of sin! Thou art as miserable as I ... O Lord, I-I can smell the stench of hell upon thee ...

拉蒂斯：你从地狱归来了，玛丽安娜……可悲的人……
Ladislas: Thou hast passed through the gates of hell and returned, Marianne ... How wretched ...

玛丽安娜：拉蒂斯，你真的疯了。
Sentinel: You are ill, Ladislas. Gravely so.

玛丽安娜：到巴黎之后，去找一个安静的疗养院吧。
Sentinel: Take a moment's rest in the quiet of a sanatorium upon reaching Paris, won't you? It ought to do you good.

拉蒂斯狡黠地眯起眼，像一个正在分享秘密的孩童。
Ladislas squints like a child sharing a secret.

拉蒂斯：我也许会乖乖在疗养院休养，但你不想回去，对吧？
Ladislas: Perhaps I shall. But thou wilt not return with us, wilt thou?

玛丽安娜：……我还没有决定……
Sentinel: I am yet undecided. Perhaps I will ...

拉蒂斯：不……不！你不能回去，你永远不能再回去。
Ladislas: Nay. Nay. Thou must not! Thou must never return!

玛丽安娜：你说什么？
Sentinel: Why?

拉蒂斯：我和别人不一样，能在你身上看见特别的东西……你已经不再是——不再是……
Ladislas: I see that which others cannot, and I see it in thee. Thou art not who thou once wast! Inside thee, there is ...

拉蒂斯：恶魔……萦绕在家族之血中的恶魔，它睁开了眼睛……它的眼睛——
Ladislas: A demon, the demon which doth linger in our veins. It hath opened its eyes, its wretched eyes!

拉蒂斯：啊——
Ladislas: Aaagghh!

拉蒂斯发出痛苦的哀嚎，浑身颤抖不止，手中的锁链也连带着撞出更加刺耳的噪音。
Ladislas howls in pain, his body shaking violently. The chain in his hand clatters and rings.

拉蒂斯：不能回头了！你已经不能回头……你的路在外面，不在里面……
Ladislas: Thou cannot return—cannot turn back! For there is no path left for thee ...

拉蒂斯：但是……但是我想帮助你，我的堂亲。我会帮助所有人，但尤其是你，以偿还我的罪孽。
Ladislas: But ... but I desire naught more than to aid thee, my dear cousin. Yea, I shall help us all, but most especially thee—to atone for my transgressions ...

他止住了颤抖，以极尽恭顺的姿态低下瘦长的身躯，将手中的锁链捧在玛丽安娜眼前。
The shaking stops, and all at once, he bows with a gesture of utter submission, presenting the chain before her.

玛丽安娜：——拉蒂斯？
Sentinel: Ladislas?

拉蒂斯：这是束缚灵魂的枷锁……牢笼。是的，但我恳求你能将它收下……
Ladislas: These shackles are a soul-binding chain—a cage, yea, but I beg thee accept them.

拉蒂斯：我会奉献我的一生为你的灵魂祈祷，堂亲，日日夜夜，愿你的灵魂不至于永堕黑暗。
Ladislas: And I shall devote my life to prayer over thee—both night and day—that thy soul shall not be shaded in eternal darkness.

玛丽安娜：……
Sentinel: ...

拉蒂斯：愿你的血洁净，洒向大地，新的土地将因此繁茂。愿你走在地狱的路上，依旧念着神圣的名。
Ladislas: May thy blood be washed clean one day. May it nourish the soil when thou art laid to rest. May thy journey to hell yet be graced by God's mercy.

又是一份不轻的负累，它将时刻提醒拥有者可施加之恶的极限。
Another not-so-light burden to serve as a constant reminder of the limits of evil.

玛丽安娜：如果我不接受这份镣铐呢？
Sentinel: And if I refuse these shackles?

拉蒂斯：我的祈祷也不会因此停歇，一如过往的一切时日。
Ladislas: It mattereth not. I shall pray for thee still, as I have ever done.

艾格尼丝如同在静默地倾听着这一切。
A sudden impulse moves her to look at the statue of Agnès.

拉蒂斯：……
Ladislas: ...

最终，她取走了锁链。
At last, she takes the chain.

冰冷的金属垂在手中，如有千钧之重。
The metal hangs in her hand; its weight feels far greater than its size would merit.

玛丽安娜：告诉我父亲，我不回去了。
Sentinel: Tell my father that I will not return.

玛丽安娜：——除非战争有真正结束的那一天。
Sentinel: Until the true conflict is brought to an end.

11TH-24 山 / The Hill

一座完成的山。无法企及死亡的千万分之一。
A completed mountain. Though only a mere fraction of what death truly claims.

卡戎：……
Charon: ...

它扔下了过往的一切：一件大衣，一顶头盔，一双短靴……一只蝴蝶封面的笔记本。
It left everything behind: a coat, a helmet, a pair of boots ... a butterfly-covered notebook.

——曾属于名叫保罗的年轻人的一切。
—Everything that once belonged to a young man named Paul.

卡戎：你的战争结束了，保罗。
Charon: Your war is over, Paul.

遗物被妥善安葬在最后一处坟墓中，紧挨着一位在山顶死去的少校。
His belongings are fittingly buried at the last grave, beside the major who died atop the hill.

远处有渐近的马蹄声。
A clatter of hooves approaches from the road.

卡戎：……安德烈森？
Charon: Andreas?

一声轻柔到几乎像是不想吵醒任何人的呼唤。
The name is whispered softly, as if not to disturb those resting here.

它在软烂的泥土路上驻足，片刻之后，蹄声踏破晨雾，徐徐靠近。
The sound stops where gravel meets the mush of mud and snowmelt.

安德烈森：咴——
Andreas: Neigh—

一匹黑马出现在收尸人面前。
A black horse breaks the veil of mist and approaches.

它轻吐鼻息，渴望一次轻抚。
The horse exhales a comforting snort—leaning in—yearning for his hand.

卡戎：好孩子——
Charon: Good boy.

卡戎：你消失了很长一段时间——你又去了一些过于危险的地方寻找你丢失的好友？
Charon: You have been gone for a long time. Off to dangerous places again to search for your lost friends?

安德烈森：咴……
Andreas: ...

卡戎：或许在你身上附着着某种特殊的命运，使你能在这场屠杀中躲过众多致命的威胁。
Charon: It seems luck has been on your side. You have dodged danger time and again amidst this slaughter.

卡戎：但我仍然担心流弹与毒气会将你置于死地。
Charon: But I cannot help but worry that, one day, a stray bullet will pierce you, or a poison gas will choke you.

安德烈森：……咴咴——咴。
Andreas: Neigh!

马儿低下了头。
The horse lowers its head.

卡戎：我没有在责备你，安德烈森，相反，你能重新回到我身边，令我心怀感激。
Charon: Harshness is not my intention, Andreas. But I am grateful that you have returned to my side hale and whole.

亡者看向东方。日光升起之地，噩兆的乌云弥漫。
They look eastward. Toward the rising sun, where ominous clouds gather.

卡戎：该走了……下一个目的地无比遥远，我正需要你的帮助。
Charon: It's time. The next destination is a distant one. Your help will be appreciated.

安德烈森：——咴。
Andreas: ...

安德烈森向一侧偏头，示意主人注意早就靠到近前的青年人。
Andreas tilts its head to one side, signaling its master's attention to the youth who has arrived behind them.

“警官”：卡戎先生，这匹马是你的吗？
"Officer": Mr. Charon, is this your horse?

直到这时，迟钝的亡者才注意到有人向自己打招呼。
The grim figure turns his face toward the source of the question.

卡戎：……是的，年轻人。
Charon: In a sense, young man.

“警官”：那就没关系了。这匹马突然出现在蒙佩附近，我还以为和重塑之手有关系，就一直追了过来。
"Officer": Oh, then it's nothing. He showed up near Montpaix all by himself, so I followed him here to see if he might be connected to Manus Vindictae.

卡戎：基金会仍然留在蒙佩吗？
Charon: The Foundation is still in Montpaix?

“警官”：我们很快就会离开，军队需要转移到更安全的地方去。
"Officer": We'll head off soon along with the soldiers to a safer position.

“警官”：对了，你知道“乌鸫”去了哪里吗？
"Officer": By the way, do you know where Blackbird is?

卡戎：“乌鸫”？
Charon: Blackbird?

“警官”：噢，梅蕾尔，就是那个和你一起去前线的女孩。她在重塑之手发动袭击之后就失联了。
"Officer": Oh, I mean Merel—the girl who went to the front with you. I haven't been able to get in touch with her since the Manus attacked.

“警官”：我正在找她……希望她不要出什么事才好。
"Officer": Where could she be? I just hope she hasn't gotten herself into any serious trouble.

卡戎：她还活着。
Charon: She is alive and well.

意外的收获。青年的眼中显露出明显的光彩。
A surprise. The young man's eyes alight with joy.

“警官”：她还活着？！——你见过她？
"Officer": She is? Where did you see her?

卡戎：……我不能告诉你。
Charon: That, I cannot tell.

光彩瞬间熄灭，帕拉维扬怎么也没想到会在这个问题上遭到拒绝。
His gleam dims as Paravyan adjusts to the unexpected refusal.

“警官”：为什么？
"Officer": Why?

卡戎：她不希望你们找到她。
Charon: She does not wish to be found.

“警官”：什……什么？难道她不想回来吗？
"Officer": Wh-What? She doesn't wanna come back with us?

卡戎：是的。她很害怕之后的战争。
Charon: Correct. She is afraid of the war that lies ahead.

卡戎：真实的杀戮，直白的死亡……对这位少女来说，她或许没有做好接受这一切的准备。
Charon: Bloodshed, carnage ... She was unprepared to witness such harrowing scenes.

卡戎：她向我索要了一个承诺，不将她的行踪透露给基金会的诸位。
Charon: She requested I not reveal her whereabouts to the Foundation—in fact, she demanded a promise.

“警官”：……我……我不懂，你就这么放她走了？
"Officer": I don't understand. How could you just let her go like that?

“警官”：她一个人待着不会更危险吗？而且……她的档案会被记录为“逃亡”……天呐。
"Officer": Isn't she more likely to run into danger if she's on her own? And leaving like this, she'll be marked as a deserter. Oh, no.

卡戎：我不明白你说的这些。
Charon: I know little of your rules.

卡戎：但我的承诺如此，也理解她的恐慌。每个人都有正当的理由去逃避畏惧的事物。
Charon: But a promise was made, and her reasoning is understandable. It is her right to turn away from her fear, just as it is anyone else's.

青年从来没有想过要怎么应付眼前的场景，只觉得有一种力量无处挥舞的别扭。
The young man never thought about how to cope with such a situation.

他急躁地抓挠着头发，最终做出了决定。
He scratches his head, at last arriving at a simple conclusion.

“警官”：好吧……至少她还活着。
"Officer": Fine. At least she's still alive.

“警官”：我会另想办法找到她的，不能让她一个人在外面游荡。
"Officer": But I can't leave her alone out there. I'll find a way to track her down.

清澈的声音做出承诺，他仿佛刚刚接受了一项艰巨的任务。
The voice is clear and certain. He is willing and able, no matter how daunting the task ahead.

“警官”：感谢你提供的信息。再见，卡戎先生。
"Officer": Thank you for the information, Mr. Charon. Goodbye.

青年踏上返回蒙佩的道路。
He sets off on the road back to Montpaix.

一刻钟后，他的背影隐没在东部的树林里。
They watch him together, horse and rider, as he disappears into the woods.

“草丛”：“沙沙——”
Long Grass: "Hiss—"

安德烈森：咴？
Andreas: ...?

梅蕾尔：……他走了？
Merel: Has he gone?

卡戎：是的。
Charon: Yes.

安德烈森：咴咴——咴。
Andreas: Neigh ...

少女从草丛中蹿出来。
The girl leaps out from the grass.

梅蕾尔：你怎么告诉他我还活着？
Merel: Why did you tell him that I'm still alive?

卡戎：你没有让我不说这个。
Charon: You did not request that to be kept a secret.

梅蕾尔：……
Merel: ...

梅蕾尔：好吧。
Merel: Fine.

亡者点头致意，缓缓离去。
He nods his assent and begins to shuffle away.

安德烈森打着响鼻，在卡戎与梅蕾尔之间绕着圈徘徊。
Andreas snorts as it circles between them.

安德烈森：咴。
Andreas: ...

梅蕾尔轻拍马儿的面颊。
Merel pats the horse's cheek.

梅蕾尔：那个……卡戎？
Merel: Umm, Charon?

卡戎：嗯？
Charon: Huh?

梅蕾尔：其实……我并没有打算在这里当一个守墓人。
Merel: Actually, I wasn't serious, you know, when I said I wanted to become a gravekeeper here.

卡戎：死者不需要陪伴，作为纪念的墓碑也有朽烂的一日，最终，时间会将我们带入遗忘之海。
Charon: The dead need no company, and every tombstone will one day fall to decay. In the end, time will pull us all into the sea of oblivion.

卡戎：没有任何事物值得以不朽为名。
Charon: Nothing in this world is immortal.

年轻女孩挠了挠遮脸的布料，或者是成为“逃兵”的紧张，让她的皮肤感到有些发痒。
The young girl scratches at the fabric covering her face. The tension of being a "deserter" seems to make her skin itch.

梅蕾尔：好吧，关于守墓人的玩笑很差劲……我想说的是，我不知道该去哪里……离开基金会之后，我不认识其他能帮我的人。
Merel: Right. Well, anyway, the gravekeeper joke was a bad one, I admit it. But what I'm trying to say is, I'm not sure where to go next. I mean, who else can I depend on besides the Foundation?

梅蕾尔：我更不想被重塑之手的人抓到，你不知道他们在南极都做了些什么……
Merel: I definitely don't want to get caught by Manus Vindictae, that's for sure. Trust me, you don't want to know what they were doing in Antarctica.

梅蕾尔：噢……不是这个时代的南极，是之前的南极。总之我一个人完全没办法对付他们。
Merel: Oh, not the Antarctica in this era—the one from before. Anyway, my point is, I can't deal with them on my own.

安德烈森：咴……
Andreas: ...

梅蕾尔：可我还是能做一些事的，一些讨人厌的魔精我能很轻松地对付。
Merel: But I can still do something, like dealing with troublemaking critters.

梅蕾尔：所以……如果你……需要，嗯，帮手的话，我们……可以一起走？至少你不会撒谎。
Merel: So, um, if you need that kind of help, maybe we can travel together? I trust you.

卡戎：我并不会去一个安全的地方。
Charon: My path will have little safety.

梅蕾尔：等遇到危险的时候，我自己就会逃跑的。这点你就放心吧。
Merel: That's alright. I'll just run off when danger comes.

卡戎：……既然如此，请跟上我。
Charon: In that case, follow me.

卡戎：不想经过基金会监视地区的话，我们要绕一个更远的路。
Charon: We will take a detour to avoid entering territories under the Foundation's surveillance.

它从衣兜内拿出一根只有半截的巧克力，即使一直贴身存放，也并未融化。
He retrieves the familiar chocolates from his coat; they're unmelted and cool to the touch, despite having been kept so close to his body.

卡戎：如果你饿了，这些东西都可以还给你。如果你累了，安德烈森可以驮着你前进。
Charon: If you're hungry, these can be returned to you. Andreas will carry you should you grow tired.

从战争中逃脱的士兵雀跃地点头。
The soldier who has at last escaped war nods with joy.

梅蕾尔：……好、好的！
Merel: Got it!

Z：……有关《暴雨改革》法案的修订已经提上日程，委员会很快就会开启下一轮协商，你也要出席会议。
Z: The revision to the Storm Reformation Act has been added to the agenda, and the Committee will soon begin the next round of discussion. You'll need to attend the meetings as well.

Z：近期的事件令“鹰派”掌握了较大话语权，他们都很支持扩大司辰小队的权责与预算。
Z: Recent events have given the Hawks a stronger voice, and they are in favor of expanding the authority and budget of Team Timekeeper.

Z：做好准备，维尔汀。
Z: Stay ready, Vertin.

维尔汀：……我明白了。
Vertin: Understood.

基金会职员与委员们在走廊中匆忙地穿行而过。
Foundation staff and Committee members hurry through the hallway.

刚退出Z女士的办公室，就再度听见了熟悉的声音。
Just as they exit Ms. Z's office, they're met with a familiar voice.

刻雷乌斯：……司辰？
Creius: Timekeeper?

维尔汀：你在等我？
Vertin: Were you waiting for me?

刻雷乌斯：只是凑巧而已。不过我很高兴你能记得我。
Creius: No, just a happy coincidence. I'm glad to know that you remember me.

维尔汀：当然。你的行动拯救了很多士兵的生命。
Vertin: Of course. Your decisiveness saved the lives of many soldiers on the battlefield.

维尔汀：蒙佩的危机解除之后，“鸽派”也同意了扩大“前线应急预案”的决议。
Vertin: I also heard that the Doves agreed to further implement your "frontline contingency plan" after the Montpaix crisis was resolved.

刻雷乌斯：呵呵……没想到你还关心政治。
Creius: Heh. I'm surprised to see you're interested in politics.

维尔汀：……我不关心，只是有所了解。
Vertin: I'm not interested, just informed.

刻雷乌斯毫不在意地抛开了政治话题。
Creius brushes aside the topic without comment.

刻雷乌斯：上次的会面太过仓促，我一直想找个机会继续……不过，这里也并不是个适合谈话的地方。
Creius: I've been wanting to speak with you since our last meeting was cut short, but this certainly isn't the place for a proper conversation either.

刻雷乌斯：但我或许可以给你提供一些有价值的简单情报。有关于基金会，有关于……
Creius: Contact me if you're interested. I have some very valuable information for you, I'm sure. Both about the Foundation and about ...

刻雷乌斯：“兀尔德”。
Creius: Urd.

维尔汀：……！
Vertin: ...!

看见预料之中的反应，男人露出笑容，将一枚信封递了过来。
Seeing the expected reaction, he smiles and hands over an envelope.

刻雷乌斯：期待你的联络。我想，我们一定能合作愉快。
Creius: I look forward to hearing from you. I'm sure we will make excellent collaborators.

十四行诗：……司辰，打扰一下。
Sonetto: Excuse me, Timekeeper.

第一助手匆匆赶来，以疑问和警惕参半的目光看向红发男子。
Sonetto rushes over, looking at the red-haired man with a mix of suspicion and confusion.

十四行诗：请问您有什么要紧事吗，刻雷乌斯先生？如果您有需要，我可以帮你们安排会议时间……
Sonetto: Oh, Mr. Creius, do you have an urgent matter you'd like to discuss with the Timekeeper? I can arrange a meeting for you if necessary.

刻雷乌斯：不必，我们只是偶然遇见问候一下而已。
Creius: No need for that. I was just saying hello.

刻雷乌斯：下次再见，司辰，十四行诗小姐。
Creius: Until next time—Timekeeper, Ms. Sonetto.

男人微微点头，随后匆匆走远了。
He gives a nod, slight but confident, then takes his leave.

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

十四行诗：司辰？你还好吗……
Sonetto: Timekeeper, is there something wrong?

维尔汀：……没什么。你看起来很匆忙，十四行诗。
Vertin: It's nothing. You seem a little anxious, Sonetto. What's the matter?

第一助手神色不安地拿出通讯器。
Sonetto takes out her communicator.

十四行诗：司辰，我是来给你看这个的。这是一则紧急留言。
Sonetto: Timekeeper, you need to look at this. It's an important message.

维尔汀：联络人……红弩箭？
Vertin: Sent from ... Lilya?

*紧急情况*

受索姆将军直接调遣，我正在东线执行任务。
I've been on a mission on the eastern front, under the direct orders of Admiral Somme.

头儿，猜猜看我发现了……&%#……什么？一个管辖……*#@……外的……￥%&#……芝诺驻扎地。
Guess what I found, Captain? An *static noise* Zeno outpost without *static noise*.

根据我的判断，这是……*&%……叛军。
From the looks of it, I think it's the *static noise* rebels.

详情……$#@……尽快回电。
I can tell *static noise* in more detail. Call me back as soon as you can.

留言在一阵杂音中结束。
The message ends in a burst of static.

十四行诗：我收到留言后就尝试过联络红弩箭小姐，但……呼叫无法接通。
Sonetto: I tried to contact Ms. Lilya after receiving the message, but I couldn't get through.

十四行诗：她在留言中提到了芝诺的叛军，我担心……
Sonetto: She mentioned Zeno rebels. This is worrying.

维尔汀：……是伊戈尔？红弩箭有麻烦了。
Vertin: Could it be ... Igor? Lilya might be in trouble.

维尔汀：十四行诗，和我回一趟Z女士的办公室。
Vertin: Sonetto, I think we'd better pay another visit to Madam Z.
